 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet janamejaya uvācaa evaṃ nipātite karṇe samare savyasācināc alpāvaśiṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ kim akurvata vai dvijaa udīryamāṇaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā suyodhanaḥc pāṇḍavaiḥ prāptakālaṃ ca kiṃ prāpadyata kauravaḥa etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ tad ācakṣva dvijottamac na hi tṛpyāmi pūrveṣāṃ śṛṇvānaś caritaṃ mahat vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tataḥ karṇe hate rājan dhārtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanaḥc bhṛśaṃ śokārṇave magno nirāśaḥ sarvato bhavata hā karṇa hā karṇa iti śocamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥc kṛcchrāt svaśibiraṃ prāyād dhataśeṣair nṛpaiḥ sahaa sa samāśvāsyamāno pi hetubhiḥ śāstraniścitaiḥc rājabhir nālabhac charma sūtaputravadhaṃ smarana sa daivaṃ balavan matvā bhavitavyaṃ ca pārthivaḥc saṃgrāme niścayaṃ kṛtvā punar yuddhāya niryayaua śalyaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā vidhivad rājapuṃgavaḥb madrarājaṃ puraskṛtya yuddhāyopajagāma hac raṇāya niryayau rājā hataśeṣair nṛpaiḥ sahaa tataḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥc babhūva bharataśreṣṭha devāsuraraṇopamama tataḥ śalyo mahārāja kṛtvā kadanam āhavec pāṇḍusainyasya madhyāhne dharmarājena pātitaḥa tato duryodhano rājā hatabandhū raṇājirātc apasṛtya hradaṃ ghoraṃ viveśa ripujād bhayāta athāparāhṇe tasyāhnaḥ parivārya mahārathaiḥb tathāparāhṇe tatrasthaṃ parivārya suyodhanamc hradād āhūya yogena bhīmasenena pātitaḥa tasmin hate maheṣvāse hataśiṣṭās trayo rathāḥa   sānubandhe suyodhanea kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇirb suptaṃ śibiram āviśya dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamānc saṃrabhān niśi rājendra jaghnuḥ pāñcālasainikāna tataḥ pūrvāhṇasamaye śibirād etya saṃjayaḥc praviveśa purīṃ dīno duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥa praviśya ca puraṃ tūrṇaṃ bhujāv ucchritya duḥkhitaḥc vepamānas tato rājñaḥ praviveśa niveśanama ruroda ca naravyāghra hā rājann iti duḥkhitaḥc aho bata vivignāḥ sma nidhanena mahātmanaḥa aho subalavān kālo gatiś ca paramā tathāb vidhis tu balavān atra pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakamc śakratulyabalāḥ sarve yatrāvadhyanta pārthivāḥa dṛṣṭvaiva ca puro rājañ janaḥ sarvaḥ sa saṃjayamb kleśena mahatā yuktaḥ sarvato rājasattamac praruroda bhṛśodvigno hā rājann iti sasvarama ākumāraṃ naravyāghra tat puraṃ vai samantataḥc ārtanādaṃ mahac cakre śrutvā vinihataṃ nṛpama dhāvataś cāpy apaśyac ca tatra trīn puruṣarṣabhānc naṣṭacittān ivonmattāñ śokena bhṛśapīḍitānd dṛṣṭvaiva ca narāñ śīghraṃ vyājahārātiduḥkhitaḥa tathā sa vihvalaḥ sūtaḥ praviśya nṛpatikṣayamc dadarśa nṛpatiśreṣṭhaṃ prajñācakṣuṣam īśvarama dṛṣṭvā cāsīnam anaghaṃ samantāt parivāritamc snuṣābhir bharataśreṣṭha gāndhāryā vidureṇa caa tathānyaiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca jñātibhiś ca hitaiṣibhiḥc tam eva cārthaṃ dhyāyantaṃ karṇasya nidhanaṃ pratia rudann evābravīd vākyaṃ rājānaṃ janamejayac nātihṛṣṭamanāḥ sūto bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girād uvāca bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipama saṃjayo haṃ naravyāghra namas te bharatarṣabhac madrādhipo hataḥ śalyaḥ śakuniḥ saubalas tathāe ulūkaḥ puruṣavyāghra kaitavyo dṛḍhavikramaḥa saṃśaptakā hatāḥ sarve kāmbojāś ca śakaiḥ sahac mlecchāś ca pārvatīyāś ca yavanāś ca nipātitāḥa prācyā hatā mahārāja dākṣiṇātyāś ca sarvaśaḥc udīcyā nihatāḥ sarve pratīcyāś ca narādhipae rājāno rājaputrāś ca sarvato nihatā nṛpaa duryodhano hato rājan yathoktaṃ pāṇḍavena cac bhagnasaktho mahārāja śete pāṃsuṣu rūṣitaḥd duryodhanasya bhīmena bhagnāv ūrū sutasya ted sa bhūmau patitaḥ śete pāṃśubhiḥ pariguṇṭhitaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumno hato rājañ śikhaṇḍī cāparājitaḥc uttamaujā yudhāmanyus tathā rājan prabhadrakāḥa pāñcālāś ca naravyāghrāś cedayaś ca niṣūditāḥc tava putrā hatāḥ sarve draupadeyāś ca bhāratae karṇaputro hataḥ śūro vṛṣaseno mahābalaḥa narā vinihatāḥ sarve gajāś ca vinipātitāḥc rathinaś ca naravyāghra hayāś ca nihatā yudhia kiṃciccheṣaṃ ca śibiraṃ tāvakānāṃ kṛtaṃ vibhoc pāṇḍavānāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ samāsādya parasparama prāyaḥ strīśeṣam abhavaj jagat kālena mohitamc sapta pāṇḍavataḥ śeṣā dhārtarāṣṭrās tathā trayaḥa te caiva bhrātaraḥ pañca vāsudevo tha sātyakiḥc kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiś ca jayatāṃ varaḥa tavāpy ete mahārāja rathino nṛpasattamac akṣauhiṇīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ sametānāṃ janeśvarae ete śeṣā mahārāja sarve nye nidhanaṃ gatāḥa kālena nihataṃ sarvaṃ jagad vai bharatarṣabhac duryodhanaṃ vai purataḥ kṛtvā vairasya bhārataa etac chrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥc nipapāta mahārāja gatasattvo mahītalea tasmin nipatite bhūmau viduro pi mahāyaśāḥc nipapāta mahārāja rājavyasanakarśitaḥa gāndhārī ca nṛpaśreṣṭha sarvāś ca kuruyoṣitaḥc patitāḥ sahasā bhūmau śrutvā krūraṃ vacaś ca tāḥa niḥsaṃjñaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau tadāsīd rājamaṇḍalamc pralāpayuktā mahatī kathā nyastā paṭe yathāa kṛcchreṇa tu tato rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥc śanair alabhata prāṇān putravyasanakarśitaḥa labdhvā tu sa nṛpaḥ saṃjñāṃ vepamānaḥ suduḥkhitaḥc udīkṣya ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ kṣattāraṃ vākyam abravīta vidvan kṣattar mahāprājña tvaṃ gatir bharatarṣabhac mamānāthasya subhṛśaṃ putrair hīnasya sarvaśaḥe evam uktvā tato bhūyo visaṃjño nipapāta haa taṃ tathā patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāndhavā ye sya ke canac śītais tu siṣicus toyair vivyajur vyajanair apia sa tu dīrgheṇa kālena pratyāśvasto mahīpatiḥc tūṣṇīṃ dadhyau mahīpālaḥ putravyasanakarśitaḥe niḥśvasañ jihmaga iva kumbhakṣipto viśāṃ patea saṃjayo py arudat tatra dṛṣṭvā rājānam āturamc tathā sarvāḥ striyaś caiva gāndhārī ca yaśasvinīa tato dīrgheṇa kālena viduraṃ vākyam abravītc dhṛtarāṣṭro naravyāghro muhyamāno muhur muhuḥa gacchantu yoṣitaḥ sarvā gāndhārī ca yaśasvinīc tatheme suhṛdaḥ sarve bhraśyate me mano bhṛśama evam uktas tataḥ kṣattā tāḥ striyo bharatarṣabhac visarjayām āsa śanair vepamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥa niścakramus tataḥ sarvās tāḥ striyo bharatarṣabhac suhṛdaś ca tataḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā rājānam āturama tato narapatiṃ tatra labdhasaṃjñaṃ paraṃtapab gatir me ko bhaved adya iti cintāsamākulaḥc avekṣya saṃjayo dīno rodamānaṃ bhṛśāturama prāñjalir niḥśvasantaṃ ca taṃ narendraṃ muhur muhuḥb jñātīn striyo tha niryāpya praviśya viduraḥ punaḥb rājānaṃ śocamānas tu taṃ śocantaṃ muhur muhuḥc samāśvāsayata kṣattā vacasā madhureṇa ha vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa visṛṣṭāsv atha nārīṣu dhṛtarāṣṭro mbikāsutaḥc vilalāpa mahārāja duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ gataḥa sadhūmam iva niḥśvasya karau dhunvan punaḥ punaḥc vicintya ca mahārāja tato vacanam abravītd yac chrutvā suhṛdāṃ cātikaruṇā samajāyataa aho bata mahad duḥkhaṃ yad ahaṃ pāṇḍavān raṇec kṣemiṇaś cāvyayāṃś caiva tvattaḥ sūta śṛṇomi vaia vajrasāramayaṃ nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ mamac yac chrutvā nihatān putrān dīryate na sahasradhāa cintayitvā vacas teṣāṃ bālakrīḍāṃ ca saṃjayac adya śrutvā hatān putrān bhṛśaṃ me dīryate manaḥa andhatvād yadi teṣāṃ tu na me rūpanidarśanamc putrasnehakṛtā prītir nityam eteṣu dhāritāa bālabhāvam atikrāntān yauvanasthāṃś ca tān ahamc madhyaprāptāṃs tathā śrutvā hṛṣṭa āsaṃ tathānaghaa tān adya nihatāñ śrutvā hṛtaiśvaryān hṛtaujasaḥc na labhe vai kva cic chāntiṃ putrādhibhir abhiplutaḥa ehy ehi putra rājendra mamānāthasya sāṃpratamc tvayā hīno mahābāho kāṃ nu yāsyāmy ahaṃ gatima gatir bhūtvā mahārāja jñātīnāṃ suhṛdāṃ tathāc andhaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca māṃ vīra vihāya kva nu gacchasia sā kṛpā sā ca te prītiḥ sā ca rājan sumānitāc kathaṃ vinihataḥ pārthaiḥ saṃyugeṣv aparājitaḥa kathaṃ tvaṃ pṛthivīpālān bhuktvā tāta samāgatānc śeṣe vinihato bhūmau prākṛtaḥ kunṛpo yathāa ko nu mām utthitaṃ kālye tāta tāteti vakṣyatic mahārājeti satataṃ lokanātheti cāsakṛta pariṣvajya ca māṃ kaṇṭhe snehenāklinnalocanaḥc anuśādhīti kauravya tat sādhu vada me vacaḥa nanu nāmāham aśrauṣaṃ vacanaṃ tava putrakac bhūyasī mama pṛthvīyaṃ yathā pārthasya no tathāa bhagadattaḥ kṛpaḥ śalya āvantyo tha jayadrathaḥc bhūriśravāḥ somadatto mahārājo tha bāhlikaḥa aśvatthāmā ca bhojaś ca māgadhaś ca mahābalaḥc bṛhadbalaś ca kāśīśaḥ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥa mlecchāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ śakāś ca yavanaiḥ sahac sudakṣiṇaś ca kāmbojas trigartādhipatis tathāa bhīṣmaḥ pitāmahaś caiva bhāradvājo tha gautamaḥc śrutāyuś cācyutāyuś ca śatāyuś cāpi vīryavāna jalasaṃdho thārśyaśṛṅgī rākṣasaś cāpy alāyudhaḥc alaṃbuso mahābāhuḥ subāhuś ca mahārathaḥa ete cānye ca bahavo rājāno rājasattamac madartham udyatāḥ sarve prāṇāṃs tyaktvā raṇe prabhoa yeṣāṃ madhye sthito yuddhe bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥc yodhayiṣyāmy ahaṃ pārthān pāñcālāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥa cedīṃś ca nṛpaśārdūla draupadeyāṃś ca saṃyugec sātyakiṃ kuntibhojaṃ ca rākṣasaṃ ca ghaṭotkacama eko py eṣāṃ mahārāja samarthaḥ saṃnivāraṇec samare pāṇḍaveyānāṃ saṃkruddho hy abhidhāvatāme kiṃ punaḥ sahitā vīrāḥ kṛtavairāś ca pāṇḍavaiḥa atha vā sarva evaite pāṇḍavasyānuyāyibhiḥc yotsyanti saha rājendra haniṣyanti ca tān mṛdhea karṇas tv eko mayā sārdhaṃ nihaniṣyati pāṇḍavānc tato nṛpatayo vīrāḥ sthāsyanti mama śāsanea yaś ca teṣāṃ praṇetā vai vāsudevo mahābalaḥc na sa saṃnahyate rājann iti mām abravīd vacaḥa tasyāhaṃ vadataḥ sūta bahuśo mama saṃnidhauc yuktito hy anupaśyāmi nihatān pāṇḍavān mṛdhea teṣāṃ madhye sthitā yatra hanyante mama putrakāḥc vyāyacchamānāḥ samare kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa bhīṣmaś ca nihato yatra lokanāthaḥ pratāpavānc śikhaṇḍinaṃ samāsādya mṛgendra iva jambukama droṇaś ca brāhmaṇo yatra sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥc nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd karṇaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye divyāstrajño mahābalaḥa bhūriśravā hato yatra somadattaś ca saṃyugec bāhlīkaś ca mahārāja kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd bhagadatto hato yatra gajayuddhaviśāradaḥd jayadrathaś ca nihataḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa sudakṣiṇo hato yatra jalasaṃdhaś ca kauravaḥc śrutāyuś cācyutāyuś ca kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd mahābalas tathā pāṇḍyaḥ sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥd nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa bṛhadbalo hato yatra māgadhaś ca mahābalaḥb ugrāyudhaś ca vikrāntaḥ pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatāmb śatāyuś caiva vikrāntaḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥc āvantyo nihato yatra trigartaś ca janādhipaḥe saṃśaptakāś ca bahavaḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥf   śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥf trigartaś ca mahābāhuḥ saṃśaptāś ca mahābalāḥf yatra śūrā maheṣvāsā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥf nihatā bhīmasenena kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa alaṃbusas tathā rājan rākṣasaś cāpy alāyudhaḥc ārśyaśṛṅgaś ca nihataḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa nārāyaṇā hatā yatra gopālā yuddhadurmadāḥc mlecchāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa śakuniḥ saubalo yatra kaitavyaś ca mahābalaḥc nihataḥ sabalo vīraḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥa rājāno rājaputrāś ca śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥc nihatā bahavo yatra kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd yatra śūrā maheṣvāsāḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥd yatra śūrā mahātmānaḥ sarvaśāstrāstrapāragāḥd bahavo nihatāḥ sūta mahendrasamavikramāḥa nānādeśasamāvṛttāḥ kṣatriyā yatra saṃjayac nihatāḥ samare sarve kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa putrāś ca me vinihatāḥ pautrāś caiva mahābalāḥb duryodhano hato yatra putraś cāsya mahātmanaḥc vayasyā bhrātaraś caiva kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥd pārthena saṃyuge ghore kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa bhāgadheyasamāyukto dhruvam utpadyate naraḥc yaś ca bhāgyasamāyuktaḥ sa śubhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥa ahaṃ viyuktaḥ svair bhāgyaiḥ putraiś caiveha saṃjayac katham adya bhaviṣyāmi vṛddhaḥ śatruvaśaṃ gataḥa nānyad atra paraṃ manye vanavāsād ṛte prabhoc so haṃ vanaṃ gamiṣyāmi nirbandhur jñātisaṃkṣayea na hi me nyad bhavec chreyo vanābhyupagamād ṛtec imām avasthāṃ prāptasya lūnapakṣasya saṃjayaa duryodhano hato yatra śalyaś ca nihato yudhic duḥśāsano viśastaś ca vikarṇaś ca mahābalaḥa kathaṃ hi bhīmasenasya śroṣye haṃ śabdam uttamamc ekena samare yena hataṃ putraśataṃ mamaa asakṛd vadatas tasya duryodhanavadhena cac duḥkhaśokābhisaṃtapto na śroṣye paruṣā giraḥa evaṃ sa śokasaṃtaptaḥ pārthivo hatabāndhavaḥc muhur muhur muhyamānaḥ putrādhibhir abhiplutaḥa vilapya suciraṃ kālaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro mbikāsutaḥc dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya cintayitvā parābhavama duḥkhena mahatā rājā saṃtapto bharatarṣabhac punar gāvalgaṇiṃ sūtaṃ paryapṛcchad yathātathama bhīṣmadroṇau hatau śrutvā sūtaputraṃ ca pātitamc senāpatiṃ praṇetāraṃ kim akurvata māmakāḥd tathā śalyaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ madrāṇām īśvaraṃ vibhuma yaṃ yaṃ senāpraṇetāraṃ yudhi kurvanti māmakāḥc acireṇaiva kālena taṃ taṃ nighnanti pāṇḍavāḥa raṇamūrdhni hato bhīṣmaḥ paśyatāṃ vaḥ kirīṭināc evam eva hato droṇaḥ sarveṣām eva paśyatāma evam eva hataḥ karṇaḥ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānc sa rājakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ paśyatāṃ vaḥ kirīṭināa pūrvam evāham ukto vai vidureṇa mahātmanāc duryodhanāparādhena prajeyaṃ vinaśiṣyatia ke cin na samyak paśyanti mūḍhāḥ samyak tathāparec tad idaṃ mama mūḍhasya tathābhūtaṃ vacaḥ sma haa yad abravīn me dharmātmā viduro dīrghadarśivānc tat tathā samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ satyavādinaḥa daivopahatacittena yan mayāpakṛtaṃ purāc anayasya phalaṃ tasya brūhi gāvalgaṇe punaḥa ko vā mukham anīkānām āsīt karṇe nipātitec arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca ko vā pratyudyayau rathīa ke rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ madrarājasya saṃyugec vāmaṃ ca yoddhukāmasya ke vā vīrasya pṛṣṭhataḥa kathaṃ ca vaḥ sametānāṃ madrarājo mahābalaḥc nihataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃkhye putro vā mama saṃjayaa brūhi sarvaṃ yathātattvaṃ bharatānāṃ mahākṣayamc yathā ca nihataḥ saṃkhye putro duryodhano mamaa pāñcālāś ca yathā sarve nihatāḥ sapadānugāḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥa pāṇḍavāś ca yathā muktās tathobhau sātvatau yudhic kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhāradvājasya cātmajaḥa yad yathā yādṛśaṃ caiva yuddhaṃ vṛttaṃ ca sāṃpratamc akhilaṃ śrotum icchāmi kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa śṛṇu rājann avahito yathā vṛtto mahān kṣayaḥc kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca samāsādya parasparama nihate sūtaputre tu pāṇḍavena mahātmanāc vidruteṣu ca sainyeṣu samānīteṣu cāsakṛtd ghore manuṣyadehānām ājau gajavarakṣayed yat tat karṇe hate pārthaḥ siṃhanādam athākarotd tadā tava sutān rājan prāviśat sumahad bhayamd na saṃdhātum anīkāni na caivātha parākramed āsīd buddhir hate karṇe tava yodhasya kasya citd vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyām agādhe viplavā ivad apāre pāram icchanto hate dvīpe kirīṭinād sūtaputre hate rājan vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥd anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā ivad bhagnaśṛṅgā iva vṛṣāḥ śīrṇadaṃṣṭrā ivoragāḥd pratyupāyāma sāyāhne nirjitāḥ savyasācinād hatapravīrā vidhvastā nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd sūtaputre hate rājan putrās te prādravan bhayātd viśastrakavacāḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkā vicetasaḥd anyonyam abhinighnanto vīkṣamāṇā bhayārditāḥd mām eva nūnaṃ bībhatsur mām eva ca vṛkodaraḥd abhiyātīti manvānāḥ petur mamluś ca bhāratad hayān anye gajān anye rathān anye mahārathāḥd āruhya javasaṃpannān pādātān prajahur bhayātd kuñjaraiḥ syandanā bhagnāḥ sādinaś ca mahārathaiḥd padātisaṃghāś cāśvaughaiḥ palāyadbhir bhṛśaṃ hatāḥd vyālataskarasaṃkīrṇe sārthahīnā yathā vaned tathā tvadīyā nihate sūtaputre tadābhavand hatārohās tathā nāgāś chinnahastās tathāpared sarvaṃ pārthamayaṃ lokam apaśyan vai bhayārditāḥd tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditānd duryodhano tha svaṃ sūtaṃ hāhākṛtvedam abravītd nātikramiṣyate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitamd jaghane yudhyamānaṃ māṃ tūrṇam aśvān pracodayad samare yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥd notsahetābhyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahārṇavaḥd adyārjunaṃ sagovindaṃ māninaṃ ca vṛkodaramd nihatya śiṣṭāñ śatrūṃś ca karṇasyānṛṇyam āpnuyāmd tac chrutvā kururājasya śūrāryasadṛśaṃ vacaḥd sūto hemaparicchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayatd gajāśvarathahīnās tu pādātāś caiva māriṣad pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ prādravañ śanakair ivad tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥd balena caturaṅgeṇa parikṣipyāhanac charaiḥd pratyayudhyanta te sarve bhīmasenaṃ sapārṣatamd pārthapārṣatayoś cānye jagṛhus tatra nāmanīd akrudhyata raṇe bhīmas tair mṛdhe pratyavasthitaiḥd so vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāpāṇir ayudhyatad na tān rathastho bhūmiṣṭhān dharmāpekṣī vṛkodaraḥd yodhayām āsa kaunteyo bhujavīryaṃ samāśritaḥd jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmd nyavadhīt tāvakān sarvān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥd padātayo hi saṃrabdhās tyaktajīvitabāndhavāḥd bhīmam abhyadravan saṃkhye pataṃgā jvalanaṃ yathād āsādya bhīmasenaṃ te saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥd vineśuḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā bhūtagrāmā ivāntakamd śyenavad vyacarad bhīmaḥ khaḍgena gadayā tathād pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāṃs tāvakānām apothayatd hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya punas tasthau mahābalaḥd dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam anvapadyata vīryavānd mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahābalaḥd javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā ghnanto dauryodhanaṃ balamd tasyāśvavārān subahūṃs te nihatya śitaiḥ śaraiḥd tam anvadhāvaṃs tvaritās tatra yuddham avartatad tato dhanaṃjayo rājan rathānīkam agāhatad viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu gāṇḍīvaṃ vyākṣipan dhanuḥd kṛṣṇasārathim āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetahayaṃ rathamd arjunaṃ cāpi yoddhāraṃ tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayātd viprahīnarathāśvāś ca śaraiś ca parivāritāḥd pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ pārtham ārchan padātayaḥd hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathaḥd bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyatad mahādhanurdharaḥ śrīmān amitragaṇamardanaḥd putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāyaśāḥd pārāvatasavarṇāśvaṃ kovidāravaradhvajamd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayātd gāndhārarājaṃ śīghrāstram anusṛtya yaśasvinaud nacirāt pratyadṛśyetāṃ mādrīputrau sasātyakīd cekitānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāś ca māriṣad hatvā tvadīyaṃ sumahat sainyaṃ śaṅkhān athādhamand te sarve tāvakān prekṣya dravato vai parāṅmukhānd abhyadhāvanta nighnanto vṛṣāñ jitvā vṛṣā ivad senāvaśeṣaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putrasya pāṇḍavaḥd vyavasthitaṃ savyasācī cukrodha balavan nṛpad tata enaṃ śarai rājan sahasā samavākiratd rajasā codgatenātha na sma kiṃ cana dṛśyated andhakārīkṛte loke śarībhūte mahītaled diśaḥ sarvā mahārāja tāvakāḥ prādravan bhayātd bhajyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kururājo viśāṃ pated pareṣām ātmanaś caiva samantāt samupādravatd tato duryodhanaḥ sarvān ājuhāvātha pāṇḍavānd yuddhāya bharataśreṣṭha devān iva purā baliḥd ta enam abhigarjantaṃ sahitāḥ samupādravand nānāśastrasṛjaḥ kruddhā bhartsayanto muhur muhuḥd duryodhano py asaṃbhrāntas tān arīn vyadhamac charaiḥd tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣamd yad enaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekur ativartitumd nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyaned duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam apaśyad bhṛśavikṣatamd tato vasthāpya rājendra kṛtabuddhis tavātmajaḥd harṣayann iva tān yodhān idaṃ vacanam abravītd na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu cad yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥd svalpaṃ caiva balaṃ teṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣataud yadi sarve tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhavetd viprayātāṃs tu vo bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣānd anusṛtya haniṣyanti śreyo naḥ samare vadhaḥd sukhaḥ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyataḥd mṛto duḥkhaṃ na jānīte pretya cānantyam aśnuted śṛṇvantu kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvanto vai samāgatāḥd dviṣato bhīmasenasya kruddhasya vaśam eṣy athad pitāmahair ācaritaṃ na dharmaṃ hātum arhathad na hi karmāsti pāpīyaḥ kṣatriyasya palāyanātd na yuddhadharmāc chreyān hi panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥd sucireṇārjitāṃl lokān sadyo yodhaḥ samaśnuted tasya tad vacanaṃ rājñaḥ pūjayitvā mahārathāḥd punar evābhyavartanta kṣatriyāḥ pāṇḍavān pratid parājayam amṛṣyantaḥ kṛtacittāś ca vikramed tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ punar eva sudāruṇamd tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca devāsuraraṇopamamd yudhiṣṭhirapurogāṃś ca sarvasainyena pāṇḍavānd anvadhāvan mahārāja putro duryodhanas tavaa vimukhe tava putre tu śokopahatacetasib pātiteṣu turaṃgeṣu gajeṣu ca ratheṣu cac bhṛśodvigneṣu sainyeṣu dṛṣṭvā pārthasya vikramama dhyāyamāneṣu sainyeṣu duḥkhaṃ prāpteṣu bhāratac balānāṃ mathyamānānāṃ śrutvā ninadam uttamama abhijñānaṃ narendrāṇāṃ vikṛtaṃ prekṣya saṃyugec patitān rathanīḍāṃś ca rathāṃś cāpi mahātmanāma raṇe vinihatān nāgān dṛṣṭvā pattīṃś ca māriṣac āyodhanaṃ cātighoraṃ rudrasyākrīḍasaṃnibhama aprakhyātiṃ gatānāṃ tu rājñāṃ śatasahasraśaḥc kṛpāviṣṭaḥ kṛpo rājan vayaḥśīlasamanvitaḥa abravīt tatra tejasvī so bhisṛtya janādhipamc duryodhanaṃ manyuvaśād vacanaṃ vacanakṣamaḥa duryodhana nibodhedaṃ yat tvā vakṣyāmi kauravac śrutvā kuru mahārāja yadi te rocate naghaa na yuddhadharmāc chreyān vai panthā rājendra vidyatec yaṃ samāśritya yudhyante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaa putro bhrātā pitā caiva svasreyo mātulas tathāc saṃbandhibāndhavāś caiva yodhyā vai kṣatrajīvināa vadhe caiva paro dharmas tathādharmaḥ palāyanec te sma ghorāṃ samāpannā jīvikāṃ jīvitārthinaḥa tatra tvāṃ prativakṣyāmi kiṃ cid eva hitaṃ vacaḥc hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca karṇe caiva mahārathea jayadrathe ca nihate tava bhrātṛṣu cānaghac lakṣmaṇe tava putre ca kiṃ śeṣaṃ paryupāsmahea yeṣu bhāraṃ samāsajya rājye matim akurmahic te saṃtyajya tanūr yātāḥ śūrā brahmavidāṃ gatima vayaṃ tv iha vinābhūtā guṇavadbhir mahārathaiḥc kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāma pātayitvā nṛpān bahūna sarvair api ca jīvadbhir bībhatsur aparājitaḥc kṛṣṇanetro mahābāhur devair api durāsadaḥa indrakārmukavajrābham indraketum ivocchritamc vānaraṃ ketum āsādya saṃcacāla mahācamūḥa siṃhanādena bhīmasya pāñcajanyasvanena cac gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣāt saṃhṛṣyanti manāṃsi naḥa carantīva mahāvidyun muṣṇanti nayanaprabhāmc alātam iva cāviddhaṃ gāṇḍīvaṃ samadṛśyataa jāmbūnadavicitraṃ ca dhūyamānaṃ mahad dhanuḥc dṛśyate dikṣu sarvāsu vidyud abhraghaneṣv ivad śvetāś ca vegasaṃpannāḥ śaśikāśasamaprabhāḥd pibanta iva cākāśaṃ rathe yuktās tu vājinaḥa uhyamānaś ca kṛṣṇena vāyuneva balāhakaḥb jāmbūnadavicitrāṅgā vahante cārjunaṃ raṇec tāvakaṃ tad balaṃ rājann arjuno stravidāṃ varaḥe gahanaṃ śiśire kakṣaṃ dadāhāgnir ivotthitaḥa gāhamānam anīkāni mahendrasadṛśaprabhamc dhanaṃjayam apaśyāma caturdantam iva dvipama vikṣobhayantaṃ senāṃ te trāsayantaṃ ca pārthivānc dhanaṃjayam apaśyāma nalinīm iva kuñjarama trāsayantaṃ tathā yodhān dhanur ghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavamc bhūya enam apaśyāma siṃhaṃ mṛgagaṇā ivaa sarvalokamaheṣvāsau vṛṣabhau sarvadhanvināmc āmuktakavacau kṛṣṇau lokamadhye virejatuḥa adya saptadaśāhāni vartamānasya bhāratac saṃgrāmasyātighorasya vadhyatāṃ cābhito yudhia vāyuneva vidhūtāni tavānīkāni sarvaśaḥc śaradambhodajālāni vyaśīryanta samantataḥa tāṃ nāvam iva paryastāṃ bhrāntavātāṃ mahārṇavec tava senāṃ mahārāja savyasācī vyakampayata kva nu te sūtaputro bhūt kva nu droṇaḥ sahānugaḥc ahaṃ kva ca kva cātmā te hārdikyaś ca tathā kva nue duḥśāsanaś ca bhrātā te bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ kva nua bāṇagocarasaṃprāptaṃ prekṣya caiva jayadrathamc saṃbandhinas te bhrātṝṃś ca sahāyān mātulāṃs tathāa sarvān vikramya miṣato lokāṃś cākramya mūrdhanic jayadratho hato rājan kiṃ nu śeṣam upāsmahea ko veha sa pumān asti yo vijeṣyati pāṇḍavamb asti kaḥ puruṣaś cādya yo jeṣyati dhanaṃjayamc tasya cāstrāṇi divyāni vividhāni mahātmanaḥe gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣo vīryāṇi harate hi naḥa naṣṭacandrā yathā rātriḥ seneyaṃ hatanāyakāa   kāminī ca mṛtapriyāc nāgabhagnadrumā śuṣkā nadīvākulatāṃ gatād yathā nadī śuṣkajalā senā karṇaṃ vinā tathāa dhvajinyāṃ hatanetrāyāṃ yatheṣṭaṃ śvetavāhanaḥc cariṣyati mahābāhuḥ kakṣe gnir iva saṃjvalana sātyakeś caiva yo vego bhīmasenasya cobhayoḥc dārayeta girīn sarvāñ śoṣayeta ca sāgarāna uvāca vākyaṃ yad bhīmaḥ sabhāmadhye viśāṃ patec kṛtaṃ tat sakalaṃ tena bhūyaś caiva kariṣyatia pramukhasthe tadā karṇe balaṃ pāṇḍavarakṣitamc durāsadaṃ tathā guptaṃ gūḍhaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanāa yuṣmābhis tāni cīrṇāni yāny asādhūni sādhuṣuc akāraṇakṛtāny eva teṣāṃ vaḥ phalam āgatama ātmano rthe tvayā loko yatnataḥ sarva āhṛtaḥc sa te saṃśayitas tāta ātmā ca bharatarṣabhaa rakṣa duryodhanātmānam ātmā sarvasya bhājanamc bhinne hi bhājane tāta diśo gacchati tadgatama hīyamānena vai saṃdhiḥ paryeṣṭavyaḥ samena cac vigraho vardhamānena nītir eṣā bṛhaspateḥa te vayaṃ pāṇḍuputrebhyo hīnāḥ svabalaśaktitaḥc atra te pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃdhiṃ manye kṣamaṃ prabhoa na jānīte hi yaḥ śreyaḥ śreyasaś cāvamanyatec sa kṣipraṃ bhraśyate rājyān na ca śreyo nuvindatia praṇipatya hi rājānaṃ rājyaṃ yadi labhemahic śreyaḥ syān na tu mauḍhyena rājan gantuṃ parābhavama vaicitravīryavacanāt kṛpāśīlo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc viniyuñjīta rājye tvāṃ govindavacanena cad ajātaśatruḥ kauravyo guruśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥd dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vacanaṃ nāvamaṃsyati dhārmikaḥd kurvanti bhrātaraś cāsya vacanaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥa yad brūyād dhi hṛṣīkeśo rājānam aparājitamc arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca sarvaṃ kuryur asaṃśayama nātikramiṣyate kṛṣṇo vacanaṃ kauravasya hac dhṛtarāṣṭrasya manye haṃ nāpi kṛṣṇasya pāṇḍavaḥa etat kṣamam ahaṃ manye tava pārthair avigrahamc na tvā bravīmi kārpaṇyān na prāṇaparirakṣaṇāte pathyaṃ rājan bravīmi tvāṃ tat parāsuḥ smariṣyasia iti vṛddho vilapyaitat kṛpaḥ śāradvato vacaḥc dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya śuśoca ca mumoha ca saṃjaya uvācaa evam uktas tato rājā gautamena yaśasvināc niḥśvasya dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ patea tato muhūrtaṃ sa dhyātvā dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥc kṛpaṃ śāradvataṃ vākyam ity uvāca paraṃtapaḥa yat kiṃ cit suhṛdā vācyaṃ tat sarvaṃ śrāvito hy ahamc kṛtaṃ ca bhavatā sarvaṃ prāṇān saṃtyajya yudhyatāa gāhamānam anīkāni yudhyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥc pāṇḍavair atitejobhir lokas tvām anudṛṣṭavāna suhṛdā yad idaṃ vācyaṃ bhavatā śrāvito hy ahamc na māṃ prīṇāti tat sarvaṃ mumūrṣor iva bheṣajama hetukāraṇasaṃyuktaṃ hitaṃ vacanam uttamamc ucyamānaṃ mahābāho na me viprāgrya rocatea rājyād vinikṛto smābhiḥ kathaṃ so smāsu viśvasetc akṣadyūte ca nṛpatir jito smābhir mahādhanaḥe sa kathaṃ mama vākyāni śraddadhyād bhūya eva tua tathā dautyena saṃprāptaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārthahite rataḥc pralabdhaś ca hṛṣīkeśas tac ca karma virodhitame sa ca me vacanaṃ brahman katham evābhimaṃsyatea vilalāpa hi yat kṛṣṇā sabhāmadhye sameyuṣīc na tan marṣayate kṛṣṇo na rājyaharaṇaṃ tathāa ekaprāṇāv ubhau kṛṣṇāv anyonyaṃ prati saṃhatauc purā yac chrutam evāsīd adya paśyāmi tat prabhoa svasrīyaṃ ca hataṃ śrutvā duḥkhaṃ svapiti keśavaḥc kṛtāgaso vayaṃ tasya sa madarthaṃ kathaṃ kṣameta abhimanyor vināśena na śarma labhate rjunaḥc sa kathaṃ maddhite yatnaṃ prakariṣyati yācitaḥa madhyamaḥ pāṇḍavas tīkṣṇo bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc pratijñātaṃ ca tenograṃ sa bhajyeta na saṃnametd sa haniṣyati māṃ rudrahastenāpi hi rakṣitama ubhau tau baddhanistriṃśāv ubhau cābaddhakaṅkaṭauc kṛtavairāv ubhau vīrau yamāv api yamopamaua dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca kṛtavairau mayā sahac tau kathaṃ maddhite yatnaṃ prakuryātāṃ dvijottamaa duḥśāsanena yat kṛṣṇā ekavastrā rajasvalāc parikliṣṭā sabhāmadhye sarvalokasya paśyataḥa tathā vivasanāṃ dīnāṃ smaranty adyāpi pāṇḍavāḥb kṛṣṇaḥ pratyaham evedaṃ vakti nāśe mamoditaḥb teṣu jīvatsu pārtheṣu tasmiñ jīvati keśaveb vināśam eva yāsyāmi svapāpenaiva sānujaḥc na nivārayituṃ śakyāḥ saṃgrāmāt te paraṃtapāḥa yadā ca draupadī kṛṣṇā madvināśāya duḥkhitāc ugraṃ tepe tapaḥ kṛṣṇā bhartṝṇām arthasiddhayee sthaṇḍile nityadā śete yāvad vairasya yātanāa nikṣipya mānaṃ darpaṃ ca vāsudevasahodarāc kṛṣṇāyāḥ preṣyavad bhūtvā śuśrūṣāṃ kurute sadāa iti sarvaṃ samunnaddhaṃ na nirvāti kathaṃ canac abhimanyor vināśena sa saṃdheyaḥ kathaṃ mayāa kathaṃ ca nāma bhuktvemāṃ pṛthivīṃ sāgarāmbarāmc pāṇḍavānāṃ prasādena bhuñjīyāṃ rājyam alpakama upary upari rājñāṃ vai jvalito bhāskaro yathāc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ kathaṃ paścād anuyāsyāmi dāsavata kathaṃ bhuktvā svayaṃ bhogān dattvā dāyāṃś ca puṣkalānc kṛpaṇaṃ vartayiṣyāmi kṛpaṇaiḥ saha jīvikāma nābhyasūyāmi te vākyam uktaṃ snigdhaṃ hitaṃ tvayāc na tu saṃdhim ahaṃ manye prāptakālaṃ kathaṃ canaa sunītam anupaśyāmi suyuddhena paraṃtapac nāyaṃ klībayituṃ kālaḥ saṃyoddhuṃ kāla eva naḥa iṣṭaṃ me bahubhir yajñair dattā vipreṣu dakṣiṇāḥc prāptāḥ kramaśrutā vedāḥ śatrūṇāṃ mūrdhni ca sthitama bhṛtyā me subhṛtās tāta dīnaś cābhyuddhṛto janaḥb notsahe dya dvijaśreṣṭha pāṇḍavān vaktum īdṛśamc yātāni pararāṣṭrāṇi svarāṣṭram anupālitama bhuktāś ca vividhā bhogās trivargaḥ sevito mayāc pitṝṇāṃ gatam ānṛṇyaṃ kṣatradharmasya cobhayoḥa na dhruvaṃ sukham astīha kuto rājyaṃ kuto yaśaḥc iha kīrtir vidhātavyā sā ca yuddhena nānyathāa gṛhe yat kṣatriyasyāpi nidhanaṃ tad vigarhitamc adharmaḥ sumahān eṣa yac chayyāmaraṇaṃ gṛhea araṇye yo vimuñceta saṃgrāme vā tanuṃ naraḥc kratūn āhṛtya mahato mahimānaṃ sa gacchatia kṛpaṇaṃ vilapann ārto jarayābhipariplutaḥc mriyate rudatāṃ madhye jñātīnāṃ na sa pūruṣaḥa tyaktvā tu vividhān bhogān prāptānāṃ paramāṃ gatimc apīdānīṃ suyuddhena gaccheyaṃ satsalokatāma śūrāṇām āryavṛttānāṃ saṃgrāmeṣv anivartināmc dhīmatāṃ satyasaṃdhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ kratuyājināma śastrāvabhṛtham āptānāṃ dhruvaṃ vāsas triviṣṭapec mudā nūnaṃ prapaśyanti śubhrā hy apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd mṛdhe tanutyajo yodhān prekṣanty apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd nūnaṃ mudopatiṣṭhanti svarge tān apsarogaṇāḥa paśyanti nūnaṃ pitaraḥ pūjitāñ śakrasaṃsadic apsarobhiḥ parivṛtān modamānāṃs triviṣṭapea panthānam amarair yātaṃ śūraiś caivānivartibhiḥc api taiḥ saṃgataṃ mārgaṃ vayam apy āruhemahia pitāmahena vṛddhena tathācāryeṇa dhīmatāc jayadrathena karṇena tathā duḥśāsanena cad sārdhaṃ duryodhanaḥ svarge khelatāṃ yuddhapātitaḥa ghaṭamānā madarthe smin hatāḥ śūrā janādhipāḥc śerate lohitāktāṅgāḥ pṛthivyāṃ śaravikṣatāḥa uttamāstravidaḥ śūrā yathoktakratuyājinaḥc tyaktvā prāṇān yathānyāyam indrasadmasu dhiṣṭhitāḥa tais tv ayaṃ racitaḥ panthā durgamo hi punar bhavetc saṃpatadbhir mahāvegair ito yādbhiś ca sadgatima ye madarthe hatāḥ śūrās teṣāṃ kṛtam anusmaranc ṛṇaṃ tat pratimuñcāno na rājye mana ādadhea pātayitvā vayasyāṃś ca bhrātṝn atha pitāmahānc jīvitaṃ yadi rakṣeyaṃ loko māṃ garhayed dhruvama kīdṛśaṃ ca bhaved rājyaṃ mama hīnasya bandhubhiḥc sakhibhiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca praṇipatya ca pāṇḍavama so ham etādṛśaṃ kṛtvā jagato sya parābhavamc suyuddhena tataḥ svargaṃ prāpsyāmi na tad anyathāa evaṃ duryodhanenoktaṃ sarve saṃpūjya tad vacaḥb tac chrutvā tava putrasya sattvayuktasya bhāṣitamc sādhu sādhv iti rājānaṃ kṣatriyāḥ saṃbabhāṣirea parājayam aśocantaḥ kṛtacittāś ca vikramec sarve suniścitā yoddhum udagramanaso bhavana tato vāhān samāśvāsya sarve yuddhābhinandinaḥc ūne dviyojane gatvā pratyatiṣṭhanta kauravāḥa ākāśe vidrume puṇye prasthe himavataḥ śubhec aruṇāṃ sarasvatīṃ prāpya papuḥ sasnuś ca tajjalama tava putrāḥ kṛtotsāhāḥ paryavartanta te tataḥc paryavasthāpya cātmānam anyonyena punas tadāe sarve rājan nyavartanta kṣatriyāḥ kālacoditāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa atha haimavate prasthe sthitvā yuddhābhinandinaḥc sarva eva mahārāja yodhās tatra samāgatāḥa śalyaś ca citrasenaś ca śakuniś ca mahārathaḥc aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥa suṣeṇo riṣṭasenaś ca dhṛtasenaś ca vīryavānc jayatsenaś ca rājānas te rātrim uṣitās tataḥa raṇe karṇe hate vīre trāsitā jitakāśibhiḥc nālabhañ śarma te putrā himavantam ṛte girima te bruvan sahitās tatra rājānaṃ sainyasaṃnidhauc kṛtayatnā raṇe rājan saṃpūjya vidhivat tadāa kṛtvā senāpraṇetāraṃ parāṃs tvaṃ yoddhum arhasic yenābhiguptāḥ saṃgrāme jayemāsuhṛdo vayama tato duryodhanaḥ sthitvā rathe rathavarottamamc sarvayuddhavibhāgajñam antakapratimaṃ yudhia svaṅgaṃ pracchannaśirasaṃ kambugrīvaṃ priyaṃvadamc vyākośapadmābhimukhaṃ vyāghrāsyaṃ merugauravama sthāṇor vṛṣasya sadṛśaṃ skandhanetragatisvaraiḥc puṣṭaśliṣṭāyatabhujaṃ suvistīrṇaghanorasama jave bale ca sadṛśam aruṇānujavātayoḥc ādityasya tviṣā tulyaṃ buddhyā cośanasā samama kāntirūpamukhaiśvaryais tribhiś candramasopamamc kāñcanopalasaṃghātaiḥ sadṛśaṃ śliṣṭasaṃdhikama suvṛttorukaṭījaṅghaṃ supādaṃ svaṅgulīnakhamc smṛtvā smṛtvaiva ca guṇān dhātrā yatnād vinirmitama sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ nipuṇaṃ śrutisāgaramc jetāraṃ tarasārīṇām ajeyaṃ śatrubhir balātd prayogabalasaṃhāraprāyaścittaṃ sumaṅgalamd prayogaviniyogau ca smṛtiṃ yasya guṇān viduḥa daśāṅgaṃ yaś catuṣpādam iṣvastraṃ veda tattvataḥc sāṅgāṃś ca caturo vedān samyag ākhyānapañcamāna ārādhya tryambakaṃ yatnād vratair ugrair mahātapāḥc ayonijāyām utpanno droṇenāyonijena yaḥa tam apratimakarmāṇaṃ rūpeṇāsadṛśaṃ bhuvic pāragaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ guṇārṇavam aninditame tam abhyetyātmajas tubhyam aśvatthāmānam abravīta yaṃ puraskṛtya sahitā yudhi jeṣyāma pāṇḍavānc guruputro dya sarveṣām asmākaṃ paramā gatiḥe bhavāṃs tasmān niyogāt te ko stu senāpatir mama drauṇir uvācaa ayaṃ kulena vīryeṇa tejasā yaśasā śriyāc sarvair guṇaiḥ samuditaḥ śalyo no stu camūpatiḥa bhāgineyān nijāṃs tyaktvā kṛtajño smān upāgataḥc mahāseno mahābāhur mahāsena ivāparaḥa enaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā nṛpatiṃ nṛpasattamac śakyaḥ prāptuṃ jayo smābhir devaiḥ skandam ivājitama tathokte droṇaputreṇa sarva eva narādhipāḥc parivārya sthitāḥ śalyaṃ jayaśabdāṃś ca cakriree yuddhāya ca matiṃ cakrūr āveśaṃ ca paraṃ yayuḥa tato duryodhanaḥ śalyaṃ bhūmau sthitvā rathe sthitamc uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā rāmabhīṣmasamaṃ raṇea ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto mitrāṇāṃ mitravatsalac yatra mitram amitraṃ vā parīkṣante budhā janāḥa sa bhavān astu naḥ śūraḥ praṇetā vāhinīmukhec raṇaṃ ca yāte bhavati pāṇḍavā mandacetasaḥe bhaviṣyanti sahāmātyāḥ pāñcālāś ca nirudyamāḥf duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā śalyo madrādhipas tadāf uvāca vākyaṃ dharmajño rājānaṃ rājasaṃnidhau śalya uvācaa yat tu māṃ manyase rājan kururāja karomi tatc tvatpriyārthaṃ hi me sarvaṃ prāṇā rājyaṃ dhanāni ca duryodhana uvācaa senāpatyena varaye tvām ahaṃ mātulātulamc so smān pāhi yudhāṃ śreṣṭha skando devān ivāhavea abhiṣicyasva rājendra devānām iva pāvakiḥc jahi śatrūn raṇe vīra mahendro dānavān iva saṃjaya uvācaa etac chrutvā vaco rājño madrarājaḥ pratāpavānc duryodhanaṃ tadā rājan vākyam etad uvāca haa duryodhana mahābāho śṛṇu vākyavidāṃ varac yāv etau manyase kṛṣṇau rathasthau rathināṃ varaue na me tulyāv ubhāv etau bāhuvīrye kathaṃ canaa udyatāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sasurāsuramānavāmc yodhayeyaṃ raṇamukhe saṃkruddhaḥ kim u pāṇḍavāne vijeṣye ca raṇe pārthān somakāṃś ca samāgatāna ahaṃ senāpraṇetā te bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥc taṃ ca vyūhaṃ vidhāsyāmi na tariṣyanti yaṃ paree iti satyaṃ bravīmy eṣa duryodhana na saṃśayaḥa evam uktas tato rājā madrādhipatim añjasāc abhyaṣiñcata senāyā madhye bharatasattamae vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena hṛṣṭarūpo viśāṃ patea abhiṣikte tatas tasmin siṃhanādo mahān abhūtc tava sainyeṣv avādyanta vāditrāṇi ca bhārataa hṛṣṭāś cāsaṃs tadā yodhā madrakāś ca mahārathāḥc tuṣṭuvuś caiva rājānaṃ śalyam āhavaśobhinama jaya rājaṃś ciraṃ jīva jahi śatrūn samāgatānc tava bāhubalaṃ prāpya dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥe nikhilāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ praśāsantu hatadviṣaḥa tvaṃ hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ sasurāsuramānavānc martyadharmāṇa iha tu kim u somakasṛñjayāna evaṃ saṃstūyamānas tu madrāṇām adhipo balīc harṣaṃ prāpa tadā vīro durāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ śalya uvācaa adyaivāhaṃ raṇe sarvān pāñcālān saha pāṇḍavaiḥc nihaniṣyāmi rājendra svargaṃ yāsyāmi vā hataḥa adya paśyantu māṃ lokā vicarantam abhītavatc adya pāṇḍusutāḥ sarve vāsudevaḥ sasātyakiḥa pāñcālāś cedayaś caiva draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sarve cāpi prabhadrakāḥa vikramaṃ mama paśyantu dhanuṣaś ca mahad balamc lāghavaṃ cāstravīryaṃ ca bhujayoś ca balaṃ yudhia adya paśyantu me pārthāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥc yādṛśaṃ me balaṃ bāhvoḥ saṃpad astreṣu yā ca mea adya me vikramaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc pratīkāraparā bhūtvā ceṣṭantāṃ vividhāḥ kriyāḥa adya sainyāni pāṇḍūnāṃ drāvayiṣye samantataḥc droṇabhīṣmāv ati vibho sūtaputraṃ ca saṃyugee vicariṣye raṇe yudhyan priyārthaṃ tava kaurava saṃjaya uvācaa abhiṣikte tadā śalye tava sainyeṣu mānadac na karṇavyasanaṃ kiṃ cin menire tatra bhārataa hṛṣṭāḥ sumanasaś caiva babhūvus tatra sainikāḥc menire nihatān pārthān madrarājavaśaṃ gatāna praharṣaṃ prāpya senā tu tāvakī bharatarṣabhac tāṃ rātriṃ sukhinī suptā svasthacitteva sābhavata sainyasya tava taṃ śabdaṃ śrutvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc vārṣṇeyam abravīd vākyaṃ sarvakṣatrasya śṛṇvataḥa madrarājaḥ kṛtaḥ śalyo dhārtarāṣṭreṇa mādhavac senāpatir maheṣvāsaḥ sarvasainyeṣu pūjitaḥa etac chrutvā yathābhūtaṃ kuru mādhava yat kṣamamc bhavān netā ca goptā ca vidhatsva yad anantarama tam abravīn mahārāja vāsudevo janādhipamc ārtāyanim ahaṃ jāne yathātattvena bhārataa vīryavāṃś ca mahātejā mahātmā ca viśeṣataḥc kṛtī ca citrayodhī ca saṃyukto lāghavena caa yādṛg bhīṣmas tathā droṇo yādṛk karṇaś ca saṃyugec tādṛśas tad viśiṣṭo vā madrarājo mato mamad evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena dharmarājo viśāṃ patiḥd saṃgrāmāya matiṃ cakre tataḥ parapuraṃjayaḥd bherīmṛdaṅgaśaṅkhānāṃ paṭahānāṃ tathaiva cad ninādair ubhayos tatra sainyayor vyāptam ambarama yudhyamānasya tasyājau cintayann eva bhāratac yoddhāraṃ nādhigacchāmi tulyarūpaṃ janādhipaa śikhaṇḍyarjunabhīmānāṃ sātvatasya ca bhāratac dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca tathā balenābhyadhiko raṇea madrarājo mahārāja siṃhadviradavikramaḥc vicariṣyaty abhīḥ kāle kālaḥ kruddhaḥ prajāsv ivaa tasyādya na prapaśyāmi pratiyoddhāram āhavec tvām ṛte puruṣavyāghra śārdūlasamavikramama sadevaloke kṛtsne smin nānyas tvattaḥ pumān bhavetc madrarājaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ yo hanyāt kurunandanae ahany ahani yudhyantaṃ kṣobhayantaṃ balaṃ tavaa tasmāj jahi raṇe śalyaṃ maghavān iva śambaramc atipaścād asau vīro dhārtarāṣṭreṇa satkṛtaḥa tavaiva hi jayo nūnaṃ hate madreśvare yudhic tasmin hate hataṃ sarvaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ mahata etac chrutvā mahārāja vacanaṃ mama sāṃpratamc pratyudyāhi raṇe pārtha madrarājaṃ mahābalame jahi cainaṃ mahābāho vāsavo namuciṃ yathāa na caivātra dayā kāryā mātulo yaṃ mameti vaic kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya jahi madrajaneśvarama bhīṣmadroṇārṇavaṃ tīrtvā karṇapātālasaṃbhavamc mā nimajjasva sagaṇaḥ śalyam āsādya goṣpadama yac ca te tapaso vīryaṃ yac ca kṣātraṃ balaṃ tavab cakṣur dharmeti yal loke kathyase tvaṃ janādhipac tad darśaya raṇe sarvaṃ jahi cainaṃ mahārathama etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ keśavaḥ paravīrahāc jagāma śibiraṃ sāyaṃ pūjyamāno tha pāṇḍavaiḥa keśave tu tadā yāte dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc visṛjya sarvān bhrātṝṃś ca pāñcālān atha somakāne suṣvāpa rajanīṃ tāṃ tu viśalya iva kuñjaraḥa te ca sarve maheṣvāsāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavās tathāb abravīt tāvakān sarvān karṇasya nidhanena vaic karṇasya nidhane hṛṣṭāḥ suṣupus tāṃ niśāṃ tadāa gatajvaraṃ maheṣvāsaṃ tīrṇapāraṃ mahārathamc babhūva pāṇḍaveyānāṃ sainyaṃ pramuditaṃ niśie sūtaputrasya nidhane jayaṃ labdhvā ca māriṣaf prabhātasamaye hṛṣṭāḥ saṃnahyanta rathottamāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa vyatītāyāṃ rajanyāṃ tu rājā duryodhanas tadāc abravīt tāvakān sarvān saṃnahyantāṃ mahārathāḥa rājñas tu matam ājñāya samanahyata sā camūḥc ayojayan rathāṃs tūrṇaṃ paryadhāvaṃs tathāparea akalpyanta ca mātaṅgāḥ samanahyanta pattayaḥc hayān āstaraṇopetāṃś cakrur anye sahasraśaḥa vāditrāṇāṃ ca ninadaḥ prādurāsīd viśāṃ patec bodhanārthaṃ hi yodhānāṃ sainyānāṃ cāpy udīryatāma tato balāni sarvāṇi senāśiṣṭāni bhāratac saṃnaddhāny eva dadṛśur mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama śalyaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā madrarājaṃ mahārathāḥc pravibhajya balaṃ sarvam anīkeṣu vyavasthitāḥa tataḥ sarve samāgamya putreṇa tava sainikāḥc kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiḥ śalyo tha saubalaḥa anye ca pārthivāḥ śeṣāḥ samayaṃ cakrire tadāc na na ekena yoddhavyaṃ kathaṃ cid api pāṇḍavaiḥa yo hy ekaḥ pāṇḍavair yudhyed yo vā yudhyantam utsṛjetc sa pañcabhir bhaved yuktaḥ pātakaiḥ sopapātakaiḥd adyācāryasuto drauṇir naiko yudhyeta śatrubhiḥe anyonyaṃ parirakṣadbhir yoddhavyaṃ sahitaiś ca naḥa evaṃ te samayaṃ kṛtvā sarve tatra mahārathāḥc madrarājaṃ puraskṛtya tūrṇam abhyadravan parāna tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan vyūhya sainyaṃ mahāraṇec abhyayuḥ kauravān sarvān yotsyamānāḥ samantataḥa tad balaṃ bharataśreṣṭha kṣubdhārṇavasamasvanamc samuddhūtārṇavākāram uddhūtarathakuñjaram dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa droṇasya bhīṣmasya ca vai rādheyasya ca me śrutamc pātanaṃ śaṃsa me bhūyaḥ śalyasyātha sutasya mea kathaṃ raṇe hataḥ śalyo dharmarājena saṃjayab kathaṃ ca nihataḥ saṃkhye gadāyuddhaviśāradaḥc bhīmena ca mahābāhuḥ putro duryodhano mama saṃjaya uvācaa kṣayaṃ manuṣyadehānāṃ rathanāgāśvasaṃkṣayamc śṛṇu rājan sthiro bhūtvā saṃgrāmaṃ śaṃsato mamad śṛṇu rājann avahito gajāśvanarasaṃkṣayamd vakṣye haṃ sarvayodhānāṃ saṃgrāmaṃ tava dāruṇama āśā balavatī rājan putrāṇāṃ te bhavat tadāc hate bhīṣme ca droṇe ca sūtaputre ca pātitee śalyaḥ pārthān raṇe sarvān nihaniṣyati māriṣaa tām āśāṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā samāśvāsya ca bhāratac madrarājaṃ ca samare samāśritya mahārathame nāthavantam athātmānam amanyata sutas tavaa yadā karṇe hate pārthāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrirec tadā rājan dhārtarāṣṭrān āviveśa mahad bhayama tān samāśvāsya tu tadā madrarājaḥ pratāpavānc vyūhya vyūhaṃ mahārāja sarvatobhadram ṛddhimata pratyudyāto raṇe pārthān madrarājaḥ pratāpavānc vidhunvan kārmukaṃ citraṃ bhāraghnaṃ vegavattarama rathapravaram āsthāya saindhavāśvaṃ mahārathaḥc tasya sītā mahārāja rathasthāśobhayad rathamd tasya sthitvā mahārāja mukhe vyūhasya daṃśitaḥa sa tena saṃvṛto vīro rathenāmitrakarśanaḥc tasthau śūro mahārāja putrāṇāṃ te bhayapraṇuta prayāṇe madrarājo bhūn mukhaṃ vyūhasya daṃśitaḥc madrakaiḥ sahito vīraiḥ karṇaputraiś ca durjayaiḥa savye bhūt kṛtavarmā ca trigartaiḥ parivāritaḥc gautamo dakṣiṇe pārśve śakaiś ca yavanaiḥ sahaa aśvatthāmā pṛṣṭhato bhūt kāmbojaiḥ parivāritaḥc duryodhano bhavan madhye rakṣitaḥ kurupuṃgavaiḥa hayānīkena mahatā saubalaś cāpi saṃvṛtaḥc prayayau sarvasainyena kaitavyaś ca mahārathaḥa pāṇḍavāś ca maheṣvāsā vyūhya sainyam ariṃdamāḥc tridhā bhūtvā mahārāja tava sainyam upādravana dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc śalyasya vāhinīṃ tūrṇam abhidudruvur āhavea tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥc śalyam evābhidudrāva jighāṃsur bharatarṣabhaa hārdikyaṃ tu maheṣvāsam arjunaḥ śatrupūgahāc saṃśaptakagaṇāṃś caiva vegato bhividudruvea gautamaṃ bhīmaseno vai somakāś ca mahārathāḥc abhyadravanta rājendra jighāṃsantaḥ parān yudhia mādrīputrau tu śakunim ulūkaṃ ca mahārathauc sasainyau sahasenau tāv upatasthatur āhavea tathaivāyutaśo yodhās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavān raṇec abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa hate bhīṣme maheṣvāse droṇe karṇe mahārathec kuruṣv alpāvaśiṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu ca saṃyugea susaṃrabdheṣu pārtheṣu parākrānteṣu saṃjayac māmakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca kiṃ śiṣṭam abhavad balam saṃjaya uvācaa yathā vayaṃ pare rājan yuddhāya samavasthitāḥc yāvac cāsīd balaṃ śiṣṭaṃ saṃgrāme tan nibodha mea ekādaśa sahasrāṇi rathānāṃ bharatarṣabhac daśa dantisahasrāṇi sapta caiva śatāni caa pūrṇe śatasahasre dve hayānāṃ bharatarṣabhac narakoṭyas tathā tisro balam etat tavābhavata rathānāṃ ṣaṭsahasrāṇi ṣaṭsahasrāś ca kuñjarāḥc daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi pattikoṭī ca bhārataa etad balaṃ pāṇḍavānām abhavac cheṣam āhaveb svalpam apy etad eveha balavat parirakṣitamc eta eva samājagmur yuddhāya bharatarṣabhad śastrāstreṣv abhavan ghorāḥ ketavaḥ kṣayakāriṇaḥd bhrāntyāśvāḥ śataśas tatra netrāṇy uccair avarṣayana evaṃ vibhajya rājendra madrarājamate sthitāḥc pāṇḍavān pratyudīyāma jayagṛddhāḥ pramanyavaḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ samare jitakāśinaḥc upayātā naravyāghrāḥ pāñcālāś ca yaśasvinaḥa evam ete balaughena parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥc upayātā naravyāghrāḥ pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ prati prabhoa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakamc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nighnatām itaretaram saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ bhayavardhanamc sṛñjayaiḥ saha rājendra ghoraṃ devāsuropamama narā rathā gajaughāś ca sādinaś ca sahasraśaḥc vājinaś ca parākrāntāḥ samājagmuḥ parasparama nāgānāṃ bhīmarūpāṇāṃ dravatāṃ nisvano mahānc aśrūyata yathā kāle jaladānāṃ nabhastalea nāgair abhyāhatāḥ ke cit sarathā rathino patanc vyadravanta raṇe vīrā drāvyamāṇā madotkaṭaiḥa hayaughān pādarakṣāṃś ca rathinas tatra śikṣitāḥc śaraiḥ saṃpreṣayām āsuḥ paralokāya bhārataa sādinaḥ śikṣitā rājan parivārya mahārathānc vicaranto raṇe bhyaghnan prāsaśaktyṛṣṭibhis tathāa dhanvinaḥ puruṣāḥ ke cit saṃnivārya mahārathānc ekaṃ bahava āsādya preṣayeyur yamakṣayama nāgaṃ rathavarāṃś cānye parivārya mahārathāḥc sottarāyudhinaṃ jaghnur dravamāṇā mahāravama tathā ca rathinaṃ kruddhaṃ vikirantaṃ śarān bahūnc nāgā jaghnur mahārāja parivārya samantataḥa nāgo nāgam abhidrutya rathī ca rathinaṃ raṇec śaktitomaranārācair nijaghnus tatra tatra haa pādātān avamṛdnanto rathavāraṇavājinaḥc raṇamadhye vyadṛśyanta kurvanto mahad ākulama hayāś ca paryadhāvanta cāmarair upaśobhitāḥc haṃsā himavataḥ prasthe pibanta iva medinīma teṣāṃ tu vājināṃ bhūmiḥ khuraiś citrā viśāṃ patec aśobhata yathā nārī karajakṣatavikṣatāa vājināṃ khuraśabdena rathanemisvanena cac pattīnāṃ cāpi śabdena nāgānāṃ bṛṃhitena caa vāditrāṇāṃ ca ghoṣeṇa śaṅkhānāṃ nisvanena cac abhavan nāditā bhūmir nirghātair iva bhārataa dhanuṣāṃ kūjamānānāṃ nistriṃśānāṃ ca dīpyatāmc kavacānāṃ prabhābhiś ca na prājñāyata kiṃ canaa bahavo bāhavaś chinnā nāgarājakaropamāḥc udveṣṭante viveṣṭante vegaṃ kurvanti dāruṇama śirasāṃ ca mahārāja patatāṃ vasudhātalec cyutānām iva tālebhyaḥ phalānāṃ śrūyate svanaḥa śirobhiḥ patitair bhāti rudhirārdrair vasuṃdharāc tapanīyanibhaiḥ kāle nalinair iva bhārataa udvṛttanayanais tais tu gatasattvaiḥ suvikṣataiḥc vyabhrājata mahārāja puṇḍarīkair ivāvṛtāa bāhubhiś candanādigdhaiḥ sakeyūrair mahādhanaiḥc patitair bhāti rājendra mahī śakradhvajair ivaa ūrubhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ vinikṛttair mahāhavec hastihastopamair anyaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ tad raṇāṅgaṇama kabandhaśatasaṃkīrṇaṃ chatracāmaraśobhitamc senāvanaṃ tac chuśubhe vanaṃ puṣpācitaṃ yathāa tatra yodhā mahārāja vicaranto hy abhītavatc dṛśyante rudhirāktāṅgāḥ puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥa mātaṅgāś cāpy adṛśyanta śaratomarapīḍitāḥc patantas tatra tatraiva chinnābhrasadṛśā raṇea gajānīkaṃ mahārāja vadhyamānaṃ mahātmabhiḥc vyadīryata diśaḥ sarvā vātanunnā ghanā ivaa te gajā ghanasaṃkāśāḥ petur urvyāṃ samantataḥc vajrarugṇā iva babhuḥ parvatā yugasaṃkṣayea hayānāṃ sādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ patitānāṃ mahītalec rāśayaḥ saṃpradṛśyante girimātrās tatas tataḥa saṃjajñe raṇabhūmau tu paralokavahā nadīc śoṇitodā rathāvartā dhvajavṛkṣāsthiśarkarāa bhujanakrā dhanuḥsrotā hastiśailā hayopalāc medomajjākardaminī chatrahaṃsā gadoḍupāa kavacoṣṇīṣasaṃchannā patākāruciradrumāc cakracakrāvalījuṣṭā triveṇūdaṇḍakāvṛtāa śūrāṇāṃ harṣajananī bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinīc prāvartata nadī raudrā kurusṛñjayasaṃkulāa tāṃ nadīṃ pitṛlokāya vahantīm atibhairavāmc terur vāhananaubhis te śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥa vartamāne tathā yuddhe nirmaryāde viśāṃ patec caturaṅgakṣaye ghore pūrvaṃ devāsuropamea akrośan bāndhavān anye tatra tatra paraṃtapac krośadbhir bāndhavaiś cānye bhayārtā na nivartirea nirmaryāde tathā yuddhe vartamāne bhayānakec arjuno bhīmasenaś ca mohayāṃ cakratuḥ parāna sā vadhyamānā mahatī senā tava janādhipac amuhyat tatra tatraiva yoṣin madavaśād ivaa mohayitvā ca tāṃ senāṃ bhīmasenadhanaṃjayauc dadhmatur vārijau tatra siṃhanādaṃ ca nedatuḥa śrutvaiva tu mahāśabdaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinauc dharmarājaṃ puraskṛtya madrarājam abhidrutaua tatrāścaryam apaśyāma ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec śalyena saṃgatāḥ śūrā yad ayudhyanta bhāgaśaḥa mādrīputrau sarabhasau kṛtāstrau yuddhadurmadauc abhyayātāṃ tvarāyuktau jigīṣantau balaṃ tavaa tato nyavartata balaṃ tāvakaṃ bharatarṣabhac śaraiḥ praṇunnaṃ bahudhā pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥa vadhyamānā camūḥ sā tu putrāṇāṃ prekṣatāṃ tavac bheje diśo mahārāja praṇunnā dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥe hāhākāro mahāñ jajñe yodhānāṃ tava bhārataa tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti vāg āsīd drāvitānāṃ mahātmanāmc kṣatriyāṇāṃ tadānyonyaṃ saṃyuge jayam icchatāme ādravann eva bhagnās te pāṇḍavais tava sainikāḥa tyaktvā yuddhe priyān putrān bhrātṝn atha pitāmahānc mātulān bhāgineyāṃś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavāna hayān dvipāṃs tvarayanto yodhā jagmuḥ samantataḥc ātmatrāṇakṛtotsāhās tāvakā bharatarṣabha saṃjaya uvācaa tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā madrarājaḥ pratāpavānc uvāca sārathiṃ tūrṇaṃ codayāśvān mahājavāna eṣa tiṣṭhati vai rājā pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena pāṇḍureṇa virājatāa atra māṃ prāpaya kṣipraṃ paśya me sārathe balamc na samarthā hi me pārthāḥ sthātum adya puro yudhia evam uktas tataḥ prāyān madrarājasya sārathiḥc yatra rājā satyasaṃdho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa āpatantaṃ ca sahasā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balamc dadhāraiko raṇe śalyo velevoddhṛtam arṇavama pāṇḍavānāṃ balaughas tu śalyam āsādya māriṣac vyatiṣṭhata tadā yuddhe sindhor vega ivācalama madrarājaṃ tu samare dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya viṣṭhitamc kuravaḥ saṃnyavartanta mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama teṣu rājan nivṛtteṣu vyūḍhānīkeṣu bhāgaśaḥc prāvartata mahāraudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇitodakaḥe samārchac citrasenena nakulo yuddhadurmadaḥf nātheva ca mahārāja citrasenas tu pāṇḍavama tau parasparam āsādya citrakārmukadhāriṇauc meghāv iva yathodvṛttau dakṣiṇottaravarṣiṇaua śaratoyaiḥ siṣicatus tau parasparam āhavec nāntaraṃ tatra paśyāmi pāṇḍavasyetarasya vāa ubhau kṛtāstrau balinau rathacaryāviśāradauc parasparavadhe yattau chidrānveṣaṇatatparaua citrasenas tu bhallena pītena niśitena cac nakulasya mahārāja muṣṭideśe cchinad dhanuḥa athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥc tribhiḥ śarair asaṃbhrānto lalāṭe vai samarpayata hayāṃś cāsya śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ preṣayām āsa mṛtyavec tathā dhvajaṃ sārathiṃ ca tribhis tribhir apātayata sa śatrubhujanirmuktair lalāṭasthais tribhiḥ śaraiḥc nakulaḥ śuśubhe rājaṃs triśṛṅga iva parvataḥa sa chinnadhanvā virathaḥ khaḍgam ādāya carma cac rathād avātarad vīraḥ śailāgrād iva kesarīa padbhyām āpatatas tasya śaravṛṣṭim avāsṛjatc nakulo py agrasat tāṃ vai carmaṇā laghuvikramaḥa citrasenarathaṃ prāpya citrayodhī jitaśramaḥc āruroha mahābāhuḥ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa sakuṇḍalaṃ samukuṭaṃ sunasaṃ svāyatekṣaṇamc citrasenaśiraḥ kāyād apāharata pāṇḍavaḥe sa papāta rathopasthād divākarasamaprabhaḥa citrasenaṃ viśastaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥb citrasenaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pāṇḍavasainikāḥb citraseno mahārāja nakulena hato raṇec sādhuvādasvanāṃś cakruḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca puṣkalāna viśastaṃ bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaputrau mahārathauc suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaś ca muñcantau niśitāñ śarāna tato bhyadhāvatāṃ tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ rathināṃ varamc jighāṃsantau yathā nāgaṃ vyāghrau rājan mahāvanea tāv abhyadhāvatāṃ tīkṣṇau dvāv apy enaṃ mahārathamc śaraughān samyag asyantau jīmūtau salilaṃ yathāa sa śaraiḥ sarvato viddhaḥ prahṛṣṭa iva pāṇḍavaḥb nakulo bharataśreṣṭhas tābhyāṃ parabalārdanaḥc anyat kārmukam ādāya ratham āruhya vīryavāne atiṣṭhata raṇe vīraḥ kruddharūpa ivāntakaḥa tasya tau bhrātarau rājañ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc rathaṃ viśakalīkartuṃ samārabdhau viśāṃ patea tataḥ prahasya nakulaś caturbhiś caturo raṇec jaghāna niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ satyasenasya vājinaḥa tataḥ saṃdhāya nārācaṃ rukmapuṅkhaṃ śilāśitamc dhanuś ciccheda rājendra satyasenasya pāṇḍavaḥa athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya dhanur ādāya cāparamc satyasenaḥ suṣeṇaś ca pāṇḍavaṃ paryadhāvatāma avidhyat tāv asaṃbhrāntau mādrīputraḥ pratāpavānc dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ mahārāja śarābhyāṃ raṇamūrdhania suṣeṇas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahad dhanuḥc ciccheda prahasan yuddhe kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya nakulaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc suṣeṇaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā dhvajam ekena cicchidea satyasenasya ca dhanur hastāvāpaṃ ca māriṣac ciccheda tarasā yuddhe tata uccukruśur janāḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya vegaghnaṃ bhārasādhanamc śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa samantāt pāṇḍunandanama saṃnivārya tu tān bāṇān nakulaḥ paravīrahāc satyasenaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām avidhyatad tataḥ śaktiṃ samudyamya satyasenāya cikṣipea tāv enaṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ pṛthak pṛthag ajihmagaiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya rājendra śarair vivyadhatuḥ śitaiḥa satyaseno ratheṣāṃ tu nakulasya dhanus tathāc pṛthak śarābhyāṃ ciccheda kṛtahastaḥ pratāpavāna sa rathe tirathas tiṣṭhan rathaśaktiṃ parāmṛśatc svarṇadaṇḍām akuṇṭhāgrāṃ tailadhautāṃ sunirmalāma lelihānām iva vibho nāgakanyāṃ mahāviṣāmc samudyamya ca cikṣepa satyasenasya saṃyugea sā tasya hṛdayaṃ saṃkhye bibheda śatadhā nṛpac sa papāta rathād bhūmau gatasattvo lpacetanaḥa bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā suṣeṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc abhyavarṣac charais tūrṇaṃ padātiṃ pāṇḍunandanamd caturbhiś caturo vāhān dhvajaṃ chittvā tu pañcabhiḥd tribhir vai sārathiṃ hatvā karṇaputro nanāda haa nakulaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā draupadeyo mahābalaḥc sutasomo bhidudrāva parīpsan pitaraṃ raṇea tato dhiruhya nakulaḥ sutasomasya taṃ rathamc śuśubhe bharataśreṣṭho giristha iva kesarīe so nyat kārmukam ādāya suṣeṇaṃ samayodhayata tāv ubhau śaravarṣābhyāṃ samāsādya parasparamc parasparavadhe yatnaṃ cakratuḥ sumahārathaua suṣeṇas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥc sutasomaṃ ca viṃśatyā bāhvor urasi cārpayata tataḥ kruddho mahārāja nakulaḥ paravīrahāc śarais tasya diśaḥ sarvāś chādayām āsa vīryavāna tato gṛhītvā tīkṣṇāgram ardhacandraṃ sutejanamc sa vegayuktaṃ cikṣepa karṇaputrasya saṃyugea tasya tena śiraḥ kāyāj jahāra nṛpasattamac paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavata sa hataḥ prāpatad rājan nakulena mahātmanāc nadīvegād ivārugṇas tīrajaḥ pādapo mahāna karṇaputravadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā nakulasya ca vikramamc pradudrāva bhayāt senā tāvakī bharatarṣabhaa tāṃ tu senāṃ mahārāja madrarājaḥ pratāpavānc apālayad raṇe śūraḥ senāpatir ariṃdamaḥd sā senā vidrutā rājan diśo daśa bhayadrutāa vibhīs tasthau mahārāja vyavasthāpya ca vāhinīmc siṃhanādaṃ bhṛśaṃ kṛtvā dhanuḥśabdaṃ ca dāruṇama tāvakāḥ samare rājan rakṣitā dṛḍhadhanvanāc pratyudyayur arātīṃs te samantād vigatavyathāḥa madrarājaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ parivārya samantataḥc sthitā rājan mahāsenā yoddhukāmāḥ samantataḥa sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ puraskṛtya hrīniṣedham ariṃdamama parivārya raṇe vīrāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrirec bāṇaśabdaravāṃś cogrān kṣveḍāṃś ca vividhān dadhuḥa tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve madrādhipatim añjasāc parivārya susaṃrabdhāḥ punar yuddham arocayana tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhanamc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama yathā devāsuraṃ yuddhaṃ pūrvam āsīd viśāṃ patec abhītānāṃ tathā rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanama tataḥ kapidhvajo rājan hatvā saṃśaptakān raṇec abhyadravata tāṃ senāṃ kauravīṃ pāṇḍunandanaḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śeṣā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥc abhyadhāvanta tāṃ senāṃ visṛjantaḥ śitāñ śarāna pāṇḍavair avakīrṇānāṃ saṃmohaḥ samajāyatac na ca jajñur anīkāni diśo vā pradiśas tathāa āpūryamāṇā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍavacoditaiḥc hatapravīrā vidhvastā kīryamāṇā samantataḥe kauravy avadhyata camūḥ pāṇḍuputrair mahārathaiḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavī senā śarai rājan samantataḥc raṇe hanyata putrais te śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa te sene bhṛśasaṃtapte vadhyamāne parasparamc vyākule samapadyetāṃ varṣāsu saritāv ivaa āviveśa tatas tīvraṃ tāvakānāṃ mahad bhayamc pāṇḍavānāṃ ca rājendra tathābhūte mahāhave saṃjaya uvācaa tasmin vilulite sainye vadhyamāne parasparamc dravamāṇeṣu yodheṣu ninadatsu ca dantiṣua kūjatāṃ stanatāṃ caiva padātīnāṃ mahāhavec vidruteṣu mahārāja hayeṣu bahudhā tadāa prakṣaye dāruṇe jāte saṃhāre sarvadehināmc nānāśastrasamāvāpe vyatiṣaktarathadvipea harṣaṇe yuddhaśauṇḍānāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhanec gāhamāneṣu yodheṣu parasparavadhaiṣiṣua prāṇādāne mahāghore vartamāne durodarec saṃgrāme ghorarūpe tu yamarāṣṭravivardhanea pāṇḍavās tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vyadhaman niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc tathaiva tāvakā yodhā jaghnuḥ pāṇḍavasainikāna tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne yuddhe bhīrubhayāvahec pūrvāhṇe caiva saṃprāpte bhāskarodayanaṃ pratia labdhalakṣāḥ pare rājan rakṣitāś ca mahātmanāc ayodhayaṃs tava balaṃ mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama balibhiḥ pāṇḍavair dṛptair labdhalakṣaiḥ prahāribhiḥc kauravy asīdat pṛtanā mṛgīvāgnisamākulāa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sīdatīṃ senāṃ paṅke gām iva durbalāmc ujjihīrṣus tadā śalyaḥ prāyāt pāṇḍucamūṃ pratia madrarājas tu saṃkruddho gṛhītvā dhanur uttamamc abhyadravata saṃgrāme pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥa pāṇḍavāś ca mahārāja samare jitakāśinaḥc madrarājaṃ samāsādya vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd tathaiva tāvakā yaudhā dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhirama tataḥ śaraśatais tīkṣṇair madrarājo mahābalaḥc ardayām āsa tāṃ senāṃ dharmarājasya paśyataḥa prādurāsaṃs tato rājan nānārūpāṇy anekaśaḥc cacāla śabdaṃ kurvāṇā mahī cāpi saparvatāa sadaṇḍaśūlā dīptāgrāḥ śīryamāṇāḥ samantataḥc ulkā bhūmiṃ divaḥ petur āhatya ravimaṇḍalama mṛgāś ca māhiṣāś cāpi pakṣiṇaś ca viśāṃ patec apasavyaṃ tadā cakruḥ senāṃ te bahuśo nṛpad bhṛgusūnudharāputrau śaśijena samanvitaud caramaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ purastāt sarvabhūbhujāmd śastrāgreṣv abhavaj jvālā netrāṇy āhatya varṣatīd śiraḥ svalīyanta bhṛśaṃ kākolūkāś ca ketuṣua tatas tad yuddham atyugram abhavat saṃghacāriṇāmc tathā sarvāṇy anīkāni saṃnipatya janādhipae abhyayuḥ kauravā rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma śalyas tu śaravarṣeṇa varṣann iva sahasradṛkc abhyavarṣad adīnātmā kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama bhīmasenaṃ śaraiś cāpi rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaḥc draupadeyāṃs tathā sarvān mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaua dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca śaineyaṃ śikhaṇḍinam athāpi cac ekaikaṃ daśabhir bāṇair vivyādha ca mahābalaḥe tato sṛjad bāṇavarṣaṃ gharmānte maghavān ivaa tataḥ prabhadrakā rājan somakāś ca sahasraśaḥc patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca dṛśyante śalyasāyakaiḥa bhramarāṇām iva vrātāḥ śalabhānām iva vrajāḥc hrādinya iva meghebhyaḥ śalyasya nyapatañ śarāḥa dviradās turagāś cārtāḥ pattayo rathinas tathāc śalyasya bāṇair nyapatan babhramur vyanadaṃs tathāa āviṣṭa iva madreśo manyunā pauruṣeṇa cac prācchādayad arīn saṃkhye kālasṛṣṭa ivāntakaḥe vinardamāno madreśo meghahrādo mahābalaḥa sā vadhyamānā śalyena pāṇḍavānām anīkinīb pradudrāva mahārāja śalyabāṇaiḥ prapīḍitāc ajātaśatruṃ kaunteyam abhyadhāvad yudhiṣṭhirama tāṃ samarpya tataḥ saṃkhye laghuhastaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥc śaravarṣeṇa mahatā yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayatd vavarṣa samare kruddho dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama tam āpatantaṃ pattyaśvaiḥ kruddho rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc avārayac charais tīkṣṇair mattaṃ dvipam ivāṅkuśaiḥa tasya śalyaḥ śaraṃ ghoraṃ mumocāśīviṣopamamc so bhyavidhyan mahātmānaṃ vegenābhyapatac ca gāma tato vṛkodaraḥ kruddhaḥ śalyaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥc pañcabhiḥ sahadevas tu nakulo daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa draupadeyāś ca śatrughnaṃ śūram ārtāyaniṃ śaraiḥc abhyavarṣan mahābhāgaṃ meghā iva mahīdharama tato dṛṣṭvā tudyamānaṃ śalyaṃ pārthaiḥ samantataḥc kṛtavarmā kṛpaś caiva saṃkruddhāv abhyadhāvatāma ulūkaś ca patatrī ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc smayamānaś ca śanakair aśvatthāmā mahārathaḥe tava putrāś ca kārtsnyena jugupuḥ śalyam āhavea bhīmasenaṃ tribhir viddhvā kṛtavarmā śilīmukhaiḥc bāṇavarṣeṇa mahatā kruddharūpam avārayata dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛpaḥ kruddho bāṇavarṣair apīḍayatc draupadeyāṃś ca śakunir yamau ca drauṇir abhyayāta duryodhano yudhāṃ śreṣṭhāv āhave keśavārjunauc samabhyayād ugratejāḥ śaraiś cābhyahanad balīa evaṃ dvaṃdvaśatāny āsaṃs tvadīyānāṃ paraiḥ sahac ghorarūpāṇi citrāṇi tatra tatra viśāṃ patea ṛśyavarṇāñ jaghānāśvān bhojo bhīmasya saṃyugec so vatīrya rathopasthād dhatāśvaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥe kālo daṇḍam ivodyamya gadāpāṇir ayudhyataa pramukhe sahadevasya jaghānāśvāṃś ca madrarāṭc tataḥ śalyasya tanayaṃ sahadevo sināvadhīta gautamaḥ punar ācāryo dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayatc asaṃbhrāntam asaṃbhrānto yatnavān yatnavattarama draupadeyāṃs tathā vīrān ekaikaṃ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥc avidhyad ācāryasuto nātikruddhaḥ smayann ivad yuktāśvasya punar madhyaṃ rathasyāroham icchataḥd punaś ca bhīmasenasya jaghānāśvāṃs tathāhaved so vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ hatāśvaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥd kālo daṇḍam ivodyamya gadāṃ kruddho mahābalaḥd pothayām āsa turagān rathaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇaḥd kṛtavarmā tv avaplutya rathāt tasmād apākramata śalyo pi rājan saṃkruddho nighnan somakapāṇḍavānc punar eva śitair bāṇair yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayata tasya bhīmo raṇe kruddhaḥ saṃdaṣṭadaśanacchadaḥc vināśāyābhisaṃdhāya gadām ādatta vīryavāna yamadaṇḍapratīkāśāṃ kālarātrim ivodyatāmc gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇāntakaraṇīm apia hemapaṭṭaparikṣiptām ulkāṃ prajvalitām ivac śaikyāṃ vyālīm ivātyugrāṃ vajrakalpām ayasmayīma candanāgurupaṅkāktāṃ pramadām īpsitām ivac vasāmedosṛgādigdhāṃ jihvāṃ vaivasvatīm ivaa paṭughaṇṭāravaśatāṃ vāsavīm aśanīm ivac nirmuktāśīviṣākārāṃ pṛktāṃ gajamadair apia trāsanīṃ ripusainyānāṃ svasainyapariharṣiṇīmc manuṣyaloke vikhyātāṃ giriśṛṅgavidāriṇīma yayā kailāsabhavane maheśvarasakhaṃ balīc āhvayām āsa kaunteyaḥ saṃkruddham alakādhipama yayā māyāvino dṛptān subahūn dhanadālayec jaghāna guhyakān kruddho mandārārthe mahābalaḥe nivāryamāṇo bahubhir draupadyāḥ priyam āsthitaḥa tāṃ vajramaṇiratnaughām aṣṭāśriṃ vajragauravāmc samudyamya mahābāhuḥ śalyam abhyadravad raṇea gadayā yuddhakuśalas tayā dāruṇanādayāc pothayām āsa śalyasya caturo śvān mahājavāna tataḥ śalyo raṇe kruddhaḥ pīne vakṣasi tomaramc nicakhāna nadan vīro varma bhittvā ca so bhyagāta vṛkodaras tv asaṃbhrātas tam evoddhṛtya tomaramb cikṣepa bhīmasenasya so sravac choṇitaṃ bahub tam evādāya bhīmas tu tataḥ kopasamanvitaḥc yantāraṃ madrarājasya nirbibheda tato hṛdia sa bhinnavarmā rudhiraṃ vaman vitrastamānasaḥc papātābhimukho dīno madrarājas tv apākramata kṛtapratikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyo vismitamānasaḥc gadām āśritya dhīrātmā pratyamitram avaikṣataa tataḥ sumanasaḥ pārthā bhīmasenam apūjayanb viyatsthitā jātaharṣās tataḥ siddhā babhāṣireb pūrvajanmani prahlādo dṛṣṭo smābhir ayaṃ baliḥc tad dṛṣṭvā karma saṃgrāme ghoram akliṣṭakarmaṇaḥd taṃ dṛṣṭvā karma śalyasya sarvasiddhās tv apūjayan saṃjaya uvācaa patitaṃ prekṣya yantāraṃ śalyaḥ sarvāyasīṃ gadāmc ādāya tarasā rājaṃs tasthau girir ivācalaḥa taṃ dīptam iva kālāgniṃ pāśahastam ivāntakamc saśṛṅgam iva kailāsaṃ savajram iva vāsavama saśūlam iva haryakṣaṃ vane mattam iva dvipama   sacakram iva cakriṇama saśaktim iva senānyaṃc javenābhyapatad bhīmaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmd madrarājam asaṃbhrāntaḥ paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvināma tataḥ śaṅkhapraṇādaś ca tūryāṇāṃ ca sahasraśaḥc siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanaḥa prekṣantaḥ sarvatas tau hi yodhā yodhamahādvipauc tāvakāś ca pare caiva sādhu sādhv ity athābruvana na hi madrādhipād anyo rāmād vā yadunandanātc soḍhum utsahate vegaṃ bhīmasenasya saṃyugea tathā madrādhipasyāpi gadāvegaṃ mahātmanaḥc soḍhum utsahate nānyo yodho yudhi vṛkodarāta tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥc āvalgitau gadāhastau madrarājavṛkodaraua maṇḍalāvartamārgeṣu gadāviharaṇeṣu cac nirviśeṣam abhūd yuddhaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥa taptahemamayaiḥ śubhrair babhūva bhayavardhanīc agnijvālair ivāviddhā paṭṭaiḥ śalyasya sā gadāa tathaiva carato mārgān maṇḍaleṣu mahātmanaḥc vidyud abhrapratīkāśā bhīmasya śuśubhe gadāa tāḍitā madrarājena bhīmasya gadayā gadāc dīpyamāneva vai rājan sasṛje pāvakārciṣaḥa tathā bhīmena śalyasya tāḍitā gadayā gadāc aṅgāravarṣaṃ mumuce tad adbhutam ivābhavata dantair iva mahānāgau śṛṅgair iva maharṣabhauc tottrair iva tadānyonyaṃ gadāgrābhyāṃ nijaghnatuḥa tau gadānihatair gātraiḥ kṣaṇena rudhirokṣitauc prekṣaṇīyatarāv āstāṃ puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukaua gadayā madrarājena savyadakṣiṇam āhataḥc bhīmaseno mahābāhur na cacālācalo yathāa tathā bhīmagadāvegais tāḍyamāno muhur muhuḥc śalyo na vivyathe rājan dantinevāhato giriḥa śuśruve dikṣu sarvāsu tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥc gadānipātasaṃhrādo vajrayor iva nisvanaḥa nivṛtya tu mahāvīryau samucchritagadāv ubhauc punar antaramārgasthau maṇḍalāni viceratuḥa athābhyetya padāny aṣṭau saṃnipāto bhavat tayoḥc udyamya lohadaṇḍābhyām atimānuṣakarmaṇoḥa prārthayānau tadānyo nyaṃ maṇḍalāni viceratuḥc kriyāviśeṣaṃ kṛtinau darśayām āsatus tadāa athodyamya gade ghore saśṛṅgāv iva parvatauc tāv ājaghnatur anyonyaṃ yathā bhūmicale calaua tau parasparavegāc ca gadābhyāṃ ca bhṛśāhatauc yugapat petatur vīrāv ubhāv indradhvajāv ivaa ubhayoḥ senayor vīrās tadā hāhākṛto bhavanc bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy abhihatāv ubhāv āstāṃ suvihvalaua tataḥ sagadam āropya madrāṇām ṛṣabhaṃ rathec apovāha kṛpaḥ śalyaṃ tūrṇam āyodhanād apia kṣībavad vihvalatvāt tu nimeṣāt punar utthitaḥc bhīmaseno gadāpāṇiḥ samāhvayata madrapama tatas tu tāvakāḥ śūrā nānāśastrasamāyutāḥc nānāvāditraśabdena pāṇḍusenām ayodhayana bhujāv ucchritya śastraṃ ca śabdena mahatā tataḥc abhyadravan mahārāja duryodhanapurogamāḥa tad anīkam abhiprekṣya tatas te pāṇḍunandanāḥc prayayuḥ siṃhanādena duryodhanavadhepsayāa teṣām āpatatāṃ tūrṇaṃ putras te bharatarṣabhac prāsena cekitānaṃ vai vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśama sa papāta rathopasthe tava putreṇa tāḍitaḥc rudhiraughapariklinnaḥ praviśya vipulaṃ tamaḥa cekitānaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc prasaktam abhyavarṣanta śaravarṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥa tāvakānām anīkeṣu pāṇḍavā jitakāśinaḥc vyacaranta mahārāja prekṣaṇīyāḥ samantataḥa kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca saubalaś ca mahābalaḥc ayodhayan dharmarājaṃ madrarājapuraskṛtāḥa bhāradvājasya hantāraṃ bhūrivīryaparākramamc duryodhano mahārāja dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayata trisāhasrā rathā rājaṃs tava putreṇa coditāḥc ayodhayanta vijayaṃ droṇaputrapuraskṛtāḥa vijaye dhṛtasaṃkalpāḥ samabhityaktajīvitāḥc prāviśaṃs tāvakā rājan haṃsā iva mahat saraḥa tato yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ parasparavadhaiṣiṇāmc anyonyavadhasaṃyuktam anyonyaprītivardhanama tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme rājan vīravarakṣayec anileneritaṃ ghoram uttasthau pārthivaṃ rajaḥa śravaṇān nāmadheyānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca kīrtanātc parasparaṃ vijānīmo ye cāyudhyann abhītavata tad rajaḥ puruṣavyāghra śoṇitena praśāmitamc diśaś ca vimalā jajñus tasmin rajasi śāmitea tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme ghorarūpe bhayānakec tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥa brahmalokaparā bhūtvā prārthayanto jayaṃ yudhic suyuddhena parākrāntā narāḥ svargam abhīpsavaḥa bhartṛpiṇḍavimokṣārthaṃ bhartṛkāryaviniścitāḥc svargasaṃsaktamanaso yodhā yuyudhire tadāa nānārūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥc anyonyam abhigarjantaḥ praharantaḥ parasparama hata vidhyata gṛhṇīta praharadhvaṃ nikṛntatac iti sma vācaḥ śrūyante tava teṣāṃ ca vai balea tataḥ śalyo mahārāja dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc vivyādha niśitair bāṇair hantukāmo mahārathama tasya pārtho mahārāja nārācān vai caturdaśac marmāṇy uddiśya marmajño nicakhāna hasann ivaa taṃ vārya pāṇḍavaṃ bāṇair hantukāmo mahāyaśāḥc vivyādha samare kruddho bahubhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥa atha bhūyo mahārāja śareṇa nataparvaṇāc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samājaghne sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa dharmarājo pi saṃkruddho madrarājaṃ mahāyaśāḥc vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥa candrasenaṃ ca saptatyā sūtaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥc drumasenaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā nijaghāna mahārathaḥa cakrarakṣe hate śalyaḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanāc nijaghāna tato rājaṃś cedīn vai pañcaviṃśatima sātyakiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā bhīmasenaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc mādrīputrau śatenājau vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa evaṃ vicaratas tasya saṃgrāme rājasattamac saṃpreṣayac chitān pārthaḥ śarān āśīviṣopamāna dhvajāgraṃ cāsya samare kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc pramukhe vartamānasya bhallenāpaharad rathāta pāṇḍuputreṇa vai tasya ketuṃ chinnaṃ mahātmanāc nipatantam apaśyāma giriśṛṅgam ivāhatama dhvajaṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavaṃ ca vyavasthitamc saṃkruddho madrarājo bhūc charavarṣaṃ mumoca haa śalyaḥ sāyakavarṣeṇa parjanya iva vṛṣṭimānc abhyavarṣad ameyātmā kṣatriyaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhaḥa sātyakiṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc ekaikaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayata tato bāṇamayaṃ jālaṃ vitataṃ pāṇḍavorasic apaśyāma mahārāja meghajālam ivodgatama tasya śalyo raṇe kruddho bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc diśaḥ pracchādayām āsa pradiśaś ca mahārathaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bāṇajālena pīḍitaḥc babhūva hṛtavikrānto jambho vṛtrahaṇā yathā saṃjaya uvācaa pīḍite dharmarāje tu madrarājena māriṣac sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaue parivārya rathaiḥ śalyaṃ pīḍayām āsur āhavea tam ekaṃ bahubhir dṛṣṭvā pīḍyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥc sādhuvādo mahāñ jajñe siddhāś cāsan praharṣitāḥe āścaryam ity abhāṣanta munayaś cāpi saṃgatāḥa bhīmaseno raṇe śalyaṃ śalyabhūtaṃ parākramec ekena viddhvā bāṇena punar vivyādha saptabhiḥa sātyakiś ca śatenainaṃ dharmaputraparīpsayāc madreśvaram avākīrya siṃhanādam athānadata nakulaḥ pañcabhiś cainaṃ sahadevaś ca saptabhiḥc viddhvā taṃ tu tatas tūrṇaṃ punar vivyādha saptabhiḥa sa tu śūro raṇe yattaḥ pīḍitas tair mahārathaiḥc vikṛṣya kārmukaṃ ghoraṃ vegaghnaṃ bhārasādhanama sātyakiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā śalyo vivyādha māriṣac bhīmasenaṃ trisaptatyā nakulaṃ saptabhis tathāa tataḥ saviśikhaṃ cāpaṃ sahadevasya dhanvinaḥc chittvā bhallena samare vivyādhainaṃ trisaptabhiḥa sahadevas tu samare mātulaṃ bhūrivarcasamc sajyam anyad dhanuḥ kṛtvā pañcabhiḥ samatāḍayate śarair āśīviṣākārair jvalaj jvalanasaṃnibhaiḥa sārathiṃ cāsya samare śareṇānataparvaṇāc vivyādha bhṛśasaṃkruddhas taṃ ca bhūyas tribhiḥ śaraiḥa bhīmasenas trisaptatyā sātyakir navabhiḥ śaraiḥc dharmarājas tathā ṣaṣṭyā gātre śalyaṃ samarpayatc   pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥc gātre bāṇais tu te sarve śūrāḥ sarve samarpayana tataḥ śalyo mahārāja nirviddhas tair mahārathaiḥc susrāva rudhiraṃ gātrair gairikaṃ parvato yathāa tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsān pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha tarasā rājaṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavata tato pareṇa bhallena dharmaputrasya māriṣac dhanuś ciccheda samare sajyaṃ sa sumahārathaḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya dharmaputro mahārathaḥc sāśvasūtadhvajarathaṃ śalyaṃ prācchādayac charaiḥa sa cchādyamānaḥ samare dharmaputrasya sāyakaiḥc yudhiṣṭhiram athāvidhyad daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd evaṃ dvaṃdvaśatāny āsaṃs tvadīyānāṃ paraiḥ sahaa sātyakis tu tataḥ kruddho dharmaputre śarārditec madrāṇām adhipaṃ śūraṃ śaraughaiḥ samavārayata sa sātyakeḥ praciccheda kṣurapreṇa mahad dhanuḥc bhīmasenamukhāṃs tāṃś ca tribhis tribhir atāḍayata tasya kruddho mahārāja sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc tomaraṃ preṣayām āsa svarṇadaṇḍaṃ mahādhanama bhīmaseno tha nārācaṃ jvalantam iva pannagamc nakulaḥ samare śaktiṃ sahadevo gadāṃ śubhāme dharmarājaḥ śataghnīṃ tu jighāṃsuḥ śalyam āhavef teṣāṃ patanti śastrāṇi bahubhiḥ sāyakair yudhia tān āpatata evāśu pañcānāṃ vai bhujacyutānb vārayām āsa samare śastrasaṃghaiḥ sa madrarāṭb ciccheda samare rājan sarveṣāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthakc sātyakiprahitaṃ śalyo bhallaiś ciccheda tomarama bhīmena prahitaṃ cāpi śaraṃ kanakabhūṣaṇamc dvidhā ciccheda samare kṛtahastaḥ pratāpavāna nakulapreṣitāṃ śaktiṃ hemadaṇḍāṃ bhayāvahāmc gadāṃ ca sahadevena śaraughaiḥ samavārayata śarābhyāṃ ca śataghnīṃ tāṃ rājñaś ciccheda bhāratac paśyatāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda cae nāmṛṣyat taṃ tu śaineyaḥ śatror vijayam āhavea athānyad dhanur ādāya sātyakiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc dvābhyāṃ madreśvaraṃ viddhvā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ śalyo mahārāja sarvāṃs tān daśabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha subhṛśaṃ kruddhas tottrair iva mahādvipāna te vāryamāṇāḥ samare madrarājñā mahārathāḥc na śekuḥ pramukhe sthātuṃ tasya śatruniṣūdanāḥa tato duryodhano rājā dṛṣṭvā śalyasya vikramamc nihatān pāṇḍavān mene pāñcālān atha sṛñjayānd tathāvidhaṃ mahārāja madrarājasya vikramamd asahyaṃ mānavair yuddhe tad babhūva nararṣabhaa tato rājan mahābāhur bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc saṃtyajya manasā prāṇān madrādhipam ayodhayata nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc parivārya tadā śalyaṃ samantād vyakirañ śaraiḥa sa caturbhir maheṣvāsaiḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaiḥc vṛtas tān yodhayām āsa madrarājaḥ pratāpavāna tasya dharmasuto rājan kṣurapreṇa mahāhavec cakrarakṣaṃ jaghānāśu madrarājasya pārthivaa tasmiṃs tu nihate śūre cakrarakṣe mahārathec madrarājo tibalavān sainikān āstṛṇoc charaiḥa samācchannāṃs tatas tāṃs tu rājan vīkṣya sa sainikānc cintayām āsa samare dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa kathaṃ nu na bhavet satyaṃ tan mādhavavaco mahatc na hi kruddho raṇe rājā kṣapayeta balaṃ mamad ahaṃ madbhrātaraś caiva sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥd pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāś caiva na śaktāś ca hi madrapamd nihaniṣyati ced adya mātulo smān mahāyaśāḥd govindavacanaṃ satyaṃ kathaṃ bhavati kiṃ tv idama tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac madreśvaraṃ samāseduḥ pīḍayantaḥ samantataḥa nānāśastraughabahulāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitāmc vyadhamat samare rājan mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥa tataḥ kanakapuṅkhāṃ tāṃ śalyakṣiptāṃ viyadgatāmc śaravṛṣṭim apaśyāma śalabhānām ivātatima te śarā madrarājena preṣitā raṇamūrdhanic saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante śalabhānāṃ vrajā ivaa madrarājadhanurmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥc nirantaram ivākāśaṃ saṃbabhūva janādhipaa na pāṇḍavānāṃ nāsmākaṃ tatra kaś cid vyadṛśyatac bāṇāndhakāre mahati kṛte tatra mahābhayea madrarājena balinā lāghavāc charavṛṣṭibhiḥc loḍyamānaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ balārṇavame vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmur devagandharvadānavāḥa sa tu tān sarvato yattāñ śaraiḥ saṃpīḍya māriṣac dharmarājam avacchādya siṃhavad vyanadan muhuḥa te channāḥ samare tena pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc na śekus taṃ tadā yuddhe pratyudyātuṃ mahārathama dharmarājapurogās tu bhīmasenamukhā rathāḥc na jahuḥ samare śūraṃ śalyam āhavaśobhinam saṃjaya uvācaa arjuno drauṇinā viddho yuddhe bahubhir āyasaiḥc tasya cānucaraiḥ śūrais trigartānāṃ mahārathaiḥe drauṇiṃ vivyādha samare tribhir eva śilīmukhaiḥa tathetarān maheṣvāsān dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc bhūyaś caiva mahābāhuḥ śaravarṣair avākirata śarakaṇṭakitās te tu tāvakā bharatarṣabhac na jahuḥ samare pārthaṃ vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa te rjunaṃ rathavaṃśena droṇaputrapurogamāḥc ayodhayanta samare parivārya mahārathāḥd parivārya mudā yuktā yodhayantaś cakāśirea tais tu kṣiptāḥ śarā rājan kārtasvaravibhūṣitāḥc arjunasya rathopasthaṃ pūrayām āsur añjasāa tathā kṛṣṇau maheṣvāsau vṛṣabhau sarvadhanvināmc śarair vīkṣya vitunnāṅgau prahṛṣṭau yuddhadurmadaua kūbaraṃ rathacakrāṇi īṣā yoktrāṇi cābhibhoc yugaṃ caivānukarṣaṃ ca śarabhūtam abhūt tadāa naitādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ rājan naiva ca naḥ śrutamc yādṛśaṃ tatra pārthasya tāvakāḥ saṃpracakrirea sa rathaḥ sarvato bhāti citrapuṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥc ulkāśataiḥ saṃpradīptaṃ vimānam iva bhūtalea tato rjuno mahārāja śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc avākirat tāṃ pṛtanāṃ megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalama te vadhyamānāḥ samare pārthanāmāṅkitaiḥ śaraiḥc pārthabhūtam amanyanta prekṣamāṇās tathāvidhama tato dbhutaśarajvālo dhanuḥśabdānilo mahānc senendhanaṃ dadāhāśu tāvakaṃ pārthapāvakaḥa cakrāṇāṃ patatāṃ caiva yugānāṃ ca dharātalec tūṇīrāṇāṃ patākānāṃ dhvajānāṃ ca rathaiḥ sahad īṣāṇāṃ cāpi yoktrāṇāṃ veṇūnāṃ cāpi sarvaśaḥd bhujānāṃ śirasāṃ caiva chattrāṇāṃ vyajanaiḥ sahad tatra kruddhasya pārthasya agamyā samabhūd dharāa īṣāṇām anukarṣāṇāṃ triveṇūnāṃ ca bhāratac akṣāṇām atha yoktrāṇāṃ pratodānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥa śirasāṃ patatāṃ caiva kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣadhāriṇāmc bhujānāṃ ca mahārāja skandhānāṃ ca samantataḥd sarveṣāṃ patatāṃ caiva chattrāṇāṃ ca samantataḥa chatrāṇāṃ vyajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ mukuṭānāṃ ca rāśayaḥc samadṛśyanta pārthasya rathamārgeṣu bhāratad tataḥ kruddhasya pārthasya rathamārge viśāṃ patea agamyarūpā pṛthivī māṃsaśoṇitakardamāc babhūva bharataśreṣṭha rudrasyākrīḍanaṃ yathāe bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananī śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanīa hatvā tu samare pārthaḥ sahasre dve paraṃtapac rathānāṃ savarūthānāṃ vidhūmo gnir iva jvalana yathā hi bhagavān agnir jagad dagdhvā carācaramc vidhūmo dṛśyate rājaṃs tathā pārtho mahārathaḥa drauṇis tu samare dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavasya parākramamc rathenātipatākena pāṇḍavaṃ pratyavārayata tāv ubhau puruṣavyāghrau śvetāśvau dhanvināṃ varauc samīyatus tadā tūrṇaṃ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaua tayor āsīn mahārāja bāṇavarṣaṃ sudāruṇamc jīmūtānāṃ yathā vṛṣṭis tapānte bharatarṣabhaa anyonyaspardhinau tau tu śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc tatakṣatur mṛdhe nyonyaṃ śṛṅgābhyāṃ vṛṣabhāv ivaa tayor yuddhaṃ mahārāja ciraṃ samam ivābhavatc astrāṇāṃ saṃgamaś caiva ghoras tatrābhavan mahāna tato rjunaṃ dvādaśabhī rukmapuṅkhaiḥ sutejanaiḥc vāsudevaṃ ca daśabhir drauṇir vivyādha bhārataa tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥc mānayitvā muhūrtaṃ ca guruputraṃ mahāhaved nirucchvāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā guruputraṃ mahāmanāḥd so sṛjat sāyakān saṃkhye arjuno jayatāṃ varaḥd caturbhiḥ sāyakaiś caiva tāḍayām āsa ghoṭakāna vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre savyasācī mahārathaḥc mṛdupūrvaṃ tataś cainaṃ tribhir vivyādha sāyakaiḥa hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan droṇaputras tv ayasmayamb yamadaṇḍanibhaṃ ghoraṃ śatrusainyabhayaṃkaramc musalaṃ pāṇḍuputrāya cikṣepa parighopamama tam āpatantaṃ sahasā hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitamc ciccheda saptadhā vīraḥ pārthaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥa sa cchinnaṃ musalaṃ dṛṣṭvā drauṇiḥ paramakopanaḥc ādade parighaṃ ghoraṃ nagendraśikharopamame cikṣepa caiva pārthāya drauṇir yuddhaviśāradaḥa tam antakam iva kruddhaṃ parighaṃ prekṣya pāṇḍavaḥc arjunas tvarito jaghne pañcabhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥa sa cchinnaḥ patito bhūmau pārthabāṇair mahāhavec dārayan pṛthivīndrāṇāṃ manaḥ śabdena bhārataa tato parais tribhir bāṇair drauṇiṃ vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥc so tividdho balavatā pārthena sumahābalaḥe na saṃbhrāntas tadā drauṇiḥ pauruṣe sve vyavasthitaḥa sudharmā tu tato rājan bhāradvājaṃ mahārathamc avākirac charavrātaiḥ sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥa tatas tu suratho py ājau pāñcālānāṃ mahārathaḥc rathena meghaghoṣeṇa drauṇim evābhyadhāvataa vikarṣan vai dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvabhārasahaṃ dṛḍhamc jvalanāśīviṣanibhaiḥ śaraiś cainam avākirata surathaṃ tu tataḥ kruddham āpatantaṃ mahārathamc cukopa samare drauṇir daṇḍāhata ivoragaḥa triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā sṛkkiṇī parilelihanc udvīkṣya surathaṃ roṣād dhanurjyām avamṛjya cae mumoca tīkṣṇaṃ nārācaṃ yamadaṇḍasamadyutima sa tasya hṛdayaṃ bhittvā praviveśātivegataḥc śakrāśanir ivotsṛṣṭā vidārya dharaṇītalama tatas taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau nārācena samāhatamc vajreṇeva yathā śṛṅgaṃ parvatasya mahādhanama tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ tam eva rathināṃ varaḥa tataḥ sajjo mahārāja drauṇir āhavadurmadaḥc arjunaṃ yodhayām āsa saṃśaptakavṛto raṇea tatra yuddhaṃ mahac cāsīd arjunasya paraiḥ sahac madhyaṃdinagate sūrye yamarāṣṭravivardhanama tatrāścaryam apaśyāma dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ parākramamc yad eko yugapad vīrān samayodhayad arjunaḥa vimardas tu mahān āsīd arjunasya paraiḥ sahac śatakrator yathā pūrvaṃ mahatyā daityasenayā saṃjaya uvācaa duryodhano mahārāja dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc cakratuḥ sumahad yuddhaṃ śaraśaktisamākulama tayor āsan mahārāja śaradhārāḥ sahasraśaḥc ambudānāṃ yathā kāle jaladhārāḥ samantataḥa rājā tu pārṣataṃ viddhvā śaraiḥ pañcabhir āyasaiḥc droṇahantāram ugreṣuḥ punar vivyādha saptabhiḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare balavān dṛḍhavikramaḥc saptatyā viśikhānāṃ vai duryodhanam apīḍayata pīḍitaṃ prekṣya rājānaṃ sodaryā bharatarṣabhac mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ parivavruḥ sma pārṣatama sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūraiḥ sarvato tirathair bhṛśamc vyacarat samare rājan darśayan hastalāghavama śikhaṇḍī kṛtavarmāṇaṃ gautamaṃ ca mahārathamc prabhadrakaiḥ samāyukto yodhayām āsa dhanvinaua tatrāpi sumahad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec prāṇān saṃtyajatāṃ yuddhe prāṇadyūtābhidevanea śalyas tu śaravarṣāṇi vimuñcan sarvatodiśamc pāṇḍavān pīḍayām āsa sasātyakivṛkodarāna tathobhau ca yamau yuddhe yamatulyaparākramauc yodhayām āsa rājendra vīryeṇa ca balena caa śalyasāyakanunnānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāmṛdhec trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta ke cit tatra mahārathāḥa tatas tu nakulaḥ śūro dharmarāje prapīḍitec abhidudrāva vegena mātulaṃ mādrinandanaḥa saṃchādya samare śalyaṃ nakulaḥ paravīrahāc vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ smayamānaḥ stanāntarea sarvapāraśavair bāṇaiḥ karmāraparimārjitaiḥc svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilādhautair dhanuryantrapracoditaiḥa śalyas tu pīḍitas tena svasrīyeṇa mahātmanāc nakulaṃ pīḍayām āsa patribhir nataparvabhiḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmaseno tha sātyakiḥc sahadevaś ca mādreyo madrarājam upādravana tān āpatata evāśu pūrayānān rathasvanaiḥc diśaś ca pradiśaś caiva kampayānāṃś ca medinīme pratijagrāha samare senāpatir amitrajita yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tribhir viddhvā bhīmasenaṃ ca saptabhiḥc sātyakiṃ ca śatenājau sahadevaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tatas tu saśaraṃ cāpaṃ nakulasya mahātmanaḥc madreśvaraḥ kṣurapreṇa tadā ciccheda māriṣae tad aśīryata vicchinnaṃ dhanuḥ śalyasya sāyakaiḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya mādrīputro mahārathaḥc madrarājarathaṃ tūrṇaṃ pūrayām āsa patribhiḥa yudhiṣṭhiras tu madreśaṃ sahadevaś ca māriṣac daśabhir daśabhir bāṇair urasy enam avidhyatāma bhīmasenas tataḥ ṣaṣṭyā sātyakir navabhiḥ śaraiḥc madrarājam abhidrutya jaghnatuḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥa madrarājas tataḥ kruddhaḥ sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha bhūyaḥ saptatyā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇāma athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ muṣṭau ciccheda māriṣac hayāṃś ca caturaḥ saṃkhye preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea virathaṃ sātyakiṃ kṛtvā madrarājo mahābalaḥc viśikhānāṃ śatenainam ājaghāna samantataḥa mādrīputrau tu saṃrabdhau bhīmasenaṃ ca pāṇḍavamc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca kauravya vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma madrarājasya pauruṣamc yad enaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā nābhyavartanta saṃyugea athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc pīḍitān pāṇḍavān dṛṣṭvā madrarājavaśaṃ gatāne abhidudrāva vegena madrāṇām adhipaṃ balīa āpatantaṃ rathaṃ tasya śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥc pratyudyayau rathenaiva matto mattam iva dvipama sa saṃnipātas tumulo babhūvādbhutadarśanaḥc sātyakeś caiva śūrasya madrāṇām adhipasya cae yādṛśo vai purā vṛttaḥ śambarāmararājayoḥa sātyakiḥ prekṣya samare madrarājaṃ vyavasthitamc vivyādha daśabhir bāṇais tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta madrarājas tu subhṛśaṃ viddhas tena mahātmanāc sātyakiṃ prativivyādha citrapuṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ pārthā maheṣvāsāḥ sātvatābhisṛtaṃ nṛpamc abhyadravan rathais tūrṇaṃ mātulaṃ vadhakāmyayāa tata āsīt parāmardas tumulaḥ śoṇitodakaḥc śūrāṇāṃ yudhyamānānāṃ siṃhānām iva nardatāma teṣām āsīn mahārāja vyatikṣepaḥ parasparamc siṃhānām āmiṣepsūnāṃ kūjatām iva saṃyugea teṣāṃ bāṇasahasraughair ākīrṇā vasudhābhavatc antarikṣaṃ ca sahasā bāṇabhūtam abhūt tadāa śarāndhakāraṃ bahudhā kṛtaṃ tatra samantataḥc abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe śarair muktair mahātmabhiḥa tatra rājañ śarair muktair nirmuktair iva pannagaiḥc svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ prakāśadbhir vyarocanta diśas tathāa tatrādbhutaṃ paraṃ cakre śalyaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥc yad ekaḥ samare śūro yodhayām āsa vai bahūna madrarājabhujotsṛṣṭaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥc saṃpatadbhiḥ śarair ghorair avākīryata medinīa tatra śalyarathaṃ rājan vicarantaṃ mahāhavec apaśyāma yathā pūrvaṃ śakrasyāsurasaṃkṣaye saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ sainyās tava vibho madrarājapuraskṛtāḥc punar abhyadravan pārthān vegena mahatā raṇea pīḍitās tāvakāḥ sarve pradhāvanto raṇotkaṭāḥc kṣaṇenaiva ca pārthāṃs te bahutvāt samaloḍayana te vadhyamānāḥ kurubhiḥ pāṇḍavā nāvatasthirec nivāryamāṇā bhīmena paśyatoḥ kṛṣṇapārthayoḥa tato dhanaṃjayaḥ kruddhaḥ kṛpaṃ saha padānugaiḥc avākirac charaugheṇa kṛtavarmāṇam eva caa śakuniṃ sahadevas tu sahasainyam avārayatc nakulaḥ pārśvataḥ sthitvā madrarājam avaikṣataa draupadeyā narendrāṃś ca bhūyiṣṭhaṃ samavārayanc droṇaputraṃ ca pāñcālyaḥ śikhaṇḍī samavārayata bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ gadāpāṇir avārayatc śalyaṃ tu saha sainyena kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ saṃsaktaṃ tatra tatra hac tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃgrāmeṣv anivartināma tatra paśyāmahe karma śalyasyātimahad raṇec yad ekaḥ sarvasainyāni pāṇḍavānām ayudhyataa vyadṛśyata tadā śalyo yudhiṣṭhirasamīpataḥc raṇe candramaso bhyāśe śanaiścara iva grahaḥa pīḍayitvā tu rājānaṃ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥc abhyadhāvat punar bhīmaṃ śaravarṣair avākirata tasya tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathaiva ca kṛtāstratāmc apūjayann anīkāni pareṣāṃ parākrāntāḥ saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ gatāḥa yathābhāgaṃ yathotsāhaṃ bhavantaḥ kṛtapauruṣāḥc bhāgo vaśiṣṭa eko yaṃ mama śalyo mahārathaḥa so ham adya yudhā jetum āśaṃse madrakeśvaramc tatra yan mānasaṃ mahyaṃ
