pārthivāḥc svayaṃ samabhisaṃdhāya vijayāyetarāya vāa tasya me bhyadhikaṃ śastraṃ sarvopakaraṇāni cac saṃyuñjantu raṇe kṣipraṃ śāstravad rathayojakāḥa śaineyo dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathottaramc pṛṣṭhagopo bhavatv adya mama pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥa puraḥsaro mamādyāstu bhīmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc evam abhyadhikaḥ śalyād bhaviṣyāmi mahāmṛdhea evam uktās tathā cakruḥ sarve rājñaḥ priyaiṣiṇaḥc tataḥ praharṣaḥ sainyānāṃ punar āsīt tadā nṛpaa pāñcālānāṃ somakānāṃ matsyānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥc pratijñāṃ tāṃ ca saṃgrāme dharmarājasya pūrayand pratijñāṃ tāṃ tadā rājā kṛtvā madreśam abhyayāta tataḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca śataśaś caiva puṣkarānc avādayanta pāñcālāḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca nedirea te bhyadhāvanta saṃrabdhā madrarājaṃ tarasvinaḥc mahatā harṣajenātha nādena kurupuṃgavāḥa hrādena gajaghaṇṭānāṃ śaṅkhānāṃ ninadena cac tūryaśabdena mahatā nādayantaś ca medinīma tān pratyagṛhṇāt putras te madrarājaś ca vīryavānc mahāmeghān iva bahūñ śailāv astodayāv ubhaua śalyas tu samaraślāghī dharmarājam ariṃdamamc vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa varṣeṇa maghavān ivaa tathaiva kururājo pi pragṛhya ruciraṃ dhanuḥc droṇopadeśān vividhān darśayāno mahāmanāḥd saṃdadhe vividhān bāṇān darśayan hastalāghavama vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi citraṃ laghu ca suṣṭhu cac na cāsya vivaraṃ kaś cid dadarśa carato raṇea tāv ubhau vividhair bāṇais tatakṣāte parasparamc śārdūlāv āmiṣaprepsū parākrāntāv ivāhavea bhīmas tu tava putreṇa raṇaśauṇḍena saṃgataḥc pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiś caiva mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaue śakunipramukhān vīrān pratyagṛhṇan samantataḥa tadāsīt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ punar eva jayaiṣiṇāmc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca rājan durmantrite tavaa duryodhanas tu bhīmasya śareṇānataparvaṇāc cicchedādiśya saṃgrāme dhvajaṃ hemavibhūṣitama sakiṅkiṇīkajālena mahatā cārudarśanaḥc papāta ruciraḥ siṃho bhīmasenasya nānadana punaś cāsya dhanuś citraṃ gajarājakaropamamc kṣureṇa śitadhāreṇa pracakarta narādhipaḥa sa cchinnadhanvā tejasvī rathaśaktyā sutaṃ tavac bibhedorasi vikramya sa rathopastha āviśata tasmin moham anuprāpte punar eva vṛkodaraḥc yantur eva śiraḥ kāyāt kṣurapreṇāharat tadāa hatasūtā hayās tasya ratham ādāya bhāratac vyadravanta diśo rājan hāhākāras tadābhavata tam abhyadhāvat trāṇārthaṃ droṇaputro mahārathaḥc kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca putraṃ te bhiparīpsavaḥa tasmin vilulite sainye trastās tasya padānugāḥc gāṇḍīvadhanvā visphārya dhanus tān ahanac charaiḥa yudhiṣṭhiras tu madreśam abhyadhāvad amarṣitaḥc svayaṃ saṃcodayann aśvān dantavarṇān manojavāna tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kuntīputre yudhiṣṭhirec purā bhūtvā mṛdur dānto yat tadā dāruṇo bhavata vivṛtākṣaś ca kaunteyo vepamānaś ca manyunāc ciccheda yodhān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śatasahasraśaḥa yāṃ yāṃ pratyudyayau senāṃ tāṃ tāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ sa pāṇḍavaḥc śarair apātayad rājan girīn vajrair ivottamaiḥa sāśvasūtadhvajarathān rathinaḥ pātayan bahūnc ākrīḍad eko balavān pavanas toyadān ivaa sāśvārohāṃś ca turagān pattīṃś caiva sahasraśaḥc vyapothayata saṃgrāme kruddho rudraḥ paśūn ivaa śūnyam āyodhanaṃ kṛtvā śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥc abhyadravata madreśaṃ tiṣṭha śalyeti cābravīta tasya tac caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme bhīmakarmaṇaḥc vitresus tāvakāḥ sarve śalyas tv enaṃ samabhyayāta tatas tau tu susaṃrabdhau pradhmāpya salilodbhavauc samāhūya tadānyonyaṃ bhartsayantau samīyatuḥa śalyas tu śaravarṣeṇa yudhiṣṭhiram avākiratc madrarājaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ śaravarṣair avākirata vyadṛśyetāṃ tadā rājan kaṅkapatribhir āhavec udbhinnarudhirau śūrau madrarājayudhiṣṭhiraua puṣpitāv iva rejāte vane śalmalikiṃśukāb puṣpitau śuśubhāte tau vasante kiṃśukau yathāc dīpyamānau mahātmānau prāṇayor yuddhadurmadaua dṛṣṭvā sarvāṇi sainyāni nādhyavasyaṃs tayor jayamc hatvā madrādhipaṃ pārtho bhokṣyate dya vasuṃdharāma śalyo vā pāṇḍavaṃ hatvā dadyād duryodhanāya gāmc itīva niścayo nābhūd yodhānāṃ tatra bhārataa pradakṣiṇam abhūt sarvaṃ dharmarājasya yudhyataḥa tataḥ śaraśataṃ śalyo mumocāśu yudhiṣṭhirec dhanuś cāsya śitāgreṇa bāṇena nirakṛntataa so nyat kārmukam ādāya śalyaṃ śaraśatais tribhiḥc avidhyat kārmukaṃ cāsya kṣureṇa nirakṛntataa athāsya nijaghānāśvāṃś caturo nataparvabhiḥc dvābhyām atha śitāgrābhyām ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathīa tato sya dīpyamānena pītena niśitena cac pramukhe vartamānasya bhallenāpāharad dhvajame tataḥ prabhagnaṃ tat sainyaṃ dauryodhanam ariṃdamaa tato madrādhipaṃ drauṇir abhyadhāvat tathākṛtamc āropya cainaṃ svarathaṃ tvaramāṇaḥ pradudruvea muhūrtam iva tau gatvā nardamāne yudhiṣṭhirec sthitvā tato madrapatir rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥc pratyudgata iva premṇā bhūmyā sa narapuṃgavaḥa priyayā kāntayā kāntaḥ patamāna ivorasic ciraṃ bhuktvā vasumatīṃ priyāṃ kāntām iva prabhuḥe sarvair aṅgaiḥ samāśliṣya prasupta iva so bhavata dharmye dharmātmanā yuddhe nihato dharmasūnunāc samyag ghuta iva sviṣṭaḥ praśānto gnir ivādhvarea śaktyā vibhinnahṛdayaṃ vipraviddhāyudhadhvajamc saṃśāntam api madreśaṃ lakṣmīr naiva vyamuñcataa tato yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpam ādāyendradhanuṣprabhamc vyadhamad dviṣataḥ saṃkhye khagarāḍ iva pannagāne dehāsūn niśitair bhallai ripūṇāṃ nāśayan kṣaṇāta tataḥ pārthasya bāṇaughair āvṛtāḥ sainikās tavac nimīlitākṣāḥ kṣiṇvanto bhṛśam anyonyam arditāḥe saṃnyastakavacā dehair vipatrāyudhajīvitāḥa tataḥ śalye nipatite madrarājānujo yuvāc bhrātuḥ sarvair guṇais tulyo rathī pāṇḍavam abhyayāta vivyādha ca naraśreṣṭho nārācair bahubhis tvaranc hatasyāpacitiṃ bhrātuś cikīrṣur yuddhadurmadaḥa taṃ vivyādhāśugaiḥ ṣaḍbhir dharmarājas tvarann ivac kārmukaṃ cāsya ciccheda kṣurābhyāṃ dhvajam eva caa tato sya dīpyamānena sudṛḍhena śitena cac pramukhe vartamānasya bhallenāpāharac chiraḥd śiraś ciccheda bāṇena bhallena nataparvaṇāa sakuṇḍalaṃ tad dadṛśe patamānaṃ śiro rathātc puṇyakṣayam iva prāpya patantaṃ svargavāsinama tasyāpakṛṣṭaśīrṣaṃ tac charīraṃ patitaṃ rathātc rudhireṇāvasiktāṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā sainyam abhajyataa vicitrakavace tasmin hate madranṛpānujec hāhākāraṃ vikurvāṇāḥ kuravo vipradudruvuḥa śalyānujaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tāvakās tyaktajīvitāḥc vitresuḥ pāṇḍavabhayād rajodhvastās tathā bhṛśama tāṃs tathā bhajyatas trastān kauravān bharatarṣabhab tat sainyaṃ tava putrasya vidrutaṃ sarvato bhayātc śiner naptā kiran bāṇair abhyavartata sātyakiḥa tam āyāntaṃ maheṣvāsam aprasahyaṃ durāsadamc hārdikyas tvarito rājan pratyagṛhṇād abhītavata tau sametau mahātmānau vārṣṇeyāv aparājitauc hārdikyaḥ sātyakiś caiva siṃhāv iva madotkaṭaua iṣubhir vimalābhāsaiś chādayantau parasparamc arcirbhir iva sūryasya divākarasamaprabhaua cāpamārgabaloddhūtān mārgaṇān vṛṣṇisiṃhayoḥc ākāśe samapaśyāma pataṃgān iva śīghragāna sātyakiṃ daśabhir viddhvā hayāṃś cāsya tribhiḥ śaraiḥc cāpam ekena ciccheda hārdikyo nataparvaṇāa tan nikṛttaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham apāsya śinipuṃgavaḥc anyad ādatta vegena vegavattaram āyudhama tad ādāya dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanvināmc hārdikyaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntarea tato rathaṃ yugeṣāṃ ca chittvā bhallaiḥ susaṃyataiḥc aśvāṃs tasyāvadhīt tūrṇam ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathīd hārdikyaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ prabhod apovāha tataḥ kṣipraṃ ratham āropya vīryavāna madrarāje hate rājan virathe kṛtavarmaṇic duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukhama tatpare nāvabudhyanta sainyena rajasā vṛtec balaṃ tu hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ tat tadāsīt parāṅmukhama tato muhūrtāt te paśyan rajo bhaumaṃ samutthitamc vividhaiḥ śoṇitasrāvaiḥ praśāntaṃ puruṣarṣabhad vividhān saritaś coghāñ śoṇitasya viśāṃ patea tato duryodhano dṛṣṭvā bhagnaṃ svabalam antikātc javenāpatataḥ pārthān ekaḥ sarvān avārayata pāṇḍavān sarathān dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatamc ānartaṃ ca durādharṣaṃ śitair bāṇair avākirata taṃ pare nābhyavartanta martyā mṛtyum ivāgatamc athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya hārdikyo pi nyavartatad pragṛhya ca dhanur ghoram abhyadhāvad yudhiṣṭhirama tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥc caturbhir nijaghānāśvān patribhiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥe vivyādha gautamaṃ cāpi ṣaḍbhir bhallaiḥ sutejanaiḥa aśvatthāmā tato rājñā hatāśvaṃ virathīkṛtamc samapovāha hārdikyaṃ svarathena yudhiṣṭhirāta tataḥ śāradvato ṣṭābhiḥ pratyavidhyad yudhiṣṭhiramc vivyādha cāśvān niśitais tasyāṣṭābhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥa evam etan mahārāja yuddhaśeṣam avartatac tava durmantrite rājan sahaputrasya bhārataa tasmin maheṣvāsavare viśastesaṃgrāmamadhye kurupuṃgavenac pārthāḥ sametāḥ paramaprahṛṣṭāḥśaṅkhān pradadhmur hatam īkṣya śalyama yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca praśaśaṃsur ājaupurā surā vṛtravadhe yathendramc cakruś ca nānāvidhavādyaśabdānninādayanto vasudhāṃ samantāt saṃjaya uvācaa śalye tu nihate rājan madrarājapadānugāḥc rathāḥ saptaśatā vīrā niryayur mahato balāta duryodhanas tu dviradam āruhyācalasaṃnibhamc chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena vījyamānaś ca cāmaraiḥe na gantavyaṃ na gantavyam iti madrān avārayata duryodhanena te vīrā vāryamāṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jighāṃsantaḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ prāviśan balama te tu śūrā mahārāja kṛtacittāḥ sma yodhanec dhanuḥśabdaṃ mahat kṛtvā sahāyudhyanta pāṇḍavaiḥa śrutvā tu nihataṃ śalyaṃ dharmaputraṃ ca pīḍitamc madrarājapriye yuktair madrakāṇāṃ mahārathaiḥa ājagāma tataḥ pārtho gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥc pūrayan rathaghoṣeṇa diśaḥ sarvā mahārathaḥa tato rjunaś ca bhīmaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc sātyakiś ca naravyāghro draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ parīpsantaḥ samantāt paryavārayana te samantāt parivṛtāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥc kṣobhayanti sma tāṃ senāṃ makarāḥ sāgaraṃ yathāa purovātena gaṅgeva kṣobhyamānā mahānadīc akṣobhyata tadā rājan pāṇḍūnāṃ dhvajinī punaḥa praskandya senāṃ mahatīṃ tyaktātmāno mahārathāḥc vṛkṣān iva mahāvātāḥ kampayanti sma tāvakāḥa bahavaś cukruśus tatra kva sa rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhrātaro vāsya te śūrā dṛśyante neha ke canaa pāñcālānāṃ mahāvīryāḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumno tha śaineyo draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥa evaṃ tān vādinaḥ śūrān draupadeyā mahārathāḥc abhyaghnan yuyudhānaś ca madrarājapadānugāna cakrair vimathitaiḥ ke cit ke cic chinnair mahādhvajaiḥc pratyadṛśyanta samare tāvakā nihatāḥ paraiḥa ālokya pāṇḍavān yuddhe yodhā rājan samantataḥc vāryamāṇā yayur vegāt tava putreṇa bhārataa duryodhanas tu tān vīrān vārayām āsa sāntvayanc na cāsya śāsanaṃ kaś cit tatra cakre mahārathaḥa tato gāndhārarājasya putraḥ śakunir abravītc duryodhanaṃ mahārāja vacanaṃ vacanakṣamaḥa kiṃ naḥ saṃprekṣamāṇānāṃ madrāṇāṃ hanyate balamc na yuktam etat samare tvayi tiṣṭhati bhārataa sahitair nāma yoddhavyam ity eṣa samayaḥ kṛtaḥc atha kasmāt parān eva ghnato marṣayase nṛpa duryodhana uvācaa vāryamāṇā mayā pūrvaṃ naite cakrur vaco mamac ete hi nihatāḥ sarve praskannāḥ pāṇḍuvāhinīm śakunir uvāca vāryamāṇo sicmayā pūrvaṃ na kṛtaṃ vacanaṃ tvayāa na bhartuḥ śāsanaṃ vīrā raṇe kurvanty amarṣitāḥc alaṃ kroddhuṃ tathaiteṣāṃ nāyaṃ kāla upekṣituma yāmaḥ sarve tra saṃbhūya savājirathakuñjarāḥc paritrātuṃ maheṣvāsān madrarājapadānugāna anyonyaṃ parirakṣāmo yatnena mahatā nṛpac evaṃ sarve nusaṃcintya prayayur yatra sainikāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa evam uktas tato rājā balena mahatā vṛtaḥc prayayau siṃhanādena kampayan vai vasuṃdharāma hata vidhyata gṛhṇīta praharadhvaṃ nikṛntatac ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdas tava sainyasya bhārataa pāṇḍavās tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā madrarājapadānugānb paśyatāṃ tava putrāṇāṃ pāṇḍuputrair asaṃbhramamc sahitān abhyavartanta gulmam āsthāya madhyamama te muhūrtād raṇe vīrā hastāhastaṃ viśāṃ patec nihatāḥ pratyadṛśyanta madrarājapadānugāḥa tato naḥ saṃprayātānāṃ hatāmitrās tarasvinaḥc hṛṣṭāḥ kilakilāśabdam akurvan sahitāḥ parea athotthitāni ruṇḍāni samadṛśyanta sarvaśaḥc papāta mahatī colkā madhyenādityamaṇḍalama rathair bhagnair yugākṣaiś ca nihataiś ca mahārathaiḥc aśvair nipatitaiś caiva saṃchannābhūd vasuṃdharāa vātāyamānais turagair yugāsaktais turaṃgamaiḥc adṛśyanta mahārāja yodhās tatra raṇājirea bhagnacakrān rathān ke cid avahaṃs turagā raṇec rathārdhaṃ ke cid ādāya diśo daśa vibabhramuḥe tatra tatra ca dṛśyante yoktraiḥ śliṣṭāḥ sma vājinaḥa rathinaḥ patamānāś ca vyadṛśyanta narottamac gaganāt pracyutāḥ siddhāḥ puṇyānām iva saṃkṣayea nihateṣu ca śūreṣu madrarājānugeṣu cac asmān āpatataś cāpi dṛṣṭvā pārthā mahārathāḥa abhyavartanta vegena jayagṛdhrāḥ prahāriṇaḥc bāṇaśabdaravān kṛtvā vimiśrāñ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥa asmāṃs tu punar āsādya labdhalakṣāḥ prahāriṇaḥc śarāsanāni dhunvānāḥ siṃhanādān pracukruśuḥa tato hatam abhiprekṣya madrarājabalaṃ mahatc madrarājaṃ ca samare dṛṣṭvā śūraṃ nipātitame duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukhama vadhyamānaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥc diśo bheje tha saṃbhrāntaṃ trāsitaṃ dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥ saṃjaya uvācaa pātite yudhi durdharṣe madrarāje mahārathec tāvakās tava putrāś ca prāyaśo vimukhābhavana vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyāṃ yathāgādhe plave rṇavec apāre pāram icchanto hate śūre mahātmania madrarāje mahārāja vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥc anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā ivaa vṛṣā yathā bhagnaśṛṅgāḥ śīrṇadantā gajā ivac madhyāhne pratyapāyāma nirjitā dharmasūnunāa na saṃdhātum anīkāni na ca rājan parākramec āsīd buddhir hate śalye tava yodhasya kasya cita bhīṣme droṇe ca nihate sūtaputre ca bhāratac yad duḥkhaṃ tava yodhānāṃ bhayaṃ cāsīd viśāṃ patee tad bhayaṃ sa ca naḥ śoko bhūya evābhyavartataa nirāśāś ca jaye tasmin hate śalye mahāratheb nirāśaś ca hate śalye rājā rājan mahāyaśāḥc hatapravīrā vidhvastā vikṛttāś ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥe madrarāje hate rājan yodhās te prādravan bhayāta aśvān anye gajān anye rathān anye mahārathāḥc āruhya javasaṃpannāḥ pādātāḥ prādravan bhayāta dvisāhasrāś ca mātaṅgā girirūpāḥ prahāriṇaḥc saṃprādravan hate śalye aṅkuśāṅguṣṭhacoditāḥa te raṇād bharataśreṣṭha tāvakāḥ prādravan diśaḥc dhāvantaś cāpy adṛśyanta śvasamānāḥ śarāturāḥa tān prabhagnān drutān dṛṣṭvā hatotsāhān parājitānc abhyadravanta pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāś ca jayaiṣiṇaḥa bāṇaśabdaravaś cāpi siṃhanādaś ca puṣkalaḥc śaṅkhaśabdaś ca śūrāṇāṃ dāruṇaḥ samapadyataa dṛṣṭvā tu kauravaṃ sainyaṃ bhayatrastaṃ pravidrutamc anyonyaṃ samabhāṣanta pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahaa adya rājā satyadhṛtir jitāmitro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc adya duryodhano hīno dīptayā nṛpatiśriyād adya diṣṭyā kṣmāśayanaṃ niratāmāmucakṣuṣaḥ sicd draupadyā yaś ca saṃkalpaḥ saṃsiddha iti ghuṣyatāma adya śrutvā hataṃ putraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥc niḥsaṃjñaḥ patito bhūmau kilbiṣaṃ pratipadyatāma adya jānātu kaunteyaṃ samarthaṃ sarvadhanvināmc adyātmānaṃ ca durmedhā garhayiṣyati pāpakṛte adya kṣattur vacaḥ satyaṃ smaratāṃ bruvato hitama adyaprabhṛti pārthāṃś ca preṣyabhūta upācaranb adyaiva ca hi pārthānāṃ yat kṛtaṃ pūrvakarmabhiḥc vijānātu nṛpo duḥkhaṃ yat prāptaṃ pāṇḍunandanaiḥa adya kṛṣṇasya māhātmyaṃ jānātu sa mahīpatiḥc adyārjunadhanurghoṣaṃ ghoraṃ jānātu saṃyuged putrāṇāṃ ca vadhaṃ ghoraṃ bhīmena śroṣyate nṛpaḥa astrāṇāṃ ca balaṃ sarvaṃ bāhvoś ca balam āhavec adya jñāsyati bhīmasya balaṃ ghoraṃ mahātmanaḥa hate duryodhane yuddhe śakreṇevāsure mayec yat kṛtaṃ bhīmasenena duḥśāsanavadhe tadāe nānyaḥ kartāsti loke tad ṛte bhīmaṃ mahābalama jānītām adya jyeṣṭhasya pāṇḍavasya parākramamc madrarājaṃ hataṃ śrutvā devair api suduḥsahama adya jñāsyati saṃgrāme mādrīputrau mahābalauc nihate saubale śūre gāndhāreṣu ca sarvaśaḥa kathaṃ teṣāṃ jayo na syād yeṣāṃ yoddhā dhanaṃjayaḥc sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa draupadyās tanayāḥ pañca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc śikhaṇḍī ca maheṣvāso rājā caiva yudhiṣṭhiraḥa yeṣāṃ ca jagatāṃ nātho nāthaḥ kṛṣṇo janārdanaḥc kathaṃ teṣāṃ jayo na syād yeṣāṃ dharmo vyapāśrayaḥd lābhas teṣāṃ jayas teṣāṃ kutas teṣāṃ parābhavaḥd yeṣāṃ nātho hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvalokavibhur hariḥa bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca madrarājānam eva cac tathānyān nṛpatīn vīrāñ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa ko nyaḥ śakto raṇe jetum ṛte pārthaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc yasya nātho hṛṣīkeśaḥ sadā dharmayaśonidhiḥa ity evaṃ vadamānās te harṣeṇa mahatā yutāḥc prabhagnāṃs tāvakān rājan sṛñjayāḥ pṛṣṭhato nvayuḥa dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavānc mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥa tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditānc duryodhanas tadā sūtam abravīd utsmayann ivaa na mātikramate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitamc jaghane sarvasainyānāṃ mamāśvān pratipādayaa jaghane yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc notsahetābhyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahodadhiḥa paśya sainyaṃ mahat sūta pāṇḍavaiḥ samabhidrutamc sainyareṇuṃ samuddhūtaṃ paśyasvainaṃ samantataḥa siṃhanādāṃś ca bahuśaḥ śṛṇu ghorān bhayānakānc tasmād yāhi śanaiḥ sūta jaghanaṃ paripālayaa mayi sthite ca samare niruddheṣu ca pāṇḍuṣuc punarāvartate tūrṇaṃ māmakaṃ balam ojasāa tac chrutvā tava putrasya śūrāgryasadṛśaṃ vacaḥc sārathir hemasaṃchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayata gajāśvarathibhir hīnās tyaktātmānaḥ padātayaḥc ekaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ saṃyugāyāvatasthirea nānādeśasamudbhūtā nānārañjitavāsasaḥc avasthitās tadā yodhāḥ prārthayanto mahad yaśaḥa teṣām āpatatāṃ tatra saṃhṛṣṭānāṃ parasparamc saṃmardaḥ sumahāñ jajñe ghorarūpo bhayānakaḥa bhīmasenaṃ tadā rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatamc balena caturaṅgeṇa nānādeśyā nyavārayana bhīmam evābhyavartanta raṇe nye tu padātayaḥc prakṣveḍyāsphoṭya saṃhṛṣṭā vīralokaṃ yiyāsavaḥa āsādya bhīmasenaṃ tu saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥc dhārtarāṣṭrā vinedur hi nānyāṃ cākathayan kathāmd nigṛhītuṃ tadā kruddhāḥ samantāt paryavārayane parivārya raṇe bhīmaṃ nijaghnus te samantataḥa sa vadhyamānaḥ samare padātigaṇasaṃvṛtaḥc na cacāla rathopasthe maināka iva parvataḥa te tu kruddhā mahārāja pāṇḍavasya mahārathamc nigrahītuṃ pracakrur hi yodhāṃś cānyān avārayana akrudhyata raṇe bhīmas tais tadā paryavasthitaiḥc so vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ padātiḥ samavasthitaḥa jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmc avadhīt tāvakān yodhān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥa rathāśvadvipahīnāṃs tu tān bhīmo gadayā balīb viprahīnarathāśvāṃs tān narān sa puruṣarṣabhaḥb bhīmaseno gadāpāṇir gadayā vajrakalpayāc ekaviṃśatisāhasrān padātīn avapothayata hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya nacirāt pratyadṛśyataa pādātā nihatā bhūmau śiśyire rudhirokṣitāḥc saṃbhagnā iva vātena karṇikārāḥ supuṣpitāḥa nānāpuṣpasrajopetā nānākuṇḍaladhāriṇaḥc nānājātyā hatās tatra nānādeśasamāgatāḥa patākādhvajasaṃchannaṃ padātīnāṃ mahad balamc nikṛttaṃ vibabhau tatra ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakama yudhiṣṭhirapurogās tu sarvasainyamahārathāḥc abhyadhāvan mahātmānaṃ putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tavaa te sarve tāvakān dṛṣṭvā maheṣvāsān parāṅmukhānb samabhyadhāvaṃs tvaritā yuddhāya jitakāśinaḥc nābhyavartanta te putraṃ veleva makarālayama tad adbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣamc yad ekaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā na śekur ativartituma nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyanec duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam abravīd bhṛśavikṣatama na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu vāc yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥa alpaṃ ca balam eteṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣatauc yadi sarve tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhaveta viprayātāṃs tu vo bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣānc anusṛtya haniṣyanti śreyo naḥ samare sthitama śṛṇudhvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥc yadā śūraṃ ca bhīruṃ ca mārayaty antakaḥ sadāe ko nu mūḍho na yudhyeta puruṣaḥ kṣatriyabruvaḥa śreyo no bhīmasenasya kruddhasya pramukhe sthitamc sukhaḥ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyatāmd martyenāvaśyamartavyaṃ gṛheṣv api kadā canad yudhyataḥ kṣatradharmeṇa mṛtyur eṣa sanātanaḥe jitveha sukham āpnoti hataḥ pretya mahat phalama na yuddhadharmāc chreyān vai panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥc acireṇa jitāṃl lokān hato yuddhe samaśnutea śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya pūjayitvā ca pārthivāḥc punar evānvavartanta pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥa tān āpatata evāśu vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥc pratyudyayus tadā pārthā jayagṛdhrāḥ prahāriṇaḥa dhanaṃjayo rathenājāv abhyavartata vīryavānc viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥa mādrīputrau ca śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahābalaḥc javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā yato vai tāvakaṃ balam saṃjaya uvācaa saṃnivṛtte balaughe tu śālvo mlecchagaṇādhipaḥc abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍūnāṃ sumahad balama āsthāya sumahānāgaṃ prabhinnaṃ parvatopamamc dṛptam airāvataprakhyam amitragaṇamardanama yo sau mahābhadrakulaprasūtaḥsupūjito dhārtarāṣṭreṇa nityamc sukalpitaḥ śāstraviniścayajñaiḥsadopavāhyaḥ samareṣu rājand airāvataṃ daityagaṇān vimṛdnañd śakro yathā saṃjanayan bhayānia tam āsthito rājavaro babhūvayathodayasthaḥ savitā kṣapāntec sa tena nāgapravareṇa rājannabhyudyayau pāṇḍusutān samantāte śitaiḥ pṛṣatkair vidadāra cāpimahendravajrapratimaiḥ sughoraiḥa tataḥ śarān vai sṛjato mahāraṇeyodhāṃś ca rājan nayato yamāyab tataḥ śarān vai sṛjatā nṛpeṇab yodhāḥ samastā gamitā yamālayamc nāsyāntaraṃ dadṛśuḥ sve pare vāyathā purā vajradharasya daityāḥd airāvaṇasthasya camūvimarded daityāḥ purā vāsavasyeva rājana te pāṇḍavāḥ somakāḥ sṛñjayāś catam eva nāgaṃ dadṛśuḥ samantātc sahasraśo vai vicarantam ekaṃyathā mahendrasya gajaṃ samīpea saṃdrāvyamāṇaṃ tu balaṃ pareṣāṃparītakalpaṃ vibabhau samantātc naivāvatasthe samare bhṛśaṃ bhayādvimardamānaṃ tu parasparaṃ tadāa tataḥ prabhagnā sahasā mahācamūḥsā pāṇḍavī tena narādhipenac diśaś catasraḥ sahasā pradhāvitāgajendravegaṃ tam apārayantīa dṛṣṭvā ca tāṃ vegavatā prabhagnāṃsarve tvadīyā yudhi yodhamukhyāḥc apūjayaṃs tatra narādhipaṃ taṃdadhmuś ca śaṅkhāñ śaśisaṃnikāśāna śrutvā ninādaṃ tv atha kauravāṇāṃharṣād vimuktaṃ saha śaṅkhaśabdaiḥc senāpatiḥ pāṇḍavasṛñjayānāṃpāñcālaputro na mamarṣa roṣāta tatas tu taṃ vai dviradaṃ mahātmāpratyudyayau tvaramāṇo jayāyac jambho yathā śakrasamāgame vaināgendram airāvaṇam indravāhyama tam āpatantaṃ sahasā tu dṛṣṭvāpāñcālarājaṃ yudhi rājasiṃhaḥc taṃ vai dvipaṃ preṣayām āsa tūrṇaṃvadhāya rājan drupadātmajasyaa sa taṃ dvipaṃ sahasābhyāpatantamavidhyad arkapratimaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥc karmāradhautair niśitair jvaladbhirnārācamukhyais tribhir ugravegaiḥa tato parān pañca śitān mahātmānārācamukhyān visasarja kumbhec sa tais tu viddhaḥ paramadvipo raṇetadā parāvṛtya bhṛśaṃ pradudruvea taṃ nāgarājaṃ sahasā praṇunnaṃvidrāvyamāṇaṃ ca nigṛhya śālvaḥc tottrāṅkuśaiḥ preṣayām āsa tūrṇaṃpāñcālarājasya rathaṃ pradiśyaa dṛṣṭvāpatantaṃ sahasā tu nāgaṃdhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ svarathāc chīghram evac gadāṃ pragṛhyāśu javena vīrobhūmiṃ prapanno bhayavihvalāṅgaḥa sa taṃ rathaṃ hemavibhūṣitāṅgaṃsāśvaṃ sasūtaṃ sahasā vimṛdyac utkṣipya hastena tadā mahādvipovipothayām āsa vasuṃdharātalea pāñcālarājasya sutaṃ sa dṛṣṭvātadārditaṃ nāgavareṇa tenac tam abhyadhāvat sahasā javenabhīmaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca śineś ca naptāa śaraiś ca vegaṃ sahasā nigṛhyatasyābhito bhyāpatato gajasyac sa saṃgṛhīto rathibhir gajo vaicacāla tair vāryamāṇaś ca saṃkhyea tataḥ pṛṣatkān pravavarṣa rājāsūryo yathā raśmijālaṃ samantātc tenāśugair vadhyamānā rathaughāḥpradudruvus tatra tatas tu sarvea tat karma śālvasya samīkṣya sarvepāñcālamatsyā nṛpa sṛñjayāś cac hāhākārair nādayantaḥ sma yuddhedvipaṃ samantād rurudhur narāgryāḥa pāñcālarājas tvaritas tu śūrogadāṃ pragṛhyācalaśṛṅgakalpāmc asaṃbhramaṃ bhārata śatrughātījavena vīro nusasāra nāgama tato tha nāgaṃ dharaṇīdharābhaṃmadaṃ sravantaṃ jaladaprakāśamc gadāṃ samāvidhya bhṛśaṃ jaghānapāñcālarājasya sutas tarasvīa sa bhinnakumbhaḥ sahasā vinadyamukhāt prabhūtaṃ kṣatajaṃ vimuñcanc papāta nāgo dharaṇīdharābhaḥkṣitiprakampāc calito yathādriḥa nipātyamāne tu tadā gajendrehāhākṛte tava putrasya sainyec sa śālvarājasya śinipravīrojahāra bhallena śiraḥ śitenaa hṛtottamāṅgo yudhi sātvatenapapāta bhūmau saha nāgarājñāc yathādriśṛṅgaṃ sumahat praṇunnaṃvajreṇa devādhipacoditena saṃjaya uvācaa tasmiṃs tu nihate śūre śālve samitiśobhanec tavābhajyad balaṃ vegād vāteneva mahādrumaḥa tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥc dadhāra samare śūraḥ śatrusainyaṃ mahābalaḥa saṃnivṛttās tu te śūrā dṛṣṭvā sātvatam āhavec śailopamaṃ sthitaṃ rājan kīryamāṇaṃ śarair yudhia tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac nivṛttānāṃ mahārāja mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama tatrāścaryam abhūd yuddhaṃ sātvatasya paraiḥ sahac yad eko vārayām āsa pāṇḍusenāṃ durāsadāma teṣām anyonyasuhṛdāṃ kṛte karmaṇi duṣkarec siṃhanādaḥ prahṛṣṭānāṃ divaḥspṛk sumahān abhūta tena śabdena vitrastān pāñcālān bharatarṣabhac śiner naptā mahābāhur anvapadyata sātyakiḥd śatavarmāṇam atyugraṃ mahāvīraṃ mahābalama sa samāsādya rājānaṃ kṣemadhūrtiṃ mahābalamc saptabhir niśitair bāṇair anayad yamasādanama tam āyāntaṃ mahābāhuṃ pravapantaṃ śitāñ śarānc javenābhyapatad dhīmān hārdikyaḥ śinipuṃgavama tau siṃhāv iva nardantau dhanvinau rathināṃ varauc anyonyam abhyadhāvetāṃ śastrapravaradhāriṇaua pāṇḍavāḥ saha pāñcālair yodhāś cānye nṛpottamāḥc prekṣakāḥ samapadyanta tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥa nārācair vatsadantaiś ca vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathauc abhijaghnatur anyonyaṃ prahṛṣṭāv iva kuñjaraua carantau vividhān mārgān hārdikyaśinipuṃgavauc muhur antardadhāte tau bāṇavṛṣṭyā parasparama cāpavegabaloddhūtān mārgaṇān vṛṣṇisiṃhayoḥc ākāśe samapaśyāma pataṃgān iva śīghragāna tam ekaṃ satyakarmāṇam āsādya hṛdikātmajaḥc avidhyan niśitair bāṇaiś caturbhiś caturo hayāna sa dīrghabāhuḥ saṃkruddhas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥc aṣṭābhiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam avidhyat parameṣubhiḥa tataḥ pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭaiḥ kṛtavarmā śilāśitaiḥc sātyakiṃ tribhir āhatya dhanur ekena cicchidea nikṛttaṃ tad dhanuḥśreṣṭham apāsya śinipuṃgavaḥc anyad ādatta vegena śaineyaḥ saśaraṃ dhanuḥa tad ādāya dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanvināmc āropya ca mahāvīryo mahābuddhir mahābalaḥa amṛṣyamāṇo dhanuṣaś chedanaṃ kṛtavarmaṇāc kupito tirathaḥ śīghraṃ kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāta tataḥ suniśitair bāṇair daśabhiḥ śinipuṃgavaḥc jaghāna sūtam aśvāṃś ca dhvajaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇaḥa tato rājan maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥc hatāśvasūtaṃ saṃprekṣya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtama roṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ śūlam udyamya māriṣac cikṣepa bhujavegena jighāṃsuḥ śinipuṃgavama tac chūlaṃ sātvato hy ājau nirbhidya niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc cūrṇitaṃ pātayām āsa mohayann iva mādhavame tato pareṇa bhallena hṛdy enaṃ samatāḍayata sa yuddhe yuyudhānena hatāśvo hatasārathiḥc kṛtavarmā kṛtāstreṇa dharaṇīm anvapadyataa tasmin sātyakinā vīre dvairathe virathīkṛtec samapadyata sarveṣāṃ sainyānāṃ sumahad bhayama putrasya tava cātyarthaṃ viṣādaḥ samapadyatac hatasūte hatāśve ca virathe kṛtavarmaṇia hatāśvaṃ ca samālakṣya hatasūtam ariṃdamamc abhyadhāvat kṛpo rājañ jighāṃsuḥ śinipuṃgavama tam āropya rathopasthe miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvināmc apovāha mahābāhus tūrṇam āyodhanād apia śaineye dhiṣṭhite rājan virathe kṛtavarmaṇic duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukhama tatpare nāvabudhyanta sainyena rajasāvṛtec tāvakāḥ pradrutā rājan duryodhanam ṛte nṛpama duryodhanas tu saṃprekṣya bhagnaṃ svabalam antikātc javenābhyapatat tūrṇaṃ sarvāṃś caiko nyavārayata pāṇḍūṃś ca sarvān saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatamc śikhaṇḍinaṃ draupadeyān pāñcālānāṃ ca ye gaṇāḥa kekayān somakāṃś caiva pāñcālāṃś caiva māriṣac asaṃbhramaṃ durādharṣaḥ śitair astrair avārayata atiṣṭhad āhave yattaḥ putras tava mahābalaḥc yathā yajñe mahān agnir mantrapūtaḥ prakāśayand tathā duryodhano rājā saṃgrāme sarvato bhavata taṃ pare nābhyavartanta martyā mṛtyum ivāhavec athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya hārdikyaḥ samapadyata saṃjaya uvācaa putras tu te mahārāja rathastho rathināṃ varaḥb durdharaḥ sa pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavān prati bhāratac durutsaho babhau yuddhe yathā rudraḥ pratāpavāna tasya bāṇasahasrais tu pracchannā hy abhavan mahīc parāṃś ca siṣice bāṇair dhārābhir iva parvatāna na ca so sti pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāhavec hayo gajo ratho vāpi yo sya bāṇair avikṣataḥa yaṃ yaṃ hi samare yodhaṃ prapaśyāmi viśāṃ patec sa sa bāṇaiś cito bhūd vai putreṇa tava bhārataa yathā sainyena rajasā samuddhūtena vāhinīc pratyadṛśyata saṃchannā tathā bāṇair mahātmanaḥa bāṇabhūtām apaśyāma pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpatec duryodhanena prakṛtāṃ kṣiprahastena dhanvināa teṣu yodhasahasreṣu tāvakeṣu pareṣu cac eko duryodhano hy āsīt pumān iti matir mamaa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya vikramamc yad ekaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā nātyavartanta bhārataa yudhiṣṭhiraṃ śatenājau vivyādha bharatarṣabhac bhīmasenaṃ ca saptatyā sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥa nakulaṃ ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc saptabhir draupadeyāṃś ca tribhir vivyādha sātyakime dhanuś ciccheda bhallena sahadevasya māriṣaa tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ mādrīputraḥ pratāpavānc abhyadhāvata rājānaṃ pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥe tato duryodhanaṃ saṃkhye vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa nakulaś ca tato vīro rājānaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc ghorarūpair maheṣvāso vivyādha ca nanāda caa sātyakiś cāpi rājānaṃ śareṇānataparvaṇāc draupadeyās trisaptatyā dharmarājaś ca saptabhiḥe aśītyā bhīmasenaś ca śarai rājānam ārdayata samantāt kīryamāṇas tu bāṇasaṃghair mahātmabhiḥc na cacāla mahārāja sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa lāghavaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ cāpi vīryaṃ caiva mahātmanaḥc ati sarvāṇi bhūtāni dadṛśuḥ sarvamānavāḥa dhārtarāṣṭrās tu rājendra yātvā tu svalpam antaramc apaśyamānā rājānaṃ paryavartanta daṃśitāḥa teṣām āpatatāṃ ghoras tumulaḥ samajāyatac kṣubdhasya hi samudrasya prāvṛṭkāle yathā niśia samāsādya raṇe te tu rājānam aparājitamc pratyudyayur maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥa bhīmasenaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ droṇaputro nyavārayatc tato bāṇair mahārāja pramuktaiḥ sarvatodiśame nājñāyanta raṇe vīrā na diśaḥ pradiśas tathāa tāv ubhau krūrakarmāṇāv ubhau bhārata duḥsahauc ghorarūpam ayudhyetāṃ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇaue trāsayantau jagat sarvaṃ jyākṣepavihatatvacaua śakunis tu raṇe vīro yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayatc tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā subalasya suto vibhuḥd yantreṇa hanyamānau tu rathāṅgāv api cicchided maṇḍalāgraṃ dhanuś cāpi niśitāṃs tomarān apid nārācān ardhanārācān supuṇyān mudgarān apid svarṇadaṇḍāṃ ca śaktiṃ ca bhiṇḍipālān parasvadhānd nirundhayan satyadhṛtiṃ kṛtvaitat karma dāruṇame nādaṃ cakāra balavān sarvasainyāni kampayana etasminn antare vīraṃ rājānam aparājitamc apovāha rathenājau sahadevaḥ pratāpavāna athānyaṃ ratham āsthāya dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc śakuniṃ navabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥe nanāda ca mahānādaṃ pravaraḥ sarvadhanvināma tad yuddham abhavac citraṃ ghorarūpaṃ ca māriṣac īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitama ulūkas tu maheṣvāsaṃ nakulaṃ yuddhadurmadamc abhyadravad ameyātmā śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥa tathaiva nakulaḥ śūraḥ saubalasya sutaṃ raṇec śaravarṣeṇa mahatā samantāt paryavārayata tau tatra samare vīrau kulaputrau mahārathauc yodhayantāv apaśyetāṃ parasparakṛtāgasaua tathaiva kṛtavarmā tu śaineyaṃ śatrutāpanamc yodhayañ śuśubhe rājan balaṃ śakra ivāhavea duryodhano dhanuś chittvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyugeb pañcabhir niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair vivyādha marṣayanc athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa dhṛṣṭadyumno pi samare pragṛhya paramāyudhamc rājānaṃ yodhayām āsa paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvināma tayor yuddhaṃ mahac cāsīt saṃgrāme bharatarṣabhac prabhinnayor yathā saktaṃ mattayor varahastinoḥa gautamas tu raṇe kruddho draupadeyān mahābalānc vivyādha bahubhiḥ śūraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa tasya tair abhavad yuddham indriyair iva dehinaḥc ghorarūpam asaṃvāryaṃ nirmaryādam atīva caa te ca taṃ pīḍayām āsur indriyāṇīva bāliśamc sa ca tān pratisaṃrabdhaḥ pratyayodhayad āhavea evaṃ citram abhūd yuddhaṃ tasya taiḥ saha bhāratac utthāyotthāya hi yathā dehinām indriyair vibhoa narāś caiva naraiḥ sārdhaṃ dantino dantibhis tathāc hayā hayaiḥ samāsaktā rathino rathibhis tathāe saṃkulaṃ cābhavad bhūyo ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patea idaṃ citram idaṃ ghoram idaṃ raudram iti prabhoc yuddhāny āsan mahārāja ghorāṇi ca bahūni caa te samāsādya samare parasparam ariṃdamāḥc vivyadhuś caiva jaghnuś ca samāsādya mahāhavea teṣāṃ śastrasamudbhūtaṃ rajas tīvram adṛśyatac pravātenoddhataṃ rājan dhāvadbhiś cāśvasādibhiḥa rathanemisamudbhūtaṃ niḥśvāsaiś cāpi dantināmc rajaḥ saṃdhyābhrakapilaṃ divākarapathaṃ yayaud ekacchāyam ivākāśaṃ samabhūt tatra dhanvināma rajasā tena saṃpṛkte bhāskare niṣprabhīkṛtec saṃchāditābhavad bhūmis te ca śūrā mahārathāḥa muhūrtād iva saṃvṛttaṃ nīrajaskaṃ samantataḥc vīraśoṇitasiktāyāṃ bhūmau bharatasattamae upāśāmyat tatas tīvraṃ tad rajo ghoradarśanama tato paśyaṃ mahārāja dvaṃdvayuddhāni bhāratac yathāprāgryaṃ yathājyeṣṭhaṃ madhyāhne vai sudāruṇee varmaṇāṃ tatra rājendra vyadṛśyantojjvalāḥ prabhāḥa śabdaḥ sutumulaḥ saṃkhye śarāṇāṃ patatām abhūtc mahāveṇuvanasyeva dahyamānasya sarvataḥ saṃjaya uvācaa vartamāne tathā yuddhe ghorarūpe bhayānakec abhajyata balaṃ tatra tava putrasya pāṇḍavaiḥa tāṃs tu yatnena mahatā saṃnivārya mahārathānc putras te yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma nivṛttāḥ sahasā yodhās tava putrapriyaiṣiṇaḥc saṃnivṛtteṣu teṣv evaṃ yuddham āsīt sudāruṇama tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca devāsuraraṇopamamc pareṣāṃ tava sainye ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥa anumānena yudhyante saṃjñābhiś ca parasparamc teṣāṃ kṣayo mahān āsīd yudhyatām itaretarama tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā krodhena mahatā yutaḥc jigīṣamāṇaḥ saṃgrāme dhārtarāṣṭrān sarājakāna tribhiḥ śāradvataṃ viddhvā rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥc caturbhir nijaghānāśvān kalyāṇān kṛtavarmaṇaḥa aśvatthāmā tu hārdikyam apovāha yaśasvinamc atha śāradvato ṣṭābhiḥ pratyavidhyad yudhiṣṭhirama tato duryodhano rājā rathān saptaśatān raṇec preṣayad yatra rājāsau dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa te rathā rathibhir yuktā manomārutaraṃhasaḥc abhyadravanta saṃgrāme kaunteyasya rathaṃ pratia te samantān mahārāja parivārya yudhiṣṭhiramc adṛśyaṃ sāyakaiś cakrur meghā iva divākaramd te dṛṣṭvā dharmarājānaṃ kauravais taṃ tathākṛtama nāmṛṣyanta susaṃrabdhāḥ śikhaṇḍipramukhā rathāḥc rathair agryajavair yuktaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālasaṃvṛtaiḥe ājagmur abhirakṣantaḥ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama tataḥ pravavṛte raudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇitodakaḥa   devāsuraraṇopamama tathānyat sumahac caivac pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥa rathān saptaśatān hatvā kurūṇām ātatāyināmc pāṇḍavāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ punar evābhyavārayana tatra yuddhaṃ mahac cāsīt tava putrasya pāṇḍavaiḥc na ca nas tādṛśaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ naiva cāpi pariśrutama vartamāne tathā yuddhe nirmaryāde samantataḥc vadhyamāneṣu yodheṣu tāvakeṣv itareṣu caa ninadatsu ca yodheṣu śaṅkhavaryaiś ca pūritaiḥb jyāghoṣair yodhamukhyānāṃ talaghoṣaiḥ samaṃtataḥc utkṛṣṭaiḥ siṃhanādaiś ca garjitena ca dhanvināma atipravṛddhe yuddhe ca chidyamāneṣu marmasuc dhāvamāneṣu yodheṣu jayagṛddhiṣu māriṣaa saṃhāre sarvato jāte pṛthivyāṃ śokasaṃbhavec bahvīnām uttamastrīṇāṃ sīmantoddharaṇe tathāa nirmaryāde tathā yuddhe vartamāne sudāruṇec prādurāsan vināśāya tadotpātāḥ sudāruṇāḥe cacāla śabdaṃ kurvāṇā saparvatavanā mahīa sadaṇḍāḥ solmukā rājañ śīryamāṇāḥ samantataḥc ulkāḥ petur divo bhūmāv āhatya ravimaṇḍalama viṣvagvātāḥ prādurāsan nīcaiḥ śarkaravarṣiṇaḥc aśrūṇi mumucur nāgā vepathuś cāspṛśad bhṛśama etān ghorān anādṛtya samutpātān sudāruṇānc punar yuddhāya saṃmantrya kṣatriyās tasthur avyathāḥe ramaṇīye kurukṣetre puṇye svargaṃ yiyāsavaḥa tato gāndhārarājasya putraḥ śakunir abravītb śakuniḥ paramayā śaktyā pāṇḍavaṃ balam ādravatc yudhyadhvam agrato yāvat pṛṣṭhato hanmi pāṇḍavānd te yāvat pṛṣṭhato hanti pāṇḍavān raṇadurmadāna tato naḥ saṃprayātānāṃ madrayodhās tarasvinaḥc hṛṣṭāḥ kilakilāśabdam akurvantāpare tathāa asmāṃs tu punar āsādya labdhalakṣā durāsadāḥc śarāsanāni dhunvantaḥ śaravarṣair avākirana tato hataṃ parais tatra madrarājabalaṃ tadāc duryodhanabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar āsīt parāṅmukhama gāndhārarājas tu punar vākyam āha tato balīc nivartadhvam adharmajñā yudhyadhvaṃ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥd suranārīratisukhaṃ vimardam evam anyathād utpāṭitaṃ dvāram etac chrīmat tridaśasadmanaḥd evam uktvā jagāmāśu śakunis tāṃ punaḥ punaḥd lakṣadhvajaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca manonilajavaṃ mahata anīkaṃ daśasāhasram aśvānāṃ bharatarṣabhac āsīd gāndhārarājasya vimalaprāsayodhināma balena tena vikramya vartamāne janakṣayec pṛṣṭhataḥ pāṇḍavānīkam abhyaghnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tad abhram iva vātena kṣipyamāṇaṃ samantataḥc abhajyata mahārāja pāṇḍūnāṃ sumahad balama tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prekṣya bhagnaṃ svabalam antikātc abhyacodayad avyagraḥ sahadevaṃ mahābalama asau subalaputro no jaghanaṃ pīḍya daṃśitaḥc senāṃ nisūdayanty eṣa paśya pāṇḍava durmatima gaccha tvaṃ draupadeyāś ca śakuniṃ saubalaṃ jahic rathānīkam ahaṃ rakṣye pāñcālasahito naghaa gacchantu kuñjarāḥ sarve vājinaś ca saha tvayāc pādātāś ca trisāhasrāḥ śakuniṃ saubalaṃ jahid kiranto yatra caivāsmān pariśiṣṭo mahāmated mamānudhyānamahimā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥd na ca śāsanakartānyas tvattas tiṣṭhati kaś canad yad ājñāpayasīty evam avadat prītimānasaḥa tato gajāḥ saptaśatāś cāpapāṇibhir āsthitāḥc pañca cāśvasahasrāṇi sahadevaś ca vīryavāna pādātāś ca trisāhasrā draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥc raṇe hy abhyadravaṃs te tu śakuniṃ yuddhadurmadama tatas tu saubalo rājann abhyatikramya pāṇḍavānc jaghāna pṛṣṭhataḥ senāṃ jayagṛdhraḥ pratāpavāna aśvārohās tu saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ tarasvināmc prāviśan saubalānīkam abhyatikramya tān rathāna te tatra sādinaḥ śūrāḥ saubalasya mahad balamc gajamadhye vatiṣṭhantaḥ śaravarṣair avākirana tad udyatagadāprāsam akāpuruṣasevitamc prāvartata mahad yuddhaṃ rājan durmantrite tavaa upāramanta jyāśabdāḥ prekṣakā rathino bhavanc na hi sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā viśeṣaḥ pratyadṛśyataa śūrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ śaktīnāṃ bharatarṣabhac jyotiṣām iva saṃpātam apaśyan kurupāṇḍavāḥa ṛṣṭibhir vimalābhiś ca tatra tatra viśāṃ patec saṃpatantībhir ākāśam āvṛtaṃ bahv aśobhataa prāsānāṃ patatāṃ rājan rūpam āsīt samantataḥc śalabhānām ivākāśe tadā bharatasattamaa rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgā vipraviddhair niyantṛbhiḥc hayāḥ paripatanti sma śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa anyonyaparipiṣṭāś ca samāsādya parasparamc avikṣatāḥ sma dṛśyante vamanto rudhiraṃ mukhaiḥa tato bhavat tamo ghoraṃ sainyena rajasā vṛtec tān apākramato drākṣaṃ tasmād deśād ariṃdamāne aśvān rājan manuṣyāṃś ca rajasā saṃvṛte satia bhūmau nipatitāś cānye vamanto rudhiraṃ bahuc keśākeśisamālagnā na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ janāḥa anyonyam aśvapṛṣṭhebhyo vikarṣanto mahābalāḥc mallā iva samāsādya nijaghnur itaretarame aśvaiś ca vyapakṛṣyanta bahavo tra gatāsavaḥa bhūmau nipatitāś cānye bahavo vijayaiṣiṇaḥc tatra tatra vyadṛśyanta puruṣāḥ śūramāninaḥa raktokṣitaiś chinnabhujair apakṛṣṭaśiroruhaiḥc vyadṛśyata mahī kīrṇā śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa dūraṃ na śakyaṃ tatrāsīd gantum aśvena kena citc sāśvārohair hatair aśvair āvṛte vasudhātalea rudhirokṣitasaṃnāhair āttaśastrair udāyudhaiḥc nānāpraharaṇair ghoraiḥ parasparavadhaiṣibhiḥe susaṃnikṛṣṭaiḥ saṃgrāme hatabhūyiṣṭhasainikaiḥa sa muhūrtaṃ tato yuddhvā saubalo tha viśāṃ patec ṣaṭsahasrair hayaiḥ śiṣṭair apāyāc chakunis tataḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavānīkaṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitamc ṣaṭsahasrair hayaiḥ śiṣṭair apāyāc chrāntavāhanama aśvārohās tu pāṇḍūnām abruvan rudhirokṣitāḥb śakuniṃ mārayāmo dya sahaputraṃ sabāndhavamb tato duryodhanaṃ pāpaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ prasādataḥc susaṃnikṛṣṭāḥ saṃgrāme bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tyaktajīvitāḥa neha śakyaṃ rathair yoddhuṃ kuta eva mahāgajaiḥc rathān eva rathā yāntu kuñjarāḥ kuñjarān apid vayaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmaḥ sahitās tyaktajīvitāḥd bhṛśaṃ palāyane tasmād upādhiṃ samupāśritāḥa pratiyāto hi śakuniḥ svam anīkam avasthitaḥc na punaḥ saubalo rājā yuddham abhyāgamiṣyatia tatas tu draupadeyāś ca te ca mattā mahādvipāḥc prayayur yatra pāñcālyo dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥa sahadevo pi kauravya rajomeghe samutthitec ekākī prayayau tatra yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥa tatas teṣu prayāteṣu śakuniḥ saubalaḥ punaḥc pārśvato bhyahanat kruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya vāhinīma tat punas tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvābhyavartatac tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca parasparavadhaiṣiṇāma te hy anyonyam avekṣanta tasmin vīrasamāgamec yodhāḥ paryapatan rājañ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa asibhiś chidyamānānāṃ śirasāṃ lokasaṃkṣayec prādurāsīn mahāśabdas tālānāṃ patatām ivaa vimuktānāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ bhinnānāṃ patatāṃ bhuvic sāyudhānāṃ ca bāhūnām urūṇāṃ ca viśāṃ patee āsīt kaṭakaṭāśabdaḥ sumahān romaharṣaṇaḥa nighnanto niśitaiḥ śastrair bhrātṝn putrān sakhīn apic yodhāḥ paripatanti sma yathāmiṣakṛte khagāḥa anyonyaṃ pratisaṃrabdhāḥ samāsādya parasparamc ahaṃ pūrvam ahaṃ pūrvam iti nyaghnan sahasraśaḥa saṃghātair āsanabhraṣṭair aśvārohair gatāsubhiḥc hayāḥ paripatanti sma śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa sphuratāṃ pratipiṣṭānām aśvānāṃ śīghrasāriṇāmc stanatāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ saṃnaddhānāṃ viśāṃ patea śaktyṛṣṭiprāsaśabdaś ca tumulaḥ samajāyatac bhindatāṃ paramarmāṇi rājan durmantrite tavad evaṃ hi yodhāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ parasparasamāhatāḥa śramābhibhūtāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ śrāntavāhāḥ pipāsitāḥc vikṣatāś ca śitaiḥ śastrair abhyavartanta tāvakāḥa mattā rudhiragandhena bahavo tra vicetasaḥc jaghnuḥ parān svakāṃś caiva prāptān prāptān anantarāna bahavaś ca gataprāṇāḥ kṣatriyā jayagṛddhinaḥc bhūmāv abhyapatan rājañ śaravṛṣṭibhir āvṛtāḥa vṛkagṛdhraśṛgālānāṃ tumule modane hanic āsīd balakṣayo ghoras tava putrasya paśyataḥa narāśvakāyasaṃchannā bhūmir āsīd viśāṃ patec rudhirodakacitrā ca bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinīa asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlais takṣamāṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥc tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva nābhyavartanta bhārataa praharanto yathāśakti yāvat prāṇasya dhāraṇamc yodhāḥ paripatanti sma vamanto rudhiraṃ vraṇaiḥa śiro gṛhītvā keśeṣu kabandhaḥ samadṛśyatac udyamya niśitaṃ khaḍgaṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitama athotthiteṣu bahuṣu kabandheṣu janādhipac tathā rudhiragandhena yodhāḥ kaśmalam āviśana mandībhūte tataḥ śabde pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balamc alpāvaśiṣṭais turagair abhyavartata saubalaḥa tato bhyadhāvaṃs tvaritāḥ pāṇḍavā jayagṛddhinaḥc padātayaś ca nāgāś ca sādinaś codyatāyudhāḥa koṣṭakīkṛtya cāpy enaṃ parikṣipya ca sarvaśaḥc śastrair nānāvidhair jaghnur yuddhapāraṃ titīrṣavaḥd drāvyamāṇaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putrasya paśyataḥa tvadīyās tāṃs tu saṃprekṣya sarvataḥ samabhidrutānc sāśvapattidviparathāḥ pāṇḍavān abhidudruvuḥa ke cit padātayaḥ padbhir muṣṭibhiś ca parasparamc nijaghnuḥ samare śūrāḥ kṣīṇaśastrās tato patana rathebhyo rathinaḥ petur dvipebhyo hastisādinaḥc vimānebhya iva bhraṣṭāḥ siddhāḥ puṇyakṣayād yathāa evam anyonyam āyastā yodhā jaghnur mahāmṛdhec pitṝn bhrātṝn vayasyāṃś ca putrān api tathāparea evam āsīd amaryādaṃ yuddhaṃ bharatasattamac prāsāsibāṇakalile vartamāne sudāruṇe saṃjaya uvācaa tasmiñ śabde mṛdau jāte pāṇḍavair nihate balec aśvaiḥ saptaśataiḥ śiṣṭair upāvartata saubalaḥa sa yātvā vāhinīṃ tūrṇam abravīt tvarayan yudhic yudhyadhvam iti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamaḥe apṛcchat kṣatriyāṃs tatra kva nu rājā mahārathaḥa śakunes tu vacaḥ śrutvā ta ūcur bharatarṣabhac asau tiṣṭhati kauravyo raṇamadhye mahārathaḥa yatraitat sumahac chatraṃ pūrṇacandrasamaprabhamc yatraite satalatrāṇā rathās tiṣṭhanti daṃśitāḥa yatraiṣa śabdas tumulaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥc tatra gaccha drutaṃ rājaṃs tato drakṣyasi kauravama evam uktas tu taiḥ śūraiḥ śakuniḥ saubalas tadāc prayayau tatra yatrāsau putras tava narādhipae sarvataḥ saṃvṛto vīraiḥ samareṣv anivartibhiḥa tato duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathānīke vyavasthitamc sarathāṃs tāvakān sarvān harṣayañ śakunis tataḥa duryodhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ hṛṣṭarūpo viśāṃ patec kṛtakāryam ivātmānaṃ manyamāno bravīn nṛpama jahi rājan rathānīkam aśvāḥ sarve jitā mayāc nātyaktvā jīvitaṃ saṃkhye śakyo jetuṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥa hate tasmin rathānīke pāṇḍavenābhipālitec gajān etān haniṣyāmaḥ padātīṃś cetarāṃs tathāa śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya tāvakā jayagṛddhinaḥc javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma sarve vivṛtatūṇīrāḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥc śarāsanāni dhunvānāḥ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrirea tato jyātalanirghoṣaḥ punar āsīd viśāṃ patec prādurāsīc charāṇāṃ ca sumuktānāṃ sudāruṇaḥa tān samīpagatān dṛṣṭvā javenodyatakārmukānc uvāca devakīputraṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥa codayāśvān asaṃbhrāntaḥ praviśaitad balārṇavamc antam adya gamiṣyāmi śatrūṇāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa aṣṭādaśa dināny adya yuddhasyāsya janārdanac vartamānasya mahataḥ samāsādya parasparama anantakalpā dhvajinī bhūtvā hy eṣāṃ mahātmanāmc kṣayam adya gatā yuddhe paśya daivaṃ yathāvidhama samudrakalpaṃ tu balaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhavac asmān āsādya saṃjātaṃ goṣpadopamam acyutaa hate bhīṣme ca saṃdadhyāc chivaṃ syād iha mādhavac na ca tat kṛtavān mūḍho dhārtarāṣṭraḥ subāliśaḥa uktaṃ bhīṣmeṇa yad vākyaṃ hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca mādhavac tac cāpi nāsau kṛtavān vītabuddhiḥ suyodhanaḥa tasmiṃs tu patite bhīṣme pracyute pṛthivītalec na jāne kāraṇaṃ kiṃ nu yena yuddham avartatad hate droṇe ca karṇe ca bhūriśravasi saṃgared duḥśāsane ca śālve ca śalye ca saparicchaded bhagadatte ca vīrendre naivāśāmyata hā raṇaḥd yena bhīṣmas tathā droṇaḥ kṛpo vidura eva cad pitā mātā śamasyārthe pratyākhyātās tu pāpināa mūḍhāṃs tu sarvathā manye dhārtarāṣṭrān subāliśānc patite śaṃtanoḥ putre ye kārṣuḥ saṃyugaṃ punaḥa anantaraṃ ca nihate droṇe brahmavidāṃ varec rādheye ca vikarṇe ca naivāśāmyata vaiśasamd rādheye sūtaputre ca naiva śāmyati vaiśasama alpāvaśiṣṭe sainye smin sūtaputre ca pātitec saputre vai naravyāghre naivāśāmyata vaiśasama śrutāyuṣi hate śūre jalasaṃdhe ca pauravec śrutāyudhe ca nṛpatau naivāśāmyata vaiśasama bhūriśravasi śalye ca śālve caiva janārdanac āvantyeṣu ca vīreṣu naivāśāmyata vaiśasama jayadrathe ca nihate rākṣase cāpy alāyudhec bāhlike somadatte ca naivāśāmyata vaiśasama bhagadatte hate śūre kāmboje ca sudakṣiṇeb nānādeśasamutthe ca hate sainye pṛthagvidhec duḥśāsane ca nihate naivāśāmyata vaiśasama dṛṣṭvā ca nihatāñ śūrān pṛthaṅ māṇḍalikān nṛpānc balinaś ca raṇe kṛṣṇa naivāśāmyata vaiśasama akṣauhiṇīpatīn dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena pātitānc mohād vā yadi vā lobhān naivāśāmyata vaiśasamd hatapravīrāṃ vidhvastāṃ dṛṣṭvā cemāṃ camūṃ raṇed alambuse ca nihate naiva śāmyati vaiśasamd bhrātṝn vinihatān dṛṣṭvā vayasyān mātulān apid putrān vinihatān saṃkhye naiva śāmyati vaiśasama ko nu rājakule jātaḥ kauraveyo viśeṣataḥc nirarthakaṃ mahad vairaṃ kuryād anyaḥ suyodhanātd nṛpapravīrān vidhvastān dṛṣṭvā cemāṃ mahācamūma guṇato bhyadhikaṃ jñātvā balataḥ śauryato pi vāc amūḍhaḥ ko nu yudhyeta jānan prājño hitāhitama yan na tasya mano hy āsīt tvayoktasya hitaṃ vacaḥc praśame pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ so nyasya śṛṇuyāt kathama yena śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo droṇo vidura eva cac pratyākhyātāḥ śamasyārthe kiṃ nu tasyādya bheṣajama maurkhyād yena pitā vṛddhaḥ pratyākhyāto janārdanac tathā mātā hitaṃ vākyaṃ bhāṣamāṇā hitaiṣiṇīe pratyākhyātā hy asatkṛtya sa kasmai rocayed vacaḥa kulāntakaraṇo vyaktaṃ jāta eṣa janārdanac tathāsya dṛśyate ceṣṭā nītiś caiva viśāṃ patee naiṣa dāsyati no rājyam iti me matir acyutaa ukto haṃ bahuśas tāta vidureṇa mahātmanāc na jīvan dāsyate bhāgaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ kathaṃ canaa yāvat prāṇā dhamiṣyanti dhārtarāṣṭrasya mānadac tāvad yuṣmāsv apāpeṣu pracariṣyati pātakama na sa yukto nyathā jetum ṛte yuddhena mādhavac ity abravīt sadā māṃ hi viduraḥ satyadarśanaḥa tat sarvam adya jānāmi vyavasāyaṃ durātmanaḥc yad uktaṃ vacanaṃ tena vidureṇa mahātmanāa yo hi śrutvā vacaḥ pathyaṃ jāmadagnyād yathātathamc avāmanyata durbuddhir dhruvaṃ nāśamukhe sthitaḥa uktaṃ hi bahubhiḥ siddhair jātamātre suyodhanec enaṃ prāpya durātmānaṃ kṣayaṃ kṣatraṃ gamiṣyatia tad idaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ niruktaṃ vai janārdanac kṣayaṃ yātā hi rājāno duryodhanakṛte bhṛśama so dya sarvān raṇe yodhān nihaniṣyāmi mādhavac kṣatriyeṣu hateṣv āśu śūnye ca śibire kṛtea vadhāya cātmano smābhiḥ saṃyugaṃ rocayiṣyatic tad antaṃ hi bhaved vairam anumānena mādhavaa evaṃ paśyāmi vārṣṇeya cintayan prajñayā svayāc vidurasya ca vākyena ceṣṭayā ca durātmanaḥa saṃyāhi bhāratīṃ vīra yāvad dhanmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥc duryodhanaṃ durātmānaṃ vāhinīṃ cāsya saṃyugea kṣemam adya kariṣyāmi dharmarājasya mādhavac hatvaitad durbalaṃ sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya paśyataḥ saṃjaya uvācaa abhīśuhasto dāśārhas tathoktaḥ savyasācināc tad balaugham amitrāṇām abhītaḥ prāviśad raṇea śarāsanavaraṃ ghoraṃ śaktikaṇṭakasaṃvṛtamc gadāparighapanthānaṃ rathanāgamahādrumama hayapattilatākīrṇaṃ gāhamāno mahāyaśāḥc vyacarat tatra govindo rathenātipatākināa te hayāḥ pāṇḍurā rājan vahanto rjunam āhavec dikṣu sarvāsv adṛśyanta dāśārheṇa pracoditāḥa tataḥ prāyād rathenājau savyasācī paraṃtapaḥc kirañ śaraśatāṃs tīkṣṇān vāridhārā ivāmbudaḥa prādurāsīn mahāñ śabdaḥ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇāmc iṣubhiś chādyamānānāṃ samare savyasācināa asajjantas tanutreṣu śaraughāḥ prāpatan bhuvic indrāśanisamasparśā gāṇḍīvapreṣitāḥ śarāḥa narān nāgān samāhatya hayāṃś cāpi viśāṃ patec apatanta raṇe bāṇāḥ pataṃgā iva ghoṣiṇaḥa āsīt sarvam avacchannaṃ gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥc na prājñāyanta samare diśo vā pradiśo pi vāa sarvam āsīj jagat pūrṇaṃ pārthanāmāṅkitaiḥ śaraiḥc rukmapuṅkhais tailadhautaiḥ karmāraparimārjitaiḥa te dahyamānāḥ pārthena pāvakeneva kuñjarāḥc samāsīdanta kauravyā vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa śaracāpadharaḥ pārthaḥ prajvalann iva bhāratac dadāha samare yodhān kakṣam agnir iva jvalana yathā vanānte vanapair visṛṣṭaḥkakṣaṃ dahet kṛṣṇagatiḥ saghoṣaḥc bhūridrumaṃ śuṣkalatāvitānaṃbhṛśaṃ samṛddho jvalanaḥ pratāpīa evaṃ sa nārācagaṇapratāpīśarārcir uccāvacatigmatejāḥc dadāha sarvāṃ tava putrasenāmamṛṣyamāṇas tarasā tarasvīa tasyeṣavaḥ prāṇaharāḥ sumuktānāsajjan vai varmasu rukmapuṅkhāḥc na ca dvitīyaṃ pramumoca bāṇaṃnare haye vā paramadvipe vāa anekarūpākṛtibhir hi bāṇairmahārathānīkam anupraviśyac sa eva ekas tava putrasenāṃjaghāna daityān iva vajrapāṇiḥc dhanaṃjayaḥ saṃyati sāyakair vā saṃjaya uvācaa asyatāṃ yatamānānāṃ śūrāṇām anivartināmc saṃkalpam akaron moghaṃ gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥa indrāśanisamasparśān aviṣahyān mahaujasaḥc visṛjan dṛśyate bāṇān dhārā muñcann ivāmbudaḥa tat sainyaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ kirīṭināc saṃpradudrāva saṃgrāmāt tava putrasya paśyataḥd pitṝn bhrātṝn parityajya vayasyān api cāparea hatadhuryā rathāḥ ke cid dhatasūtās tathāparec bhagnākṣayugacakreṣāḥ ke cid āsan viśāṃ patea anyeṣāṃ sāyakāḥ kṣīṇās tathānye śarapīḍitāḥc akṣatā yugapat ke cit prādravan bhayapīḍitāḥa ke cit putrān upādāya hatabhūyiṣṭhavāhanāḥc vicukruśuḥ pitṝn anye sahāyān apare punaḥa bāndhavāṃś ca naravyāghra bhrātṝn saṃbandhinas tathāc dudruvuḥ ke cid utsṛjya tatra tatra viśāṃ patea bahavo tra bhṛśaṃ viddhā muhyamānā mahārathāḥc niṣṭanantaḥ sma dṛśyante pārthabāṇahatā narāḥa tān anye ratham āropya samāśvāsya muhūrtakamc viśrāntāś ca vitṛṣṇāś ca punar yuddhāya jagmirea tān apāsya gatāḥ ke cit punar eva yuyutsavaḥc kurvantas tava putrasya śāsanaṃ yuddhadurmadāḥa pānīyam apare pītvā paryāśvāsya ca vāhanamc varmāṇi ca samāropya ke cid bharatasattamaa samāśvāsyāpare bhrātṝn nikṣipya śibire pi cac putrān anye pitṝn anye punar yuddham arocayana sajjayitvā rathān ke cid yathāmukhyaṃ viśāṃ patec āplutya pāṇḍavānīkaṃ punar yuddham arocayana te śūrāḥ kiṅkiṇījālaiḥ samācchannā babhāsirec trailokyavijaye yuktā yathā daiteyadānavāḥa āgamya sahasā ke cid rathaiḥ svarṇavibhūṣitaiḥc pāṇḍavānām anīkeṣu dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayana dhṛṣṭadyumno pi pāñcālyaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥc nākuliś ca śatānīko rathānīkam ayodhayana pāñcālyas tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥc abhyadravat susaṃrabdhas tāvakān hantum udyataḥd abhyayus tāvakān yuddhe śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa tatas tv āpatatas tasya tava putro janādhipac bāṇasaṃghān anekān vai preṣayām āsa bhāratad ekaikaṃ daśabhir bāṇair avidhyad bharatarṣabhaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājaṃs tava putreṇa dhanvināc nārācair bahubhiḥ kṣipraṃ bāhvor urasi cārpitaḥc nārācair ardhanārācair bahubhiḥ kṣiprakāribhiḥd vatsadantaiś ca bāṇaiś ca karmāraparimārjitaiḥd aśvāṃś ca caturo hatvāa so tividdho maheṣvāsas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥc tasyāśvāṃś caturo bāṇaiḥ preṣayām āsa mṛtyavee sāratheś cāsya bhallena śiraḥ kāyād apāharata tato duryodhano rājā pṛṣṭham āruhya vājinaḥc apākrāmad dhataratho nātidūram ariṃdamaḥa dṛṣṭvā tu hatavikrāntaṃ svam anīkaṃ mahābalaḥc tava putro mahārāja prayayau yatra saubalaḥa tato ratheṣu bhagneṣu trisāhasrā mahādvipāḥc pāṇḍavān rathinaḥ pañca samantāt paryavārayana te vṛtāḥ samare pañca gajānīkena bhāratac aśobhanta naravyāghrā grahā vyāptā ghanair ivaa tato rjuno mahārāja labdhalakṣo mahābhujaḥc viniryayau rathenaiva śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥa taiḥ samantāt parivṛtaḥ kuñjaraiḥ parvatopamaiḥc nārācair vimalais tīkṣṇair gajānīkam apothayata tatraikabāṇanihatān apaśyāma mahāgajānc patitān pātyamānāṃś ca vibhinnān savyasācināa bhīmasenas tu tān dṛṣṭvā nāgān mattagajopamaḥc kareṇa gṛhya mahatīṃ gadām abhyapatad balīe avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥa tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathamc vitresus tāvakāḥ sainyāḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥe āvignaṃ ca balaṃ sarvaṃ gadāhaste vṛkodarea gadayā bhīmasenena bhinnakumbhān rajasvalānb pātyamānān prapaśyāma līnakumbhān kṣaradvraṇānc dhāvamānān apaśyāma kuñjarān parvatopamāna pradhāvya kuñjarās te tu bhīmasenagadāhatāḥc petur ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥa tān bhinnakumbhān subahūn dravamāṇān itas tataḥc patamānāṃś ca saṃprekṣya vitresus tava sainikāḥa yudhiṣṭhiro pi saṃkruddho mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc gṛdhrapakṣaiḥ śitair bāṇair jaghnur vai gajayodhinaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare parājitya narādhipamc apakrānte tava sute hayapṛṣṭhaṃ samāśritea dṛṣṭvā ca pāṇḍavān sarvān kuñjaraiḥ parivāritānc dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja saha sarvaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥe putraḥ pāñcālarājasya jighāṃsuḥ kuñjarān yayaua adṛṣṭvā tu rathānīke duryodhanam ariṃdamamc aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥe apṛcchan kṣatriyāṃs tatra kva nu duryodhano gataḥa apaśyamānā rājānaṃ vartamāne janakṣayec manvānā nihataṃ tatra tava putraṃ mahārathāḥe viṣaṇṇavadanā bhūtvā paryapṛcchanta te sutama āhuḥ ke cid dhate sūte prayāto yatra saubalaḥc apare tv abruvaṃs tatra kṣatriyā bhṛśavikṣatāḥa duryodhanena kiṃ kāryaṃ drakṣyadhvaṃ yadi jīvatic yudhyadhvaṃ sahitāḥ sarve kiṃ vo rājā kariṣyatid tatas te kṣatriyāḥ sarve svadharmeṣu vyavasthitāḥa te kṣatriyāḥ kṣatair gātrair hatabhūyiṣṭhavāhanāḥc śaraiḥ saṃpīḍyamānāś ca nātivyaktam ivābruvana idaṃ sarvaṃ balaṃ hanmo yena sma parivāritāḥc ete sarve gajān hatvā upayānti sma pāṇḍavāḥa śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣām aśvatthāmā mahābalaḥc hitvā pāñcālarājasya tad anīkaṃ durutsahama kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca prayayur yatra saubalaḥc rathānīkaṃ parityajya śūrāḥ sudṛḍhadhanvinaḥa tatas teṣu prayāteṣu dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥc āyayuḥ pāṇḍavā rājan vinighnantaḥ sma tāvakāna dṛṣṭvā tu tān āpatataḥ saṃprahṛṣṭān mahārathānc parākrāntāṃs tato vīrān nirāśāñ jīvite tadāe vivarṇamukhabhūyiṣṭham abhavat tāvakaṃ balama parikṣīṇāyudhān dṛṣṭvā tān ahaṃ parivāritānc rājan balena dvyaṅgena tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥa ātmanāpañcamo yudhyaṃ pāñcālasya balena hac tasmin deśe vyavasthāpya yatra śāradvataḥ sthitaḥa saṃprayuddhā vayaṃ pañca kirīṭiśarapīḍitāḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahānīkaṃ tatra no bhūd raṇo mahāne jitās tena vayaṃ sarve vyapayāma raṇāt tataḥa athāpaśyaṃ sātyakiṃ tam upāyāntaṃ mahārathamc rathaiś catuḥśatair vīro māṃ cābhyadravad āhavea dhṛṣṭadyumnād ahaṃ muktaḥ kathaṃ cic chrāntavāhanaḥc patito mādhavānīkaṃ duṣkṛtī narakaṃ yathāe tatra yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ muhūrtam atidāruṇama sātyakis tu mahābāhur mama hatvā paricchadamc jīvagrāham agṛhṇān māṃ mūrchitaṃ patitaṃ bhuvid sarve jayāya dhāvanti mayā labdho dya saṃjayaḥd iti bruvāṇaḥ śaineyo rājan mām agrahīt tadāa tato muhūrtād iva tad gajānīkam avadhyatac gadayā bhīmasenena nārācair arjunena caa pratipiṣṭair mahānāgaiḥ samantāt parvatopamaiḥc nātiprasiddheva gatiḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyatad viniryayau rathenaiva śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥa rathamārgāṃs tataś cakre bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārāja vyapakarṣan mahāgajāna aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥc apaśyanto rathānīke duryodhanam ariṃdamame rājānaṃ mṛgayām āsus tava putraṃ mahārathama parityajya ca pāñcālaṃ prayātā yatra saubalaḥc rājño darśanasaṃvignā vartamāne janakṣaye saṃjaya uvācaa gajānīke hate tasmin pāṇḍuputreṇa bhāratac vadhyamāne bale caiva bhīmasenena saṃyugea carantaṃ ca tathā dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenam ariṃdamamc daṇḍahastaṃ yathā kruddham antakaṃ prāṇahāriṇama sametya samare rājan hataśeṣāḥ sutās tavac adṛśyamāne kauravye putre duryodhane tavae sodaryāḥ sahitā bhūtvā bhīmasenam upādravanf śrutavān saṃjayaś caiva jayatsenaḥ śrutāntakaḥf durvimocanakaś caiva tathā durviṣaho balīf śrutavarmā śrutarvā ca sujāto durvimocanaḥa durmarṣaṇo mahārāja jaitro bhūribalo raviḥb jayatsenaḥ sujātaś ca tathā durviṣaho rihāb durvimocananāmā ca duṣpradharṣas tathaiva cab śrutarvā ca mahābāhuḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥc ity ete sahitā bhūtvā tava putrāḥ samantataḥe bhīmasenam abhidrutya rurudhuḥ sarvatodiśama tato bhīmo mahārāja svarathaṃ punar āsthitaḥc mumoca niśitān bāṇān putrāṇāṃ tava marmasua te kīryamāṇā bhīmena putrās tava mahāraṇec bhīmasenam apāsedhan pravaṇād iva kuñjaramd bhīmam eva samājaghnuḥ smarantaṃ pūrvakilbiṣama tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmaḥ śiro durmarṣaṇasya hac kṣurapreṇa pramathyāśu pātayām āsa bhūtalea tato pareṇa bhallena sarvāvaraṇabhedināc śrutāntam avadhīd bhīmas tava putraṃ mahārathaḥa jayatsenaṃ tato viddhvā nārācena hasann ivac pātayām āsa kauravyaṃ rathopasthād ariṃdamaḥe sa papāta rathād rājan bhūmau tūrṇaṃ mamāra caa śrutarvā tu tato bhīmaṃ kruddho vivyādha māriṣac śatena gṛdhravājānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇāma tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmo jaitraṃ bhūribalaṃ ravimc trīn etāṃs tribhir ānarchad viṣāgnipratimaiḥ śaraiḥa te hatā nyapatan bhūmau syandanebhyo mahārathāḥc vasante puṣpaśabalā nikṛttā iva kiṃśukāḥa tato pareṇa tīkṣṇena nārācena paraṃtapaḥc durvimocanam āhatya preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea sa hataḥ prāpatad bhūmau svarathād rathināṃ varaḥc gires tu kūṭajo bhagno māruteneva pādapaḥa duṣpradharṣaṃ tataś caiva sujātaṃ ca sutau tavac ekaikaṃ nyavadhīt saṃkhye dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ camūmukhee tau śilīmukhaviddhāṅgau petatū rathasattamaua tato yatantam aparam abhivīkṣya sutaṃ tavac bhallena yudhi vivyādha bhīmo durviṣahaṃ raṇee sa papāta hato vāhāt paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvināma dṛṣṭvā tu nihatān bhrātṝn bahūn ekena saṃyugec amarṣavaśam āpannaḥ śrutarvā bhīmam abhyayāta vikṣipan sumahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitamc visṛjan sāyakāṃś caiva viṣāgnipratimān bahūna sa tu rājan dhanuś chittvā pāṇḍavasya mahāmṛdhec athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ viṃśatyā samavākirata tato nyad dhanur ādāya bhīmaseno mahārathaḥc avākirat tava sutaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta mahad āsīt tayor yuddhaṃ citrarūpaṃ bhayānakamc yādṛśaṃ samare pūrvaṃ jambhavāsavayor abhūta tayos tatra śarair muktair yamadaṇḍanibhaiḥ śubhaiḥa   avacchannā dharābhavatc samācchannā dharā sarvā khaṃ ca sarvā diśas tathāa tataḥ śrutarvā saṃkruddho dhanur āyamya sāyakaiḥc bhīmasenaṃ raṇe rājan bāhvor urasi cārpayata so tividdho mahārāja tava putreṇa dhanvināc bhīmaḥ saṃcukṣubhe kruddhaḥ parvaṇīva mahodadhiḥa tato bhīmo ruṣāviṣṭaḥ putrasya tava māriṣac sārathiṃ caturaś cāśvān bāṇair ninye yamakṣayama virathaṃ taṃ samālakṣya viśikhair lomavāhibhiḥc avākirad ameyātmā darśayan pāṇilāghavama śrutarvā viratho rājann ādade khaḍgacarmaṇīc athāsyādadataḥ khaḍgaṃ śatacandraṃ ca bhānumate kṣurapreṇa śiraḥ kāyāt pātayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥa chinnottamāṅgasya tataḥ kṣurapreṇa mahātmanaḥc papāta kāyaḥ sa rathād vasudhām anunādayana tasmin nipatite vīre tāvakā bhayamohitāḥc abhyadravanta saṃgrāme bhīmasenaṃ yuyutsavaḥa tān āpatata evāśu hataśeṣād balārṇavātc daṃśitaḥ pratijagrāha bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavāne te tu taṃ vai samāsādya parivavruḥ samantataḥa tatas tu saṃvṛto bhīmas tāvakair niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc pīḍayām āsa tān sarvān sahasrākṣa ivāsurāna tataḥ pañcaśatān hatvā savarūthān mahārathānc jaghāna kuñjarānīkaṃ punaḥ saptaśataṃ yudhia hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi pattīnāṃ parameṣubhiḥc vājināṃ ca śatāny aṣṭau pāṇḍavaḥ sma virājatea bhīmasenas tu kaunteyo hatvā yuddhe sutāṃs tavac mene kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ saphalaṃ janma ca prabhoa taṃ tathā yudhyamānaṃ ca vinighnantaṃ ca tāvakānc īkṣituṃ notsahante sma tava sainyāni bhārataa vidrāvya tu kurūn sarvāṃs tāṃś ca hatvā padānugānc dorbhyāṃ śabdaṃ tataś cakre trāsayāno mahādvipāna hatabhūyiṣṭhayodhā tu tava senā viśāṃ patec kiṃciccheṣā mahārāja kṛpaṇā samapadyata saṃjaya uvācaa duryodhano mahārāja sudarśaś cāpi te sutaḥc hataśeṣau tadā saṃkhye vājimadhye vyavasthitaua tato duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā vājimadhye vyavasthitamc uvāca devakīputraḥ kuntīputraṃ dhanaṃjayama śatravo hatabhūyiṣṭhā jñātayaḥ paripālitāḥc gṛhītvā saṃjayaṃ cāsau nivṛttaḥ śinipuṃgavaḥa pariśrāntaś ca nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca bhāratac yodhayitvā raṇe pāpān dhārtarāṣṭrapadānugāna suyodhanam abhityajya traya ete vyavasthitāḥc kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca drauṇiś caiva mahārathaḥa asau tiṣṭhati pāñcālyaḥ śriyā paramayā yutaḥc duryodhanabalaṃ hatvā saha sarvaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥa asau duryodhanaḥ pārtha vājimadhye vyavasthitaḥc chatreṇa dhriyamāṇena prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥa prativyūhya balaṃ sarvaṃ raṇamadhye vyavasthitaḥc enaṃ hatvā śitair bāṇaiḥ kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasia gajānīkaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tvāṃ ca prāptam ariṃdamac yāvan na vidravanty ete tāvaj jahi suyodhanama yātu kaś cit tu pāñcālyaṃ kṣipram āgamyatām itic pariśrāntabalas tāta naiṣa mucyeta kilbiṣīa tava hatvā balaṃ sarvaṃ saṃgrāme dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥc jitān pāṇḍusutān matvā rūpaṃ dhārayate mahatd yathā daityacamūṃ hatvā purā śakro mahābalaḥa nihataṃ svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā pīḍitaṃ cāpi pāṇḍavaiḥc dhruvam eṣyati saṃgrāme vadhāyaivātmano nṛpaḥa evam uktaḥ phalgunas tu kṛṣṇaṃ vacanam abravītc dhṛtarāṣṭrasutāḥ sarve hatā bhīmena mānadae yāv etāv āsthitau kṛṣṇa tāv adya na bhaviṣyataḥa hato bhīṣmo hato droṇaḥ karṇo vaikartano hataḥc madrarājo hataḥ śalyo hataḥ kṛṣṇa jayadrathaḥa hayāḥ pañcaśatāḥ śiṣṭāḥ śakuneḥ saubalasya cac rathānāṃ tu śate śiṣṭe dve eva tu janārdanae dantināṃ ca śataṃ sāgraṃ trisāhasrāḥ padātayaḥa aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva trigartādhipatis tathāc ulūkaḥ śakuniś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥa etad balam abhūc cheṣaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhavac mokṣo na nūnaṃ kālād dhi vidyate bhuvi kasya cita tathā vinihate sainye paśya duryodhanaṃ sthitamc adyāhnā hi mahārājo hatāmitro bhaviṣyatia na hi me mokṣyate kaś cit pareṣām iti cintayec ye tv adya samaraṃ kṛṣṇa na hāsyanti raṇotkaṭāḥe tān vai sarvān haniṣyāmi yady api syur amānuṣāḥa adya yuddhe susaṃkruddho dīrghaṃ rājñaḥ prajāgaramc apaneṣyāmi gāndhāraṃ pātayitvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥa nikṛtyā vai durācāro yāni ratnāni saubalaḥc sabhāyām aharad dyūte punas tāny āharāmy ahama adya tā api vetsyanti sarvā nāgapurastriyaḥc śrutvā patīṃś ca putrāṃś ca pāṇḍavair nihatān yudhia samāptam adya vai karma sarvaṃ kṛṣṇa bhaviṣyatic adya duryodhano dīptāṃ śriyaṃ prāṇāṃś ca tyakṣyatia nāpayāti bhayāt kṛṣṇa saṃgrāmād yadi cen mamac nihataṃ viddhi vārṣṇeya dhārtarāṣṭraṃ subāliśama mama hy etad aśaktaṃ vai vājivṛndam ariṃdamac soḍhuṃ jyātalanirghoṣaṃ yāhi yāvan nihanmy ahama evam uktas tu dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavena yaśasvināc acodayad dhayān rājan duryodhanabalaṃ pratia tad anīkam abhiprekṣya trayaḥ sajjā mahārathāḥc bhīmaseno rjunaś caiva sahadevaś ca māriṣae prayayuḥ siṃhanādena duryodhanajighāṃsayāa tān prekṣya sahitān sarvāñ javenodyatakārmukānc saubalo bhyadravad yuddhe pāṇḍavān ātatāyinaḥa sudarśanas tava suto bhīmasenaṃ samabhyayātc suśarmā śakuniś caiva yuyudhāte kirīṭināe sahadevaṃ tava suto hayapṛṣṭhagato bhyayāta tato hy ayatnataḥ kṣipraṃ tava putro janādhipac prāsena sahadevasya śirasi prāharad bhṛśama sopāviśad rathopasthe tava putreṇa tāḍitaḥc rudhirāplutasarvāṅga āśīviṣa iva śvasana pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ sahadevo viśāṃ patec duryodhanaṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃkruddhaḥ samavākirata pārtho pi yudhi vikramya kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc śūrāṇām aśvapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ śirāṃsi nicakarta haa tad anīkaṃ tadā pārtho vyadhamad bahubhiḥ śaraiḥc pātayitvā hayān sarvāṃs trigartānāṃ rathān yayaua tatas te sahitā bhūtvā trigartānāṃ mahārathāḥc arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca śaravarṣair avākirana satyakarmāṇam ākṣipya kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥc tato sya syandanasyeṣāṃ cicchide pāṇḍunandanaḥa śilāśitena ca vibho kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥc śiraś ciccheda prahasaṃs taptakuṇḍalabhūṣaṇamd hāhākāras tato jāto hate vīre suśarmaṇid tāvakānāṃ balaughānāṃ rājan durmantritāt tavaa satyeṣum atha cādatta yodhānāṃ miṣatāṃ tataḥc yathā siṃho vane rājan mṛgaṃ paribubhukṣitaḥa taṃ nihatya tataḥ pārthaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥc viddhvā tān ahanat sarvān rathān rukmavibhūṣitāna tatas tu pratvaran pārtho dīrghakālaṃ susaṃbhṛtamc muñcan krodhaviṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ prasthalādhipatiṃ pratia tam arjunaḥ pṛṣatkānāṃ śatena bharatarṣabhac pūrayitvā tato vāhān nyahanat tasya dhanvinaḥa tataḥ śaraṃ samādāya yamadaṇḍopamaṃ śitamc suśarmāṇaṃ samuddiśya cikṣepāśu hasann ivaa sa śaraḥ preṣitas tena krodhadīptena dhanvināc suśarmāṇaṃ samāsādya bibheda hṛdayaṃ raṇea sa gatāsur mahārāja papāta dharaṇītalec nandayan pāṇḍavān sarvān vyathayaṃś cāpi tāvakāna suśarmāṇaṃ raṇe hatvā putrān asya mahārathānc sapta cāṣṭau ca triṃśac ca sāyakair anayat kṣayama tato sya niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvān hatvā padānugānc abhyagād bhāratīṃ senāṃ hataśeṣāṃ mahārathaḥa bhīmas tu samare kruddhaḥ putraṃ tava janādhipac sudarśanam adṛśyaṃ taṃ śaraiś cakre hasann ivaa tato sya prahasan kruddhaḥ śiraḥ kāyād apāharatc kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena sa hataḥ prāpatad bhuvia tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre tatas tasya padānugāḥa   tad anīkavanaṃ mahata adahad bhīmasenas tu helayā bāṇavahnināc parivavrū raṇe bhīmaṃ kiranto viśikhāñ śitāna tatas tu niśitair bāṇais tad anīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥc indrāśanisamasparśaiḥ samantāt paryavākirate tataḥ kṣaṇena tad bhīmo nyahanad bharatarṣabhaa teṣu tūtsādyamāneṣu senādhyakṣā mahābalāḥc bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya tato yudhyanta bhāratae tāṃs tu sarvāñ śarair ghorair avākirata pāṇḍavaḥa tathaiva tāvakā rājan pāṇḍaveyān mahārathānc śaravarṣeṇa mahatā samantāt paryavārayana vyākulaṃ tad abhūt sarvaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ paraiḥ sahac tāvakānāṃ ca samare pāṇḍaveyair yuyutsatāma tatra yodhās tadā petuḥ parasparasamāhatāḥc ubhayoḥ senayo rājan saṃśocantaḥ sma bāndhavān saṃjaya uvācaa tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme naravājigajakṣayec śakuniḥ saubalo rājan sahadevaṃ samabhyayāta tato syāpatatas tūrṇaṃ sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc śaraughān preṣayām āsa pataṃgān iva śīghragāne ulūkaś ca raṇe bhīmaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa śakunis tu mahārāja bhīmaṃ viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥc sāyakānāṃ navatyā vai sahadevam avākirata te śūrāḥ samare rājan samāsādya parasparamc vivyadhur niśitair bāṇaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥe svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilādhautair ā karṇāt prahitaiḥ śaraiḥa teṣāṃ cāpabhujotsṛṣṭā śaravṛṣṭir viśāṃ patec ācchādayad diśaḥ sarvā dhārābhir iva toyadaḥa tataḥ kruddho raṇe bhīmaḥ sahadevaś ca bhāratac ceratuḥ kadanaṃ saṃkhye kurvantau sumahābalaua tābhyāṃ śaraśataiś channaṃ tad balaṃ tava bhāratac andhakāram ivākāśam abhavat tatra tatra haa aśvair viparidhāvadbhiḥ śaracchannair viśāṃ patec tatra tatra kṛto mārgo vikarṣadbhir hatān bahūna nihatānāṃ hayānāṃ ca sahaiva hayayodhibhiḥc varmabhir vinikṛttaiś ca prāsaiś chinnaiś ca māriṣad ṛṣṭibhiḥ śaktibhiś caiva tomaraiś ca paraṃtapae saṃchannā pṛthivī jajñe kusumaiḥ śabalā ivaa yodhās tatra mahārāja samāsādya parasparamc vyacaranta raṇe kruddhā vinighnantaḥ parasparama udvṛttanayanai roṣāt saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭair mukhaiḥc sakuṇḍalair mahī kravyādagaṇasaṃkīrṇā ghorābhūt pṛthivī vibhoa alpāvaśiṣṭe sainye tu kauraveyān mahāhavec prahṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavā bhūtvā ninyire yamasādanama etasminn antare śūraḥ saubaleyaḥ pratāpavānc prāsena sahadevasya śirasi prāharad bhṛśame sa vihvalo mahārāja rathopastha upāviśata sahadevaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc sarvasainyāni saṃkruddho vārayām āsa bhārataa nirbibheda ca nārācaiḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥc vinirbhidyākaroc caiva siṃhanādam ariṃdamaa tena śabdena vitrastāḥ sarve sahayavāraṇāḥc prādravan sahasā bhītāḥ śakuneś ca padānugāḥa prabhagnān atha tān dṛṣṭvā rājā duryodhano bravītc nivartadhvam adharmajñā yudhyadhvaṃ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥa iha kīrtiṃ samādhāya pretya lokān samaśnutec prāṇāñ jahāti yo vīro yudhi pṛṣṭham adarśayand śūliyāsapāśam atikramya śakralokaṃ samaśnutea evam uktās tu te rājñā saubalasya padānugāḥc pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama dravadbhis tatra rājendra kṛtaḥ śabdo tidāruṇaḥc kṣubdhasāgarasaṃkāśaḥ kṣubhitaḥ sarvato bhavata tāṃs tadāpatato dṛṣṭvā saubalasya padānugānc pratyudyayur mahārāja pāṇḍavā vijaye vṛtāḥa pratyāśvasya ca durdharṣaḥ sahadevo viśāṃ patec śakuniṃ daśabhir viddhvā hayāṃś cāsya tribhiḥ śaraiḥe dhanuś ciccheda ca śaraiḥ saubalasya hasann ivaa athānyad dhanur ādāya śakunir yuddhadurmadaḥb sahadevaṃ cābhyavarṣac charaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥb ulūkaś ca tato rājan krodhena mahatā yutaḥc vivyādha nakulaṃ ṣaṣṭyā bhīmasenaṃ ca saptabhiḥa ulūko pi mahārāja bhīmaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥc sahadevaṃ ca saptatyā parīpsan pitaraṃ raṇea taṃ bhīmasenaḥ samare vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc śakuniṃ ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā pārśvasthāṃś ca tribhis tribhiḥa te hanyamānā bhīmena nārācais tailapāyitaiḥb pradudruvur mahārāja bhīmasenabhayārditāḥb ulūkas tu tataḥ kruddho dhanur udyamya māriṣab gatotsāhā mahārāja dudruvur bhayapīḍitāḥb ulūkas tu śitair bāṇaiḥ sahadevam avidhyatac sahadevaṃ raṇe kruddhāś chādayañ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥe parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ savidyuta ivāmbudāḥa tato syāpatataḥ śūraḥ sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc ulūkasya mahārāja bhallenāpāharac chiraḥa sa jagāma rathād bhūmiṃ sahadevena pātitaḥc rudhirāplutasarvāṅgo nandayan pāṇḍavān yudhia putraṃ tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā śakunis tatra bhāratac sāśrukaṇṭho viniḥśvasya kṣattur vākyam anusmarana cintayitvā muhūrtaṃ sa bāṣpapūrṇekṣaṇaḥ śvasanc sahadevaṃ samāsādya tribhir vivyādha sāyakaiḥa tān apāsya śarān muktāñ śarasaṃghaiḥ pratāpavānc sahadevo mahārāja dhanuś ciccheda saṃyugea chinne dhanuṣi rājendra śakuniḥ saubalas tadāc pragṛhya vipulaṃ khaḍgaṃ sahadevāya prāhiṇota tam āpatantaṃ sahasā ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec dvidhā ciccheda samare saubalasya hasann ivaa asiṃ dṛṣṭvā dvidhā chinnaṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmc prāhiṇot sahadevāya sā moghā nyapatad bhuvid tato gāndhāranṛpatiḥ kṛtapraticikīrṣayāa tataḥ śaktiṃ mahāghorāṃ kālarātrim ivodyatāmc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ prati saubalaḥa tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥc tridhā ciccheda samare sahadevo hasann ivaa sā papāta tridhā chinnā bhūmau kanakabhūṣaṇāc śīryamāṇā yathā dīptā gaganād vai śatahradāa śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā saubalaṃ ca bhayārditamc dudruvus tāvakāḥ sarve bhaye jāte sasaubalāḥa athotkruṣṭaṃ mahad dhy āsīt pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥc dhārtarāṣṭrās tataḥ sarve prāyaśo vimukhābhavana tān vai vimanaso dṛṣṭvā mādrīputraḥ pratāpavānc śarair anekasāhasrair vārayām āsa saṃyugea tato gāndhārakair guptaṃ pṛṣṭhair aśvair jaye dhṛtamc āsasāda raṇe yāntaṃ sahadevo tha saubalama svam aṃśam avaśiṣṭaṃ sa saṃsmṛtya śakuniṃ nṛpac rathena kāñcanāṅgena sahadevaḥ samabhyayāte adhijyaṃ balavat kṛtvā vyākṣipan sumahad dhanuḥa sa saubalam abhidrutya gṛdhrapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥc bhṛśam abhyahanat kruddhas tottrair iva mahādvipama uvāca cainaṃ medhāvī nigṛhya smārayann ivac kṣatradharme sthito bhūtvā yudhyasva puruṣo bhavaa yat tadā hṛṣyase mūḍha glahann akṣaiḥ sabhātaleb sabhāmadhye vijityā kūṭadyūtena yad bhavānc phalam adya prapadyasva karmaṇas tasya durmatea nihatās te durātmāno ye smān avahasan purāc duryodhanaḥ kulāṅgāraḥ śiṣṭas tvaṃ tasya mātulaḥa adya te yudhāṃ patiḥc vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ krodhena prahasann ivaa śakuniṃ daśabhir viddhvā caturbhiś cāsya vājinaḥc chatraṃ dhvajaṃ dhanuś cāsya chittvā siṃha ivānadata chinnadhvajadhanuśchatraḥ sahadevena saubalaḥc tato viddhaś ca bahubhiḥ sarvamarmasu sāyakaiḥa tato bhūyo mahārāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc śakuneḥ preṣayām āsa śaravṛṣṭiṃ durāsadāma tatas tu kruddhaḥ subalasya putromādrīsutaṃ sahadevaṃ vimardec prāsena jāmbūnadabhūṣaṇenajighāṃsur eko bhipapāta śīghrama mādrīsutas tasya samudyataṃ taṃprāsaṃ suvṛttau ca bhujau raṇāgrec bhallais tribhir yugapat saṃcakartananāda coccais tarasājimadhyea tasyāśukārī susamāhitenasuvarṇapuṅkhena dṛḍhāyasenab tathaiva vegāt sudṛḍhāyudhenac bhallena sarvāvaraṇātigenaśiraḥ śarīrāt pramamātha bhūyaḥd tasyottamāṅgaṃ ca bhujau suvṛttaud śaktiś ca pūrvaṃ nipapāta bhūmaud paścāt kabandhaṃ rudhirāvasiktaṃd vispandamānaṃ nipapāta ghoramd rathottamāt pārthivapārthivasyad suvarṇaratnottamabhūṣitaṃ cad sa siṃhanādaṃ vyanadan mahātmād nihatya pāpaṃ subalasya
