pakṣālikā manthanikā jarāyur jarjarānanāc khyātā dahadahā caiva tathā dhamadhamā nṛpaa khaṇḍakhaṇḍā ca rājendra pūṣaṇā maṇikuṇḍalāc amocā caiva kauravya tathā lambapayodharāa veṇuvīṇādharā caiva piṅgākṣī lohamekhalāc śaśolūkamukhī kṛṣṇā kharajaṅghā mahājavāa śiśumāramukhī śvetā lohitākṣī vibhīṣaṇāc jaṭālikā kāmacarī dīrghajihvā balotkaṭāa kāleḍikā vāmanikā mukuṭā caiva bhāratac lohitākṣī mahākāyā haripiṇḍī ca bhūmipaa ekākṣarā sukusumā kṛṣṇakarṇī ca bhāratac kṣurakarṇī catuṣkarṇī karṇaprāvaraṇā tathāa catuṣpathaniketā ca gokarṇī mahiṣānanāc kharakarṇī mahākarṇī bherīsvanamahāsvanāa śaṅkhakumbhasvanā caiva bhaṅgadā ca mahābalāc gaṇā ca sugaṇā caiva tathābhīty atha kāmadāa catuṣpatharatā caiva bhūtitīrthānyagocarāc paśudā vittadā caiva sukhadā ca mahāyaśāḥe payodā gomahiṣadā suviṣāṇā ca bhārataa pratiṣṭhā supratiṣṭhā ca rocamānā surocanāc gokarṇī ca sukarṇī ca sasirā stherikā tathāe ekacakrā megharavā meghamālā virocanāa etāś cānyāś ca bahavo mātaro bharatarṣabhac kārttikeyānuyāyinyo nānārūpāḥ sahasraśaḥa dīrghanakhyo dīrghadantyo dīrghatuṇḍyaś ca bhāratac saralā madhurāś caiva yauvanasthāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥa māhātmyena ca saṃyuktāḥ kāmarūpadharās tathāc nirmāṃsagātryaḥ śvetāś ca tathā kāñcanasaṃnibhāḥa kṛṣṇameghanibhāś cānyā dhūmrāś ca bharatarṣabhac aruṇābhā mahābhāgā dīrghakeśyaḥ sitāmbarāḥa ūrdhvaveṇīdharāś caiva piṅgākṣyo lambamekhalāḥc lambodaryo lambakarṇās tathā lambapayodharāḥa tāmrākṣyas tāmravarṇāś ca haryakṣyaś ca tathāparāḥc varadāḥ kāmacāriṇyo nityapramuditās tathāa yāmyo raudryas tathā saumyāḥ kauberyo tha mahābalāḥc vāruṇyo tha ca māhendryas tathāgneyyaḥ paraṃtapaa vāyavyaś cātha kaumāryo brāhmyaś ca bharatarṣabhab vaiṣṇavyaś ca tathā sauryo vārāhyaś ca mahābalāḥb vaiṣṇavyo tibhayāś cānyāḥ krūrarūpā bhayaṃkarāḥc rūpeṇāpsarasāṃ tulyā jave vāyusamās tathāa parapuṣṭopamā vākye tatharddhyā dhanadopamāḥc śakravīryopamāś caiva dīptyā vahnisamās tathād śatrūṇāṃ vigrahe nityaṃ bhayadās tā bhavanty utad kāmarūpadharāś caiva jave vāyusamās tathād acintyabalavīryāś ca tathācintyaparākramāḥa vṛkṣacatvaravāsinyaś catuṣpathaniketanāḥc guhāśmaśānavāsinyaḥ śailaprasravaṇālayāḥa nānābharaṇadhāriṇyo nānāmālyāmbarās tathāc nānāvicitraveṣāś ca nānābhāṣās tathaiva cad nānāvidhair bahuguṇaiś citrāyudhavibhūṣaṇaiḥa ete cānye ca bahavo gaṇāḥ śatrubhayaṃkarāḥc anujagmur mahātmānaṃ tridaśendrasya saṃmated divyāś ca pradadau tasmai nānāratnasamācitāḥa tataḥ śaktyastram adadad bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥc guhāya rājaśārdūla vināśāya suradviṣāma mahāsvanāṃ mahāghaṇṭāṃ dyotamānāṃ sitaprabhāmc taruṇādityavarṇāṃ ca patākāṃ bharatarṣabhaa dadau paśupatis tasmai sarvabhūtamahācamūmc ugrāṃ nānāpraharaṇāṃ tapovīryabalānvitāmd ajeyāṃ svaguṇair yuktāṃ nāmnā senāṃ dhanaṃjayāmd rudratulyabalair guptāṃ yodhānām ayutais tribhiḥd na sā vijānāti raṇāt kadā cid vinivartituma viṣṇur dadau vaijayantīṃ mālāṃ balavivardhinīmc umā dadau cārajasī vāsasī sūryasaprabhea gaṅgā kamaṇḍaluṃ divyam amṛtodbhavam uttamamc dadau prītyā kumārāya daṇḍaṃ caiva bṛhaspatiḥa garuḍo dayitaṃ putraṃ mayūraṃ citrabarhiṇamc aruṇas tāmracūḍaṃ ca pradadau caraṇāyudhama pāśaṃ tu varuṇo rājā balavīryasamanvitamc kṛṣṇājinaṃ tathā brahmā brahmaṇyāya dadau prabhuḥe samareṣu jayaṃ caiva pradadau lokabhāvanaḥa senāpatyam anuprāpya skando devagaṇasya hac śuśubhe jvalito rciṣmān dvitīya iva pāvakaḥe tataḥ pāriṣadaiś caiva mātṛbhiś ca samanvitaḥf yayau daityavināśāya hlādayan surapuṃgavāna sā senā nairṛtī bhīmā saghaṇṭocchritaketanāc sabherīśaṅkhamurajā sāyudhā sapatākinīe śāradī dyaur ivābhāti jyotirbhir upaśobhitāa tato devanikāyās te bhūtasenāgaṇās tathāc vādayām āsur avyagrā bherīśaṅkhāṃś ca puṣkalāna paṭahāñ jharjharāṃś caiva kṛkacān goviṣāṇikānc āḍambarān gomukhāṃś ca ḍiṇḍimāṃś ca mahāsvanāna tuṣṭuvus te kumāraṃ ca sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥc jaguś ca devagandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥa tataḥ prīto mahāsenas tridaśebhyo varaṃ dadauc ripūn hantāsmi samare ye vo vadhacikīrṣavaḥa pratigṛhya varaṃ devās tasmād vibudhasattamātc prītātmāno mahātmāno menire nihatān ripūna sarveṣāṃ bhūtasaṃghānāṃ harṣān nādaḥ samutthitaḥc apūrayata lokāṃs trīn vare datte mahātmanāa sa niryayau mahāseno mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥc vadhāya yudhi daityānāṃ rakṣārthaṃ ca divaukasāma vyavasāyo jayo dharmaḥ siddhir lakṣmīr dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥc mahāsenasya sainyānām agre jagmur narādhipaa sa tayā bhīmayā devaḥ śūlamudgarahastayāb jvalitālātadhāriṇyā citrābharaṇavarmayāc gadāmusalanārācaśaktitomarahastayāe dṛptasiṃhaninādinyā vinadya prayayau guhaḥa taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvadaiteyā rākṣasā dānavās tathāc vyadravanta diśaḥ sarvā bhayodvignāḥ samantataḥe abhyadravanta devās tān vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥa dṛṣṭvā ca sa tataḥ kruddhaḥ skandas tejobalānvitaḥc śaktyastraṃ bhagavān bhīmaṃ punaḥ punar avāsṛjate ādadhac cātmanas tejo haviṣeddha ivānalaḥa abhyasyamāne śaktyastre skandenāmitatejasāc ulkājvālā mahārāja papāta vasudhātalea saṃhrādayantaś ca tathā nirghātāś cāpatan kṣitauc yathāntakālasamaye sughorāḥ syus tathā nṛpaa kṣiptā hy ekā tathā śaktiḥ sughorānalasūnunāc tataḥ koṭyo viniṣpetuḥ śaktīnāṃ bharatarṣabhaa sa śaktyastreṇa saṃgrāme jaghāna bhagavān prabhuḥc daityendraṃ tārakaṃ nāma mahābalaparākramame vṛtaṃ daityāyutair vīrair balibhir daśabhir nṛpaa mahiṣaṃ cāṣṭabhiḥ padmair vṛtaṃ saṃkhye nijaghnivānc tripādaṃ cāyutaśatair jaghāna daśabhir vṛtama hradodaraṃ nikharvaiś ca vṛtaṃ daśabhir īśvaraḥc jaghānānucaraiḥ sārdhaṃ vividhāyudhapāṇibhiḥa tatrākurvanta vipulaṃ nādaṃ vadhyatsu śatruṣuc kumārānucarā rājan pūrayanto diśo daśad nanṛtuś ca vavalguś ca jahasuś ca mudānvitāḥa śaktyastrasya tu rājendra tato rcirbhiḥ samantataḥb trailokyaṃ trāsitaṃ sarvaṃ jṛmbhamāṇābhir eva cac dagdhāḥ sahasraśo daityā nādaiḥ skandasya cāparea patākayāvadhūtāś ca hatāḥ ke cit suradviṣaḥc ke cid ghaṇṭāravatrastā nipetur vasudhātalee ke cit praharaṇaiś chinnā vinipetur gatāsavaḥa evaṃ suradviṣo nekān balavān ātatāyinaḥc jaghāna samare vīraḥ kārttikeyo mahābalaḥa bāṇo nāmātha daiteyo baleḥ putro mahābalaḥc krauñcaṃ parvatam āsādya devasaṃghān abādhataa tam abhyayān mahāsenaḥ suraśatrum udāradhīḥc sa kārttikeyasya bhayāt krauñcaṃ śaraṇam eyivāna tataḥ krauñcaṃ mahāmanyuḥ krauñcanādanināditamc śaktyā bibheda bhagavān kārttikeyo gnidattayāa saśālaskandhasaralaṃ trastavānaravāraṇamc pulinatrastavihagaṃ viniṣpatitapannagama golāṅgūlarkṣasaṃghaiś ca dravadbhir anunāditamc kuraṅgagatinirghoṣam udbhrāntasṛmarācitama viniṣpatadbhiḥ śarabhaiḥ siṃhaiś ca sahasā drutaiḥc śocyām api daśāṃ prāpto rarājaiva sa parvataḥa vidyādharāḥ samutpetus tasya śṛṅganivāsinaḥc kiṃnarāś ca samudvignāḥ śaktipātaravoddhatāḥa tato daityā viniṣpetuḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥc pradīptāt parvataśreṣṭhād vicitrābharaṇasrajaḥa tān nijaghnur atikramya kumārānucarā mṛdheb sa caiva bhagavān kruddho daityendrasya sutaṃ tadāb sahānujaṃ jaghānāśu vṛtraṃ devapatir yathāc bibheda śaktyā krauñcaṃ ca pāvakiḥ paravīrahāa bahudhā caikadhā caiva kṛtvātmānaṃ mahātmanāc śaktiḥ kṣiptā raṇe tasya pāṇim eti punaḥ punaḥa evaṃprabhāvo bhagavān ato bhūyaś ca pāvakiḥb śauryād dviguṇayogena tejasā yaśasā śriyāc krauñcas tena vinirbhinno daityāś ca śataśo hatāḥa tataḥ sa bhagavān devo nihatya vibudhadviṣaḥc sabhājyamāno vibudhaiḥ paraṃ harṣam avāpa had bhinne krauñce girivare caṇḍaputre ca pātitea tato dundubhayo rājan neduḥ śaṅkhāś ca bhāratac mumucur devayoṣāś ca puṣpavarṣam anuttamama divyagandham upādāya vavau puṇyaś ca mārutaḥc gandharvās tuṣṭuvuś cainaṃ yajvānaś ca maharṣayaḥa ke cid enaṃ vyavasyanti pitāmahasutaṃ prabhumc sanatkumāraṃ sarveṣāṃ brahmayoniṃ tam agrajama ke cin maheśvarasutaṃ ke cit putraṃ vibhāvasoḥc umāyāḥ kṛttikānāṃ ca gaṅgāyāś ca vadanty utaa ekadhā ca dvidhā caiva caturdhā ca mahābalamc yoginām īśvaraṃ devaṃ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa etat te kathitaṃ rājan kārttikeyābhiṣecanamc śṛṇu caiva sarasvatyās tīrthavaṃśasya puṇyatāma babhūva tīrthapravaraṃ hateṣu suraśatruṣuc kumāreṇa mahārāja triviṣṭapam ivāparama aiśvaryāṇi ca tatrastho dadāv īśaḥ pṛthak pṛthakc tadā nairṛtamukhyebhyas trailokye pāvakātmajaḥa evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tasmiṃs tīrthe daityakulāntakaḥc abhiṣikto mahārāja devasenāpatiḥ suraiḥa aujasaṃ nāma tat tīrthaṃ yatra pūrvam apāṃ patiḥc abhiṣiktaḥ suragaṇair varuṇo bharatarṣabhaa tasmiṃs tīrthavare snātvā skandaṃ cābhyarcya lāṅgalīc brāhmaṇebhyo dadau rukmaṃ vāsāṃsy ābharaṇāni caa uṣitvā rajanīṃ tatra mādhavaḥ paravīrahāc pūjya tīrthavaraṃ tac ca spṛṣṭvā toyaṃ ca lāṅgalīe hṛṣṭaḥ prītamanāś caiva hy abhavan mādhavottamaḥa etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasic yathābhiṣikto bhagavān skando devaiḥ samāgataiḥd senānīś ca kṛto rājan bāla eva mahābalaḥ janamejaya uvācaa atyadbhutam idaṃ brahmañ śrutavān asmi tattvataḥc abhiṣekaṃ kumārasya vistareṇa yathāvidhia yac chrutvā pūtam ātmānaṃ vijānāmi tapodhanac prahṛṣṭāni ca romāṇi prasannaṃ ca mano mamaa abhiṣekaṃ kumārasya daityānāṃ ca vadhaṃ tathāc śrutvā me paramā prītir bhūyaḥ kautūhalaṃ hi mea apāṃ patiḥ kathaṃ hy asminn abhiṣiktaḥ surāsuraiḥc tan me brūhi mahāprājña kuśalo hy asi sattama vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa śṛṇu rājann idaṃ citraṃ pūrvakalpe yathātathamc ādau kṛtayuge tasmin vartamāne yathāvidhie varuṇaṃ devatāḥ sarvāḥ sametyedam athābruvana yathāsmān surarāṭ śakro bhayebhyaḥ pāti sarvadāc tathā tvam api sarvāsāṃ saritāṃ vai patir bhavaa vāsaś ca te sadā deva sāgare makarālayec samudro yaṃ tava vaśe bhaviṣyati nadīpatiḥa somena sārdhaṃ ca tava hānivṛddhī bhaviṣyataḥc evam astv iti tān devān varuṇo vākyam abravīta samāgamya tataḥ sarve varuṇaṃ sāgarālayamc apāṃ patiṃ pracakrur hi vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇāa abhiṣicya tato devā varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patimc jagmuḥ svāny eva sthānāni pūjayitvā jaleśvarama abhiṣiktas tato devair varuṇo pi mahāyaśāḥc saritaḥ sāgarāṃś caiva nadāṃś caiva sarāṃsi cae pālayām āsa vidhinā yathā devāñ śatakratuḥa tatas tatrāpy upaspṛśya dattvā ca vividhaṃ vasuc agnitīrthaṃ mahāprājñaḥ sa jagāma pralambahāe naṣṭo na dṛśyate yatra śamīgarbhe hutāśanaḥa lokālokavināśe ca prādurbhūte tadānaghac upatasthur mahātmānaṃ sarvalokapitāmahama agniḥ pranaṣṭo bhagavān kāraṇaṃ ca na vidmahec sarvalokakṣayo mā bhūt saṃpādayatu no nalam janamejaya uvācaa kimarthaṃ bhagavān agniḥ pranaṣṭo lokabhāvanaḥc vijñātaś ca kathaṃ devais tan mamācakṣva tattvataḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa bhṛgoḥ śāpād bhṛśaṃ bhīto jātavedāḥ pratāpavānc śamīgarbham athāsādya nanāśa bhagavāṃs tataḥa pranaṣṭe tu tadā vahnau devāḥ sarve savāsavāḥc anveṣanta tadā naṣṭaṃ jvalanaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitāḥa tato gnitīrtham āsādya śamīgarbhastham eva hic dadṛśur jvalanaṃ tatra vasamānaṃ yathāvidhia devāḥ sarve naravyāghra bṛhaspatipurogamāḥc jvalanaṃ taṃ samāsādya prītābhūvan savāsavāḥe punar yathāgataṃ jagmuḥ sarvabhakṣaś ca so bhavata bhṛgoḥ śāpān mahīpāla yad uktaṃ brahmavādināc tatrāpy āplutya matimān brahmayoniṃ jagāma haa sasarja bhagavān yatra sarvalokapitāmahaḥc tatrāplutya tato brahmā saha devaiḥ prabhuḥ purāe sasarja cānnāni tathā devatānāṃ yathāvidhia tatra snātvā ca dattvā ca vasūni vividhāni cac kauberaṃ prayayau tīrthaṃ tatra taptvā mahat tapaḥe dhanādhipatyaṃ saṃprāpto rājann ailabilaḥ prabhuḥa tatrastham eva taṃ rājan dhanāni nidhayas tathāc upatasthur naraśreṣṭha tat tīrthaṃ lāṅgalī tataḥe gatvā snātvā ca vidhivad brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dadaua dadṛśe tatra pūrayām āsa vidhivat tataḥ khyātaḥ śatakratuḥa tasya nāmnā ca tat tīrthaṃ śivaṃ puṇyaṃ sanātanamc indratīrtham iti khyātaṃ sarvapāpapramocanama upaspṛśya ca tatrāpi vidhivan musalāyudhaḥc brāhmaṇān tato hṛṣṭaḥ stūyamāno dvijātibhiḥc tasmād ādityatīrthaṃ ca jagāma kamalekṣaṇaḥa yatreṣṭvā bhagavāñ jyotir bhāskaro rājasattamac jyotiṣām ādhipatyaṃ ca prabhāvaṃ cābhyapadyataa tasyā nadyās tu tīre vai sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥc viśvedevāḥ samaruto gandharvāpsarasaś ca haa dvaipāyanaḥ śukaś caiva kṛṣṇaś ca madhusūdanaḥc yakṣāś ca rākṣasāś caiva piśācāś ca viśāṃ patea ete cānye ca bahavo yogasiddhāḥ sahasraśaḥc tasmiṃs tīrthe sarasvatyāḥ śive puṇye paraṃtapaa tatra hatvā purā viṣṇur asurau madhukaiṭabhauc āpluto bharataśreṣṭha tīrthapravara uttamea dvaipāyanaś ca dharmātmā tatraivāplutya bhāratac saṃprāptaḥ paramaṃ yogaṃ siddhiṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥa asito devalaś caiva tasminn eva mahātapāḥc paramaṃ yogam āsthāya ṛṣir yogam avāptavān vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasminn eva tu dharmātmā vasati sma tapodhanaḥc gārhasthyaṃ dharmam āsthāya asito devalaḥ purāa dharmanityaḥ śucir dānto nyastadaṇḍo mahātapāḥc karmaṇā manasā vācā samaḥ sarveṣu jantuṣua akrodhano mahārāja tulyanindāpriyāpriyaḥb priyāpriye tulyavṛttir yamavat samadarśanaḥc kāñcane loṣṭake caiva samadarśī mahātapāḥa devatāḥ pūjayan nityam atithīṃś ca dvijaiḥ sahac brahmacaryarato nityaṃ sadā dharmaparāyaṇaḥa tato bhyetya mahārāja yogam āsthāya bhikṣukaḥc jaigīṣavyo munir dhīmāṃs tasmiṃs tīrthe samāhitaḥa devalasyāśrame rājan nyavasat sa mahādyutiḥc yoganityo mahārāja siddhiṃ prāpto mahātapāḥa taṃ tatra vasamānaṃ tu jaigīṣavyaṃ mahāmunimc devalo darśayann eva naivāyuñjata dharmataḥd na jñātas tena muninā devalena mahātmanāa evaṃ tayor mahārāja dīrghakālo vyatikramatc jaigīṣavyaṃ muniṃ caiva na dadarśātha devalaḥd jaigīṣavyaḥ kadā cit sa darśayām āsa devalama āhārakāle matimān parivrāḍ janamejayac upātiṣṭhata dharmajño bhaikṣakāle sa devalama sa dṛṣṭvā bhikṣurūpeṇa prāptaṃ tatra mahāmunimc gauravaṃ paramaṃ cakre prītiṃ ca vipulāṃ tathāa devalas tu yathāśakti pūjayām āsa bhāratac ṛṣidṛṣṭena vidhinā samā bahvyaḥ samāhitaḥa kadā cit tasya nṛpate devalasya mahātmanaḥc cintā sumahatī jātā muniṃ dṛṣṭvā mahādyutima samās tu samatikrāntā bahvyaḥ pūjayato mamac na cāyam alaso bhikṣur abhyabhāṣata kiṃ canaa evaṃ vigaṇayann eva sa jagāma mahodadhimc antarikṣacaraḥ śrīmān kalaśaṃ gṛhya devalaḥa gacchann eva sa dharmātmā samudraṃ saritāṃ patimc jaigīṣavyaṃ tato paśyad gataṃ prāg eva bhārataa tataḥ savismayaś cintāṃ jagāmāthāsitaḥ prabhuḥc kathaṃ bhikṣur ayaṃ prāptaḥ samudre snāta eva caa ity evaṃ cintayām āsa maharṣir asitas tadāc snātvā samudre vidhivac chucir japyaṃ jajāpa haa kṛtajapyāhnikaḥ śrīmān āśramaṃ ca jagāma hac kalaśaṃ jalapūrṇaṃ vai gṛhītvā janamejayaa tataḥ sa praviśann eva svam āśramapadaṃ muniḥc āsīnam āśrame tatra jaigīṣavyam apaśyataa na vyāharati caivainaṃ jaigīṣavyaḥ kathaṃ canac kāṣṭhabhūto śramapade vasati sma mahātapāḥa taṃ dṛṣṭvā cāplutaṃ toye sāgare sāgaropamamc praviṣṭam āśramaṃ cāpi pūrvam eva dadarśa saḥa asito devalo rājaṃś cintayām āsa buddhimānc dṛṣṭaḥ prabhāvaṃ tapaso jaigīṣavyasya yogajama cintayām āsa rājendra tadā sa munisattamaḥc mayā dṛṣṭaḥ samudre ca āśrame ca kathaṃ tv ayama evaṃ vigaṇayann eva sa munir mantrapāragaḥc utpapātāśramāt tasmād antarikṣaṃ viśāṃ patee jijñāsārthaṃ tadā bhikṣor jaigīṣavyasya devalaḥa so ntarikṣacarān siddhān samapaśyat samāhitānc jaigīṣavyaṃ ca taiḥ siddhaiḥ pūjyamānam apaśyataa tato sitaḥ susaṃrabdho vyavasāyī dṛḍhavrataḥc apaśyad vai divaṃ yāntaṃ jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥa tasmāc ca pitṛlokaṃ taṃ vrajantaṃ so nvapaśyatac pitṛlokāc ca taṃ yāntaṃ yāmyaṃ lokam apaśyatad tasmād ādityalokaṃ ca vrajantaṃ so nvapaśyataa tasmād api samutpatya somalokam abhiṣṭutamc vrajantam anvapaśyat sa jaigīṣavyaṃ mahāmunima lokān samutpatantaṃ ca śubhān ekāntayājināmc tato gnihotriṇāṃ lokāṃs tebhyaś cāpy utpapāta haa darśaṃ ca paurṇamāsaṃ ca ye yajanti tapodhanāḥc tebhyaḥ sa dadṛśe dhīmāṃl lokebhyaḥ paśuyājināme vrajantaṃ lokam amalam apaśyad devapūjitama cāturmāsyair bahuvidhair yajante ye tapodhanāḥc teṣāṃ sthānaṃ tathā yāntaṃ tathāgniṣṭomayājināma agniṣṭutena ca tathā ye yajanti tapodhanāḥc tat sthānam anusaṃprāptam anvapaśyata devalaḥa vājapeyaṃ kratuvaraṃ tathā bahusuvarṇakamc āharanti mahāprājñās teṣāṃ lokeṣv apaśyataa yajante puṇḍarīkeṇa rājasūyena caiva yec teṣāṃ lokeṣv apaśyac ca jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥa aśvamedhaṃ kratuvaraṃ naramedhaṃ tathaiva cac āharanti naraśreṣṭhās teṣāṃ lokeṣv apaśyataa sarvamedhaṃ ca duṣprāpaṃ tathā sautrāmaṇiṃ ca yec teṣāṃ lokeṣv apaśyac ca jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥa dvādaśāhaiś ca satrair ye yajante vividhair nṛpac teṣāṃ lokeṣv apaśyac ca jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥa mitrāvaruṇayor lokān ādityānāṃ tathaiva cac salokatām anuprāptam apaśyata tato sitaḥa rudrāṇāṃ ca vasūnāṃ ca sthānaṃ yac ca bṛhaspateḥc tāni sarvāṇy atītaṃ ca samapaśyat tato sitaḥa āruhya ca gavāṃ lokaṃ prayāntaṃ brahmasatriṇāmc lokān apaśyad gacchantaṃ jaigīṣavyaṃ tato sitaḥa trīṃl lokān aparān vipram utpatantaṃ svatejasāc pativratānāṃ lokāṃś ca vrajantaṃ so nvapaśyataa tato munivaraṃ bhūyo jaigīṣavyam athāsitaḥc nānvapaśyata yogastham antarhitam ariṃdamaa so cintayan mahābhāgo jaigīṣavyasya devalaḥc prabhāvaṃ suvratatvaṃ ca siddhiṃ yogasya cātulāma asito pṛcchata tadā siddhāṃl lokeṣu sattamānc prayataḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā dhīras tān brahmasatriṇaḥa jaigīṣavyaṃ na paśyāmi taṃ śaṃsata mahaujasamc etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi med so py apṛcchad yadā siddhān abruvan pṛcchate tadād yathābhūtaṃ tathādṛṣṭaṃ prabhāvaṃ tapasāṃ nidheḥ siddhā ūcuḥa śṛṇu devala bhūtārthaṃ śaṃsatāṃ no dṛḍhavratac jaigīṣavyo gato lokaṃ śāśvataṃ brahmaṇo vyayama sa śrutvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ siddhānāṃ brahmasatriṇāmc asito devalas tūrṇam utpapāta papāta caa tataḥ siddhās ta ūcur hi devalaṃ punar eva hac na devala gatis tatra tava gantuṃ tapodhanae brahmaṇaḥ sadanaṃ vipra jaigīṣavyo yadāptavāna teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā siddhānāṃ devalaḥ punaḥc ānupūrvyeṇa lokāṃs tān sarvān avatatāra haa svam āśramapadaṃ puṇyam ājagāma pataṃgavatc praviśann eva cāpaśyaj jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥa tato buddhyā vyagaṇayad devalo dharmayuktayāc dṛṣṭvā prabhāvaṃ tapaso jaigīṣavyasya yogajama tato bravīn mahātmānaṃ jaigīṣavyaṃ sa devalaḥc vinayāvanato rājann upasarpya mahāmunime mokṣadharmaṃ samāsthātum iccheyaṃ bhagavann ahama tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā upadeśaṃ cakāra saḥc vidhiṃ ca yogasya paraṃ kāryākāryaṃ ca śāstrataḥa saṃnyāsakṛtabuddhiṃ taṃ tato dṛṣṭvā mahātapāḥc sarvāś cāsya kriyāś cakre vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇāa saṃnyāsakṛtabuddhiṃ taṃ bhūtāni pitṛbhiḥ sahac tato dṛṣṭvā praruruduḥ ko smān saṃvibhajiṣyatia devalas tu vacaḥ śrutvā bhūtānāṃ karuṇaṃ tathāc diśo daśa vyāharatāṃ mokṣaṃ tyaktuṃ mano dadhea tatas tu phalamūlāni pavitrāṇi ca bhāratac puṣpāṇy oṣadhayaś caiva rorūyante sahasraśaḥa punar no devalaḥ kṣudro nūnaṃ chetsyati durmatiḥc abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo yo dattvā nāvabudhyatea tato bhūyo vyagaṇayat svabuddhyā munisattamaḥc mokṣe gārhasthyadharme vā kiṃ nu śreyaskaraṃ bhaveta iti niścitya manasā devalo rājasattamac tyaktvā gārhasthyadharmaṃ sa mokṣadharmam arocayata evamādīni saṃcintya devalo niścayāt tataḥc prāptavān paramāṃ siddhiṃ paraṃ yogaṃ ca bhārataa tato devāḥ samāgamya bṛhaspatipurogamāḥc jaigīṣavyaṃ tapaś cāsya praśaṃsanti tapasvinaḥa athābravīd ṛṣivaro devān vai nāradas tadāc jaigīṣavye tapo nāsti vismāpayati yo sitama tam evaṃvādinaṃ dhīraṃ pratyūcus te divaukasaḥc maivam ity eva śaṃsanto jaigīṣavyaṃ mahāmunimd nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃ cit tulyam asti prabhāvataḥd tejasas tapasaś cāsya yogasya ca mahātmanaḥd evaṃprabhāvo dharmātmā jaigīṣavyas tathāsitaḥd tayor idaṃ sthānavaraṃ tīrthaṃ caiva mahātmanoḥa tatrāpy upaspṛśya tato mahātmādattvā ca vittaṃ halabhṛd dvijebhyaḥc avāpya dharmaṃ param āryakarmājagāma somasya mahat sa tīrtham vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa yatrejivān uḍupatī rājasūyena bhāratac tasmin vṛtte mahān āsīt saṃgrāmas tārakāmayaḥa tatrāpy upaspṛśya balo dattvā dānāni cātmavānc sārasvatasya dharmātmā munes tīrthaṃ jagāma haa yatra dvādaśavārṣikyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ dvijottamānc vedān adhyāpayām āsa purā sārasvato muniḥ janamejaya uvācaa kathaṃ dvādaśavārṣikyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ tapodhanaḥc vedān adhyāpayām āsa purā sārasvato muniḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa āsīt pūrvaṃ mahārāja munir dhīmān mahātapāḥc dadhīca iti vikhyāto brahmacārī jitendriyaḥa tasyātitapasaḥ śakro bibheti satataṃ vibhoc na sa lobhayituṃ śakyaḥ phalair bahuvidhair dṛṣṭvā tasyarṣer bhāvitātmanaḥc retaḥ skannaṃ sarasvatyāṃ tat sā jagrāha nimnagāa kukṣau cāpy adadhad dṛṣṭvā tad retaḥ puruṣarṣabhac sā dadhāra ca taṃ garbhaṃ putrahetor mahānadīa suṣuve cāpi samaye putraṃ sā saritāṃ varāc jagāma putram ādāya tam ṛṣiṃ prati ca prabhoa ṛṣisaṃsadi taṃ dṛṣṭvā sā nadī munisattamamc tataḥ provāca rājendra dadatī putram asya tame brahmarṣe tava putro yaṃ tvadbhaktyā praharaṇānveṣī lokāṃs trīn vicacāra haa na copalebhe bhagavāñ śakraḥ praharaṇaṃ tadāc yad vai teṣāṃ bhaved yogyaṃ vadhāya vibudhadviṣāma tato bravīt surāñ śakro na me śakyā mahāsurāḥc ṛte sthibhir nirāhārā dehaṃ tyakṣyanty atandritāḥc yudhi vā nihatāḥ samyag api tiryaggatā nṛpaa te svargabhājo rājendra bhavantv iti mahāmatec tathāstv iti tato rājā kuruḥ śakram uvāca haa tatas tam abhyanujñāpya rājarṣibhis tathād nātaḥ parataraṃ puṇyaṃ bhūmeḥ sthānaṃ bhaviṣyatid iha tapsyanti ye ke cit tapaḥ paramakaṃ narāḥd dehatyāgena te sarve yāsyanti brahmaṇaḥ kṣayamd ye punaḥ puṇyabhājo vai dānaṃ dāsyanti mānavāḥd teṣāṃ sahasraguṇitaṃ bhaviṣyaty acireṇa vaid ye ceha nityaṃ manujā nivatsyanti śubhaiṣiṇaḥd yamasya viṣayaṃ te tu na drakṣyanti kadā canad yakṣyanti ye ca kratubhir mahadbhir manujeśvarāḥd teṣāṃ triviṣṭape vāso yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyatia api cātra svayaṃ śakro jagau gāthāṃ surādhipaḥc kurukṣetre nibaddhāṃ vai tāṃ śṛṇuṣva halāyudhaa pāṃsavo pi kurukṣetrād vāyunā samudīritāḥc maunaṃ ca vīrāsanam upāsmahed evaṃ pralapamāno pi cintayaṃś ca muhur muhuḥd dūrastho yadi vā tiṣṭhaṃl labhet svargaṃ viniścitaḥa surarṣabhā brāhmaṇasattamāś catathā nṛgādyā naradevamukhyāḥc iṣṭvā puṇyam idaṃ divaukasāṃsusaṃmataṃ svargaguṇaiḥ samanvitamc ataś ca sarve pi vasuṃdharādhipāhatā gamiṣyanti mahātmanāṃ gatimd ity uvāca svayaṃ śakraḥ saha brahmādibhis tathād tac cānumoditaṃ sarvaṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvaraiḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa kurukṣetraṃ tato dṛṣṭvā dattvā dāyāṃś ca sātvataḥc āśramaṃ sumahad divyam agamaj janamejayaa madhūkāmravanopetaṃ plakṣanyagrodhasaṃkulamc ciribilvayutaṃ puṇyaṃ panasārjunasaṃkulama taṃ dṛṣṭvā yādavaśreṣṭhaḥ pravaraṃ puṇyalakṣaṇamc papraccha tān ṛṣīn sarvān kasyāśramavaras tv ayama te tu sarve mahātmānam ūcū rājan halāyudhamc śṛṇu vistarato rāma yasyāyaṃ pūrvam āśramaḥa atra viṣṇuḥ purā devas taptavāṃs tapa uttamamc atrāsya vidhivad yajñāḥ sarve vṛttāḥ sanātanāḥa atraiva brāhmaṇī siddhā kaumārabrahmacāriṇīc yogayuktā divaṃ yātā tapaḥsiddhā tapasvinīa babhūva śrīmatī rājañ śāṇḍilyasya mahātmanaḥc sutā dhṛtavratā sādhvī niyatā brahmacāriṇīd sā tu taptvā tapo ghoraṃ duścaraṃ strījanena haa sā tu prāpya paraṃ yogaṃ gatā svargam anuttamamc bhuktvāśrame śvamedhasya phalaṃ phalavatāṃ śubhāe gatā svargaṃ mahābhāgā pūjitā niyatātmabhiḥa abhigamyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca yadupuṃgavaḥb śrutvā ṛṣīṇāṃ vacanam āśramaṃ taṃ jagāma hab ṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā jagāmāśramam uttamamb tasyāśrame śvamedhasya phaḷam āpnoti mānavaḥc ṛṣīṃs tān abhivādyātha pārśve himavato cyutaḥe skandhāvārāṇi sarvāṇi nivartyāruruhe calama nātidūraṃ tato gatvā nagaṃ tāladhvajo balīc puṇyaṃ tīrthavaraṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥa prabhavaṃ ca sarasvatyāḥ plakṣaprasravaṇaṃ balaḥc saṃprāptaḥ kārapacanaṃ tīrthapravaram uttamama halāyudhas tatra cāpi dattvā dānaṃ mahābalaḥc āplutaḥ salile śīte tasmāc cāpi jagāma hae āśramaṃ paramaprīto mitrasya varuṇasya caf āplutaḥ salile puṇye suśīte vimale śucauf saṃtarpayām āsa pitṝn devāṃś ca raṇadurmadaḥf tatroṣyaikāṃ tu rajanīṃ yatibhir brāhmaṇaiḥ sahaf mitrāvaruṇayoḥ puṇyaṃ jagāmāśramam acyutaḥa indro gnir aryamā caiva yatra prāk prītim āpnuvanc taṃ deśaṃ kārapacanād yamunāyāṃ jagāma haa snātvā tatrāpi dharmātmā parāṃ tuṣṭim avāpya cac ṛṣibhiś caiva siddhaiś ca sahito vai mahābalaḥe upaviṣṭaḥ kathāḥ śubhrāḥ śuśrāva yadupuṃgavaḥa tathā tu tiṣṭhatāṃ teṣāṃ nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥc ājagāmātha taṃ deśaṃ yatra rāmo vyavasthitaḥd tatra saṃtiṣṭhataś cātha rāmasyāpratimadyuteḥd ājagāma mahātejā nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥa jaṭāmaṇḍalasaṃvītaḥ svarṇacīrī mahātapāḥc hemadaṇḍadharo rājan kamaṇḍaludharas tathāa kacchapīṃ sukhaśabdāṃ tāṃ gṛhya vīṇāṃ manoramāmc nṛtye gīte ca kuśalo devabrāhmaṇapūjitaḥa prakartā kalahānāṃ ca nityaṃ ca kalahapriyaḥc taṃ deśam agamad yatra śrīmān rāmo vyavasthitaḥa pratyutthāya tu te sarve pūjayitvā yatavratamc devarṣiṃ paryapṛcchanta yathāvṛttaṃ kurūn pratia tato syākathayad rājan nāradaḥ sarvadharmavitc sarvam eva yathāvṛttam atītaṃ kurusaṃkṣayama tato bravīd rauhiṇeyo nāradaṃ dīnayā girāc kim avasthaṃ tu tat kṣatraṃ ye ca tatrābhavan nṛpāḥa śrutam etan mayā pūrvaṃ sarvam eva tapodhanac vistaraśravaṇe jātaṃ kautūhalam atīva me nārada uvācaa pūrvam eva hato bhīṣmo droṇaḥ sindhupatis tathāc hato vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ putrāś cāsya mahārathāḥa bhūriśravā rauhiṇeya madrarājaś ca vīryavānc ete cānye ca bahavas tatra tatra mahābalāḥa priyān prāṇān parityajya priyārthaṃ kauravasya vaic rājāno rājaputrāś ca samareṣv anivartinaḥd nihatāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sarve gatāḥ svargagatiṃ pratia ahatāṃs tu mahābāho śṛṇu me tatra mādhavac dhārtarāṣṭrabale śeṣāḥ kṛpo bhojaś ca vīryavāne aśvatthāmā ca vikrānto bhagnasainyā diśo gatāḥf   trayaḥ samitimardanāḥf kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca droṇaputraś ca vīryavānf te pi vai vidrutā rāma diśo daśa bhayāt tadāa duryodhano hate sainye pradruteṣu kṛpādiṣuc hradaṃ dvaipāyanaṃ nāma viveśa bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥa śayānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ tu stambhite salile tadāc pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇena vāgbhir ugrābhir ārdayana sa tudyamāno balavān vāgbhī rāma samantataḥc utthitaḥ prāg ghradād vīraḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāma sa cāpy upagato yuddhaṃ bhīmena saha sāṃpratamc bhaviṣyati ca tat sadyas tayo rāma sudāruṇama yadi kautūhalaṃ te sti vraja mādhava mā ciramc paśya yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ śiṣyayor yadi manyasec   adya rāmāhave dvayoḥc bhīmakauravayor vīra vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā tān abhyarcya dvijarṣabhānc sarvān visarjayām āsa ye tenābhyāgatāḥ sahae gamyatāṃ dvārakāṃ ceti so nvaśād anuyāyinaḥa so vatīryācalaśreṣṭhāt plakṣaprasravaṇāc chubhātc tataḥ prītamanā rāmaḥ śrutvā tīrthaphalaṃ mahate viprāṇāṃ saṃnidhau ślokam agāyad idam acyutaḥa sarasvatīvāsasamā kuto ratiḥsarasvatīvāsasamāḥ kuto guṇāḥc sarasvatīṃ prāpya divaṃ gatā janāḥsadā smariṣyanti nadīṃ sarasvatīma sarasvatī sarvanadīṣu puṇyāsarasvatī lokasukhāvahā sadāc sarasvatīṃ prāpya janāḥ suduṣkṛtāḥsadā na śocanti paratra ceha caa tato muhur muhuḥ prītyā prekṣamāṇaḥ sarasvatīmc hayair yuktaṃ rathaṃ śubhram ātiṣṭhata paraṃtapaḥa sa śīghragāminā tena rathena yadupuṃgavaḥc didṛkṣur abhisaṃprāptaḥ śiṣyayuddham upasthitam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ janamejayac yatra duḥkhānvito rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro bravīd idama rāmaṃ saṃnihitaṃ dṛṣṭvā gadāyuddha upasthitec mama putraḥ kathaṃ bhīmaṃ pratyayudhyata saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa rāmasāṃnidhyam āsādya putro duryodhanas tavac yuddhakāmo mahābāhuḥ samahṛṣyata vīryavāna dṛṣṭvā lāṅgalinaṃ rājā pratyutthāya ca bhāratac prītyā paramayā yukto yudhiṣṭhiram athābravītc   samabhyarcya yathāvidhic āsanaṃ ca dadau tasmai paryapṛcchad anāmayamc tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ rāmo vākyam etad uvāca hac madhuraṃ dharmasaṃyuktaṃ śūrāṇāṃ hitam eva cac mayā śrutaṃ kathayatām ṛṣīṇāṃ rājasattamac kurukṣetraṃ paraṃ puṇyaṃ pāvanaṃ svargyam eva cac daivatair ṛṣibhir juṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇaiś ca mahātmabhiḥc tatra vai yotsyamānā ye dehaṃ tyakṣyanti mānavāḥc teṣāṃ svarge dhruvo vāsaḥ śakreṇa saha māriṣaa samantapañcakaṃ kṣipram ito yāma viśāṃ patec prathitottaravedī sā devaloke prajāpateḥa tasmin mahāpuṇyatame trailokyasya sanātanec saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ prāpya dhruvaṃ svargo bhaviṣyatia tathety uktvā mahārāja kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc samantapañcakaṃ vīraḥ prāyād abhimukhaḥ prabhuḥa tato duryodhano rājā pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmc padbhyām amarṣād dyutimān agacchat pāṇḍavaiḥ sahaa tathā yāntaṃ gadāhastaṃ varmaṇā cāpi daṃśitamc antarikṣagatā devāḥ sādhu sādhv ity apūjayane vātikāś ca narā ye tra dṛṣṭvā te harṣam āgatāḥa sa pāṇḍavaiḥ parivṛtaḥ kururājas tavātmajaḥc mattasyeva gajendrasya gatim āsthāya so vrajata tataḥ śaṅkhaninādena bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥc siṃhanādaiś ca śūrāṇāṃ diśaḥ sarvāḥ prapūritāḥd tatas te tu kurukṣetraṃ prāptā naravarottamāḥa pratīcyabhimukhaṃ deśaṃ yathoddiṣṭaṃ sutena tec gatvā ca taiḥ parikṣiptaṃ samantāt sarvatodiśama dakṣiṇena sarasvatyāḥ svayanaṃ tīrtham uttamamc tasmin deśe tv aniriṇe tatra yuddham arocayana tato bhīmo mahākoṭiṃ gadāṃ gṛhyātha varmabhṛtc bibhrad rūpaṃ mahārāja sadṛśaṃ hi garutmataḥa avabaddhaśirastrāṇaḥ saṃkhye kāñcanavarmabhṛtc rarāja rājan putras te kāñcanaḥ śailarāḍ ivaa varmabhyāṃ saṃvṛtau vīrau bhīmaduryodhanāv ubhauc saṃyuge ca prakāśete saṃrabdhāv iva kuñjaraua raṇamaṇḍalamadhyasthau bhrātarau tau nararṣabhauc aśobhetāṃ mahārāja candrasūryāv ivoditaua tāv anyonyaṃ nirīkṣetāṃ kruddhāv iva mahādvipauc dahantau locanai rājan parasparavadhaiṣiṇaua saṃprahṛṣṭamanā rājan gadām ādāya kauravaḥc sṛkkiṇī saṃlihan rājan krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śvasana tato duryodhano rājā gadām ādāya vīryavānc bhīmasenam abhiprekṣya gajo gajam ivāhvayata adrisāramayīṃ bhīmas tathaivādāya vīryavānc āhvayām āsa nṛpatiṃ siṃhaḥ siṃhaṃ yathā vanea tāv udyatagadāpāṇī duryodhanavṛkodarauc saṃyuge sma prakāśete girī saśikharāv ivaa tāv ubhāv abhisaṃkruddhāv ubhau bhīmaparākramauc ubhau śiṣyau gadāyuddhe rauhiṇeyasya dhīmataḥa ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau yamavāsavayor ivac tathā sadṛśakarmāṇau varuṇasya mahābalaua vāsudevasya rāmasya tathā vaiśravaṇasya cac sadṛśau tau mahārāja madhukaiṭabhayor yudhia ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau raṇe sundopasundayoḥb rāmarāvaṇayoś caiva vālisugrīvayos tathāc tathaiva kālasya samau mṛtyoś caiva paraṃtapaua anyonyam abhidhāvantau mattāv iva mahādvipauc vāśitāsaṃgame dṛptau śaradīva madotkaṭaua
